/* Removed duplicate function onOpen; v1.0.1 uses dashboard/template authority implementation. */


function runMonthlyUpdate() {
  const monthParts = promptForLockedYearReportMonth_("Monthly Update");
  if (!monthParts) return;


  const messages = [];
  messages.push("Automatic monthly-sheet hiding is disabled in v1.3.5; archive monthly sheets separately.");


  try {
    const reportSheet = buildMonthlyChangeReportFromDemoPForMonth_(monthParts);
    messages.push("Monthly Change Report: " + (reportSheet ? reportSheet.getName() : "No report created"));
  } catch (err) {
    notify_("Monthly Update stopped during Monthly Change Report: " + err.message);
    throw err;
  }


  try {
    const masterSheet = updateMasterListForMonth_(monthParts);
    messages.push("Master List Update: " + (masterSheet ? masterSheet.getName() : "Not completed"));
  } catch (err) {
    notify_("Monthly Update stopped during Update Master List: " + err.message);
    throw err;
  }


  try {
    createIndexSheet();
  } catch (err) {
    Logger.log("Monthly Update final index refresh skipped: " + err.message);
  }


  notify_("Monthly Update complete.\n\n" + messages.join("\n"));
}

function hidePreviousMonthSheets() {
  const monthParts = promptForLockedYearReportMonth_("Hide Previous Month Sheets");
  if (!monthParts) return;


  const result = hidePreviousMonthSheets_(monthParts);


  const message =
    "Older monthly sheets hidden.\n" +
    "Current month entered: " + formatDateForSheetName_(monthParts.firstDay) + "\n" +
    "Hidden count: " + result.hiddenNames.length + "\n" +
    (
      result.hiddenNames.length
        ? "Hidden: " + result.hiddenNames.join(", ")
        : "No older monthly sheets were hidden."
    );


  notify_(message);
  Logger.log(message);


  if (result.notHiddenNames.length > 0) {
    Logger.log("Matched but NOT hidden: " + result.notHiddenNames.join(", "));
  }
}


function hidePreviousMonthSheets_(monthParts) {
  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();


  const currentMonthStart = new Date(
    monthParts.firstDay.getFullYear(),
    monthParts.firstDay.getMonth(),
    1
  );


  activateSafeSheetBeforeHiding_(ss);


  const hiddenNames = [];
  const notHiddenNames = [];


  ss.getSheets().forEach(sheet => {
    const sheetName = String(sheet.getName() || "").trim();


    if (isSystemSheetName_(sheetName)) return;


    const sheetMonthStart = getSheetMonthStartFromName_(sheetName);
    if (!sheetMonthStart) return;


    if (sheetMonthStart.getTime() >= currentMonthStart.getTime()) return;


    hideSheetSafely_(sheet, hiddenNames, notHiddenNames);
  });


  hideBannerReportForPreviousMonth_(ss, monthParts, hiddenNames, notHiddenNames);
  hideSystemSheets_();


  return {
    hiddenNames: hiddenNames,
    notHiddenNames: notHiddenNames
  };
}


function autoHidePreviousMonthSheetsAfterWorkflow_(monthParts) {
  // v1.3.5: Automatic monthly-sheet hiding removed. Monthly files are archived separately.
  // Use Hide System Sheets or install the system-sheet trigger if needed.
  return;
}


function activateSafeSheetBeforeHiding_(ss) {
  const sheets = ss.getSheets();


  const safeSheet =
    ss.getSheetByName("Index") ||
    sheets.find(sheet => {
      const name = String(sheet.getName() || "").trim();
      return !isSystemSheetName_(name) &&
        name.toLowerCase().indexOf("banner") === -1 &&
        !sheet.isSheetHidden();
    }) ||
    sheets.find(sheet => !sheet.isSheetHidden());


  if (safeSheet) {
    ss.setActiveSheet(safeSheet);
  }
}


function getSheetMonthStartFromName_(sheetName) {
  const match = String(sheetName || "").trim().match(/(\d{1,2})\.(\d{1,2})\.(\d{2}|\d{4})/);
  if (!match) return null;


  let year = Number(match[3]);
  if (year < 100) year += 2000;


  const month = Number(match[1]) - 1;
  const day = Number(match[2]);
  const date = new Date(year, month, day);


  if (
    date.getFullYear() !== year ||
    date.getMonth() !== month ||
    date.getDate() !== day
  ) {
    return null;
  }


  return new Date(year, month, 1);
}


function hideBannerReportForPreviousMonth_(ss, monthParts, hiddenNames, notHiddenNames) {
  const previousStartText = formatDateForSheetName_(monthParts.previousMonthFirstDay);
  const previousEndText = formatDateForSheetName_(monthParts.previousMonthLastDay);
  const previousRangeText = previousStartText + " - " + previousEndText;


  ss.getSheets().forEach(sheet => {
    const sheetName = String(sheet.getName() || "").trim();
    const lower = sheetName.toLowerCase();


    if (isSystemSheetName_(sheetName)) return;
    if (lower.indexOf("banner") === -1) return;
    if (sheetName.indexOf(previousRangeText) === -1) return;
    if (hiddenNames.indexOf(sheetName) !== -1) return;


    hideSheetSafely_(sheet, hiddenNames, notHiddenNames);
  });
}


function hideSheetSafely_(sheet, hiddenNames, notHiddenNames) {
  const sheetName = String(sheet.getName() || "").trim();


  try {
    sheet.hideSheet();


    if (sheet.isSheetHidden()) {
      hiddenNames.push(sheetName);
    } else {
      notHiddenNames.push(sheetName + " - hideSheet ran but sheet is still visible");
    }
  } catch (err) {
    notHiddenNames.push(sheetName + " - " + err.message);
    Logger.log("Could not hide sheet " + sheetName + ": " + err.message);
  }
}


function isSystemSheetName_(sheetName) {
  return (
    sheetName === INDEX_SHEET ||
    sheetName === "Index" ||
    sheetName === MASTER_LIST_CHANGE_LOG_SHEET ||
    sheetName === DISENROLLED_EXCLUSION_SHEET ||
    sheetName === MASTER_LIST_TEMPLATE_SHEET ||
    sheetName === DEMO_P_TEMPLATE_SHEET
  );
}


function hideStandardColumnsOnActiveSheet() {
  const sheet = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSheet();
  const hiddenCount = hideStandardColumnsForSheet_(sheet);
  notify_("Standard columns hidden for " + sheet.getName() + ". Columns hidden: " + hiddenCount);
}


function hideStandardColumnsForSheet_(sheet) {
  if (!sheet) return 0;


  let headersToHide = [];
  const name = String(sheet.getName() || "").toLowerCase();


  if (name.indexOf("master list") !== -1) {
    headersToHide = headersToHide.concat(MASTER_LIST_COLUMNS_TO_HIDE || []);
    headersToHide = headersToHide.concat(getMasterListAdditionalHiddenHeaders_());
  }


  if (headersToHide.length === 0) {
    headersToHide = headersToHide.concat(MASTER_LIST_COLUMNS_TO_HIDE || []);
    headersToHide = headersToHide.concat(getMasterListAdditionalHiddenHeaders_());
  }


  return hideColumnsByHeaders_(sheet, headersToHide);
}


function getMasterListAdditionalHiddenHeaders_() {
  const headers = [];


  for (let i = 1; i <= 8; i++) {
    headers.push("Contact - " + i);
  }


  for (let i = 1; i <= 4; i++) {
    headers.push("Phone " + i + " - Label");
    headers.push("Phone " + i + " - Value");
  }


  headers.push("Address 1 - Street");
  headers.push("Custom Field 1 - Label");
  headers.push("Custom Field 1 - Value");
  headers.push("Master List Update Status");
  headers.push("Master List Update Month");
  headers.push("Master List Source Sheet");


  return headers;
}


function hideColumnsByHeaders_(sheet, headerNames) {
  /*
   * v1.4.25:
   * Runtime header-based column hiding is restricted. Templates receive hidden
   * column settings from Dashboard Section D during template build only.
   */
  return 0;
}


function showColumnsByHeaders_(sheet, headerNames) {
  /*
   * v1.4.25:
   * Runtime header-based column showing is restricted. Templates receive hidden
   * column settings from Dashboard Section D during template build only.
   */
  return 0;
}




function normalizeHeaderForHide_(value) {
  return String(value || "")
    .trim()
    .toLowerCase()
    .replace(/\s+/g, " ")
    .replace(/[–—]/g, "-");
}


function hideColumnNumberBatches_(sheet, columnNumbers) {
  if (!columnNumbers || columnNumbers.length === 0) return;


  const sorted = Array.from(new Set(columnNumbers)).sort((a, b) => a - b);
  let start = sorted[0];
  let previous = sorted[0];


  for (let i = 1; i < sorted.length; i++) {
    const current = sorted[i];


    if (current === previous + 1) {
      previous = current;
      continue;
    }


    sheet.hideColumns(start, previous - start + 1);
    start = current;
    previous = current;
  }


  sheet.hideColumns(start, previous - start + 1);
}


function notify_(message) {
  try {
    SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet().toast(String(message), "Master List Tools", 5);
  } catch (err) {
    Logger.log(message);
  }
}


function promptForReportMonth_(title) {
  const ui = SpreadsheetApp.getUi();
  const response = ui.prompt(
    title || "Report Month",
    "Enter any date in the report month. Example: 05/01/26",
    ui.ButtonSet.OK_CANCEL
  );


  if (response.getSelectedButton() !== ui.Button.OK) return null;


  const reportDate = coerceToValidDate_(response.getResponseText());
  if (!reportDate) {
    notify_("Invalid date. Please enter a date like 05/01/26.");
    return null;
  }


  return getMonthDateParts_(reportDate);
}


function promptForLockedYearReportMonth_(title) {
  const ui = SpreadsheetApp.getUi();


  const monthResponse = ui.prompt(
    title || "Report Month",
    "Enter report month only as MM. Example: 05 for May.\n\nFebruary through November use the locked workflow year.\nDecember and January allow manual year input.",
    ui.ButtonSet.OK_CANCEL
  );


  if (monthResponse.getSelectedButton() !== ui.Button.OK) return null;


  const rawMonth = String(monthResponse.getResponseText() || "").trim();


  if (/^\d{1,2}[\/.\-]\d{1,2}[\/.\-](\d{2}|\d{4})$/.test(rawMonth)) {
    const reportDate = coerceToValidDate_(rawMonth);
    if (!reportDate) {
      notify_("Invalid date. Please enter a date like 05/01/26.");
      return null;
    }
    return getMonthDateParts_(reportDate);
  }


  if (!/^\d{1,2}$/.test(rawMonth)) {
    notify_("Invalid month. Enter a month from 01 through 12, or enter a full date like 05/01/26.");
    return null;
  }


  const month = Number(rawMonth);


  if (month < 1 || month > 12) {
    notify_("Invalid month. Enter a month from 01 through 12.");
    return null;
  }


  let year = getLockedWorkflowYearForMonthOnlyPrompt_();


  if (month === 12 || month === 1) {
    const yearResponse = ui.prompt(
      title || "Report Year",
      `Enter report year for ${String(month).padStart(2, "0")}/01. Example: ${month === 1 ? 2027 : 2026}`,
      ui.ButtonSet.OK_CANCEL
    );


    if (yearResponse.getSelectedButton() !== ui.Button.OK) return null;


    const yearText = String(yearResponse.getResponseText() || "").trim();


    if (!/^\d{4}$/.test(yearText)) {
      notify_("Invalid year. Please enter a 4-digit year such as 2026.");
      return null;
    }


    year = Number(yearText);


    if (year < 2000 || year > 2099) {
      notify_("Invalid year. Please enter a year from 2000 through 2099.");
      return null;
    }
  }


  return getMonthDateParts_(createLocalDateOnly_(year, month - 1, 1));
}


function getLockedWorkflowYearForMonthOnlyPrompt_() {
  const today = new Date();
  const currentYear = today.getFullYear();
  const currentMonth = today.getMonth() + 1;


  if (currentYear < 2027) {
    return 2026;
  }


  if (currentYear === 2027 && currentMonth >= 2) {
    return 2027;
  }


  if (currentMonth >= 2) {
    return currentYear;
  }


  return currentYear;
}


function getMonthDateParts_(date) {
  const d = coerceToValidDate_(date);
  if (!d) return null;


  const firstDay = new Date(d.getFullYear(), d.getMonth(), 1);
  const lastDay = new Date(d.getFullYear(), d.getMonth() + 1, 0);
  const previousMonthFirstDay = new Date(d.getFullYear(), d.getMonth() - 1, 1);
  const previousMonthLastDay = new Date(d.getFullYear(), d.getMonth(), 0);


  return {
    inputDate: d,
    firstDay: firstDay,
    lastDay: lastDay,
    previousMonthFirstDay: previousMonthFirstDay,
    previousMonthLastDay: previousMonthLastDay,
    firstDayName: formatDateForSheetName_(firstDay),
    lastDayName: formatDateForSheetName_(lastDay),
    previousFirstDayName: formatDateForSheetName_(previousMonthFirstDay),
    previousLastDayName: formatDateForSheetName_(previousMonthLastDay),
    monthKey: Utilities.formatDate(firstDay, Session.getScriptTimeZone(), "yyyy-MM")
  };
}


function coerceToValidDate_(value) {
  if (value instanceof Date && !isNaN(value.getTime())) {
    return isReasonableReportDate_(value) ? value : null;
  }


  if (value === null || value === undefined || value === "") return null;


  if (typeof value === "number") {
    if (value < 30000) return null;
    return spreadsheetSerialDateToLocalDate_(value);
  }


  const text = String(value).trim();
  if (!text) return null;


  const match = text.match(/^(\d{1,2})[\/.\-](\d{1,2})[\/.\-](\d{2}|\d{4})$/);
  if (match) {
    const month = Number(match[1]) - 1;
    const day = Number(match[2]);
    let year = Number(match[3]);
    if (year < 100) year += 2000;


    const d = new Date(year, month, day);
    if (d.getFullYear() !== year || d.getMonth() !== month || d.getDate() !== day) return null;
    return isReasonableReportDate_(d) ? d : null;
  }


  const d = new Date(text);
  return !isNaN(d.getTime()) && isReasonableReportDate_(d) ? d : null;
}


function spreadsheetSerialDateToLocalDate_(serialValue) {
  if (serialValue === null || serialValue === undefined || serialValue === "") return null;


  const serial = Number(serialValue);
  if (isNaN(serial) || serial < 1) return null;


  const wholeDays = Math.floor(serial);
  const fractional = serial - wholeDays;


  const date = new Date(1899, 11, 30);
  date.setDate(date.getDate() + wholeDays);


  if (fractional > 0) {
    const millisInDay = Math.round(fractional * 24 * 60 * 60 * 1000);
    date.setMilliseconds(date.getMilliseconds() + millisInDay);
  }


  return isReasonableReportDate_(date) ? date : null;
}


function isReasonableReportDate_(date) {
  const year = date.getFullYear();
  return year >= 2000 && year <= 2099;
}


function formatDateForSheetName_(date) {
  return Utilities.formatDate(date, Session.getScriptTimeZone(), DATE_SHEET_FORMAT);
}


function formatDateDisplay_(date) {
  const d = coerceToValidDate_(date);
  return d ? Utilities.formatDate(d, Session.getScriptTimeZone(), DATE_DISPLAY_FORMAT) : "";
}


function dateKey_(value) {
  const d = coerceToValidDate_(value);
  return d ? Utilities.formatDate(d, Session.getScriptTimeZone(), "yyyyMMdd") : "";
}


function monthKey_(value) {
  const d = coerceToValidDate_(value);
  return d ? Utilities.formatDate(new Date(d.getFullYear(), d.getMonth(), 1), Session.getScriptTimeZone(), "yyyyMM") : "";
}


function isSameDate_(a, b) {
  return dateKey_(a) !== "" && dateKey_(a) === dateKey_(b);
}


function isSameMonth_(a, b) {
  return monthKey_(a) !== "" && monthKey_(a) === monthKey_(b);
}


function isBeforeDate_(a, b) {
  const aKey = dateKey_(a);
  const bKey = dateKey_(b);
  return aKey !== "" && bKey !== "" && aKey < bKey;
}


function isDateInRangeInclusive_(value, startDate, endDate) {
  const testDate = coerceToValidDate_(value);
  const start = coerceToValidDate_(startDate);
  const end = coerceToValidDate_(endDate);


  if (!testDate || !start || !end) return false;


  const testKey = dateKey_(testDate);
  const startKey = dateKey_(start);
  const endKey = dateKey_(end);


  return testKey !== "" && testKey >= startKey && testKey <= endKey;
}


function localDateNumber_(value) {
  const d = coerceToValidDate_(value);
  if (!d) return null;


  return d.getFullYear() * 10000 + (d.getMonth() + 1) * 100 + d.getDate();
}


function isDateInStrictLocalRangeInclusive_(value, startDate, endDate) {
  const testNum = localDateNumber_(value);
  const startNum = localDateNumber_(startDate);
  const endNum = localDateNumber_(endDate);


  if (testNum === null || startNum === null || endNum === null) return false;


  return testNum >= startNum && testNum <= endNum;
}


function isDateDisplayInReportWindow_(value, startDate, endDate) {
  const test = coerceToValidDate_(value);
  const start = coerceToValidDate_(startDate);
  const end = coerceToValidDate_(endDate);


  if (!test || !start || !end) return false;


  const testMonth = test.getMonth() + 1;
  const testDay = test.getDate();
  const testYear = test.getFullYear();


  const startNum = start.getFullYear() * 10000 + (start.getMonth() + 1) * 100 + start.getDate();
  const endNum = end.getFullYear() * 10000 + (end.getMonth() + 1) * 100 + end.getDate();
  const testNum = testYear * 10000 + testMonth * 100 + testDay;


  return testNum >= startNum && testNum <= endNum;
}


function getMonthlyChangeReportHeaders_(sourceHeaders) {
  const headers = sourceHeaders.slice();


  if (headers.indexOf("Columns With Change") === -1) {
    headers.push("Columns With Change");
  }


  return headers;
}


function getMostRecentDateFromRowsByHeader_(rows, headerMap, headerName) {
  const idx = headerMap[headerName];
  if (idx === undefined || idx < 0) return null;


  let mostRecent = null;


  (rows || []).forEach(item => {
    const value = item && item.values ? item.values[idx] : "";
    const date = coerceToValidDate_(value);


    if (!date) return;


    if (!mostRecent || dateKey_(date) > dateKey_(mostRecent)) {
      mostRecent = date;
    }
  });


  return mostRecent;
}


function isParticipantEnrollmentStatusDisenrolled_(rows, headerMap) {
  const idx = headerMap["Enrollment Status"];
  if (idx === undefined || idx < 0) return false;


  return (rows || []).some(item => {
    const value = item && item.values ? item.values[idx] : "";
    return String(value || "").trim().toLowerCase() === "disenrolled";
  });
}


function convertMonthlyChangeReportDateValues_(rowValues, reportHeaders) {
  const output = rowValues.slice();


  GLOBAL_DATE_FORMAT_HEADERS.forEach(headerName => {
    const idx = reportHeaders.indexOf(headerName);
    if (idx === -1 || idx >= output.length) return;


    const value = output[idx];


    if (value instanceof Date && !isNaN(value.getTime())) return;


    if (typeof value === "number" && !isNaN(value) && value > 20000) {
      const convertedDate = spreadsheetSerialDateToLocalDate_(value);
      if (convertedDate) output[idx] = convertedDate;
      return;
    }


    const parsed = coerceToValidDate_(value);
    if (parsed) output[idx] = parsed;
  });


  return output;
}


function buildMonthlyChangeReportRow_(sourceRow, sourceHeaders, reportHeaders, changedColumns) {
  const output = sourceRow.slice(0, sourceHeaders.length);


  while (output.length < reportHeaders.length) {
    output.push("");
  }


  const changeIdx = reportHeaders.indexOf("Columns With Change");
  if (changeIdx !== -1) {
    output[changeIdx] = changedColumns && changedColumns.size > 0
      ? Array.from(changedColumns).sort().join(", ")
      : "";
  }


  return convertMonthlyChangeReportDateValues_(output, reportHeaders);
}


function buildMonthlySheetName_(prefix, firstDay, lastDay) {
  // v1.4.2: Standard monthly output names use mm.yy only.
  return buildStandardMonthlySheetName_(prefix, firstDay);
}


function buildMonthlySheetNameNoDashAfterPrefix_(prefix, firstDay, lastDay) {
  // v1.4.2: Kept for legacy callers; now returns the standardized mm.yy name.
  return buildStandardMonthlySheetName_(prefix, firstDay);
}


function buildStandardMonthlySheetName_(prefix, monthDate) {
  const date = coerceToValidDate_(monthDate) || new Date();
  const monthText = Utilities.formatDate(date, Session.getScriptTimeZone(), "MM.yy");
  return String(prefix || "").trim() + " " + monthText;
}


function parseStandardMonthlySheetDateFromName_(sheetName, prefix) {
  const name = String(sheetName || "").trim();
  const prefixText = String(prefix || "").trim();
  if (!prefixText) return null;


  const escapedPrefix = prefixText.replace(/[.*+?^${}()|[\]\\]/g, "\\$&");
  const re = new RegExp("^" + escapedPrefix + "\\s+(\\d{1,2})\\.(\\d{2})(?:\\s|$|\\()", "i");
  const match = name.match(re);
  if (!match) return null;


  const month = Number(match[1]);
  const year = 2000 + Number(match[2]);
  if (month < 1 || month > 12 || year < 2000 || year > 2099) return null;


  return new Date(year, month - 1, 1);
}


function getNewestFormattedMonthlySheetByPrefix_(ss, prefix) {
  if (!ss || !prefix) return null;


  const sheets = ss.getSheets();
  const matches = [];


  sheets.forEach(sheet => {
    const parsed = parseStandardMonthlySheetDateFromName_(sheet.getName(), prefix);
    if (!parsed) return;
    matches.push({
      sheet,
      key: monthKey_(parsed),
      index: sheet.getIndex ? sheet.getIndex() : 0
    });
  });


  if (!matches.length) return null;


  matches.sort((a, b) => {
    if (a.key !== b.key) return a.key < b.key ? 1 : -1;
    return b.index - a.index;
  });


  return matches[0].sheet;
}


function setUniqueSheetName_(sheet, desiredName) {
  if (!sheet || !desiredName) return desiredName;


  const ss = sheet.getParent();
  let name = desiredName;
  let counter = 2;


  if (sheet.getName && sheet.getName() === desiredName) {
    return desiredName;
  }


  let existing = ss.getSheetByName(name);
  while (existing && existing.getSheetId && existing.getSheetId() !== sheet.getSheetId()) {
    name = `${desiredName} (${counter})`;
    counter++;
    existing = ss.getSheetByName(name);
  }


  if (sheet.getName() !== name) {
    sheet.setName(name);
    clearMonthlySheetLookupCache_();
    clearSheetRuntimeCachesForSheet_(sheet);
  }


  return name;
}


/**
 * Fast monthly output rename helper.
 * Deletes/replaces an existing monthly output with the same name before renaming,
 * then clears sheet lookup caches. This helper is required by Format Raw Data,
 * Demo P, Master List, and other monthly output functions.
 */
function setMonthlySheetNameFast_(sheet, desiredName) {
  if (!sheet || !desiredName) return desiredName;


  const ss = sheet.getParent();
  if (sheet.getName && sheet.getName() === desiredName) return desiredName;


  const existing = ss.getSheetByName(desiredName);
  if (existing && existing.getSheetId && existing.getSheetId() !== sheet.getSheetId()) {
    ss.deleteSheet(existing);
  }


  if (sheet.getName() !== desiredName) {
    sheet.setName(desiredName);
    clearMonthlySheetLookupCache_();
    clearSheetRuntimeCachesForSheet_(sheet);
  }


  return desiredName;
}


const ML_MONTHLY_SHEET_LOOKUP_CACHE_ = {};


function clearMonthlySheetLookupCache_() {
  Object.keys(ML_MONTHLY_SHEET_LOOKUP_CACHE_).forEach(key => {
    delete ML_MONTHLY_SHEET_LOOKUP_CACHE_[key];
  });
}


function getMonthlySheetLookupCacheKey_(ss, prefix, firstDay, lastDay) {
  const spreadsheetId = ss && ss.getId ? ss.getId() : "";
  const startKey = dateKey_(firstDay);
  const endKey = dateKey_(lastDay);
  return [spreadsheetId, String(prefix || "").trim().toLowerCase(), startKey, endKey].join("||");
}


function getMonthlySheetByPrefixAndDate_(ss, prefix, firstDay, lastDay) {
  // v1.4.2: all production sync sources use the standardized monthly output name Prefix mm.yy.
  if (!ss || !prefix) return null;


  const cacheKey = getMonthlySheetLookupCacheKey_(ss, prefix, firstDay, lastDay);
  const cachedSheet = ML_MONTHLY_SHEET_LOOKUP_CACHE_[cacheKey];
  if (cachedSheet) {
    try {
      if (cachedSheet.getName()) return cachedSheet;
    } catch (err) {
      delete ML_MONTHLY_SHEET_LOOKUP_CACHE_[cacheKey];
    }
  }


  const standardName = buildStandardMonthlySheetName_(prefix, firstDay);
  let sheet = ss.getSheetByName(standardName);
  if (sheet) {
    ML_MONTHLY_SHEET_LOOKUP_CACHE_[cacheKey] = sheet;
    return sheet;
  }


  sheet = getNewestFormattedMonthlySheetByPrefix_(ss, prefix);
  if (sheet) {
    ML_MONTHLY_SHEET_LOOKUP_CACHE_[cacheKey] = sheet;
    return sheet;
  }


  return null;
}




function getCurrentDemoPSheet_(monthParts) {
  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  return getMonthlySheetByPrefixAndDate_(ss, DEMO_P_PREFIX, monthParts.firstDay, monthParts.lastDay);
}


function getCurrentMasterListSheet_(monthParts) {
  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  return getMonthlySheetByPrefixAndDate_(ss, MASTER_LIST_PREFIX, monthParts.firstDay, monthParts.lastDay);
}


function getPreviousMasterListSheet_(monthParts) {
  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  return getMonthlySheetByPrefixAndDate_(ss, MASTER_LIST_PREFIX, monthParts.previousMonthFirstDay, monthParts.previousMonthLastDay);
}


function getPreviousDemoPSheet_(monthParts) {
  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  return getMonthlySheetByPrefixAndDate_(ss, DEMO_P_PREFIX, monthParts.previousMonthFirstDay, monthParts.previousMonthLastDay);
}




function getCurrentCarePlanDueSheet_(monthParts) {
  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();

  // v1.5.5: Care Plan sync must use the workflow / Master List month.
  // Example: Master List 04.26 -> CP Due 04.26.
  if (monthParts && monthParts.firstDay && monthParts.lastDay) {
    return getMonthlySheetByPrefixAndDate_(ss, "CP Due", monthParts.firstDay, monthParts.lastDay) ||
      findMonthlyOutputSheetByPrefixAndSuffix_(ss, "CP Due", formatDateForSheetName_(monthParts.firstDay));
  }

  const masterSheet = getNewestFormattedMonthlySheetByPrefix_(ss, MASTER_LIST_PREFIX);
  const suffix = getWorkflowMonthSuffixFromSheet_(masterSheet);
  return suffix
    ? findMonthlyOutputSheetByPrefixAndSuffix_(ss, "CP Due", suffix)
    : getNewestFormattedMonthlySheetByPrefix_(ss, "CP Due");
}




function getCurrentUnlockedCarePlanSheet_(monthParts) {
  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();

  // v1.5.5: Care Plan sync must use the workflow / Master List month.
  // Example: Master List 04.26 -> Unlocked CP 04.26.
  if (monthParts && monthParts.firstDay && monthParts.lastDay) {
    return getMonthlySheetByPrefixAndDate_(ss, "Unlocked CP", monthParts.firstDay, monthParts.lastDay) ||
      findMonthlyOutputSheetByPrefixAndSuffix_(ss, "Unlocked CP", formatDateForSheetName_(monthParts.firstDay));
  }

  const masterSheet = getNewestFormattedMonthlySheetByPrefix_(ss, MASTER_LIST_PREFIX);
  const suffix = getWorkflowMonthSuffixFromSheet_(masterSheet);
  return suffix
    ? findMonthlyOutputSheetByPrefixAndSuffix_(ss, "Unlocked CP", suffix)
    : getNewestFormattedMonthlySheetByPrefix_(ss, "Unlocked CP");
}




function getCurrentBannersSheet_(monthParts) {
  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  if (monthParts && monthParts.firstDay && monthParts.lastDay) {
    return getMonthlySheetByPrefixAndDate_(ss, "Banners", monthParts.firstDay, monthParts.lastDay) ||
      getNewestFormattedMonthlySheetByPrefix_(ss, "Banners");
  }
  return getNewestFormattedMonthlySheetByPrefix_(ss, "Banners");
}




const ML_HEADER_CACHE_ = {};
const ML_HEADER_MAP_CACHE_ = {};
const ML_SHEET_DIMENSION_CACHE_ = {};


function getSheetDimensionCacheKey_(sheet) {
  return sheet ? String(sheet.getSheetId()) : "";
}


function clearSheetDimensionCacheForSheet_(sheet) {
  if (!sheet) return;
  const key = getSheetDimensionCacheKey_(sheet);
  if (key) delete ML_SHEET_DIMENSION_CACHE_[key];
}


function getSheetDimensions_(sheet) {
  const key = getSheetDimensionCacheKey_(sheet);
  if (key && ML_SHEET_DIMENSION_CACHE_[key]) {
    return Object.assign({}, ML_SHEET_DIMENSION_CACHE_[key]);
  }


  const dimensions = {
    lastRow: sheet.getLastRow(),
    lastCol: sheet.getLastColumn(),
    maxRows: sheet.getMaxRows(),
    maxCols: sheet.getMaxColumns()
  };


  if (key) ML_SHEET_DIMENSION_CACHE_[key] = Object.assign({}, dimensions);
  return dimensions;
}


function clearSheetRuntimeCachesForSheet_(sheet) {
  clearHeaderCacheForSheet_(sheet);
  clearSheetDimensionCacheForSheet_(sheet);
}


function getHeaderCacheKey_(sheet, headerRow) {
  if (!sheet) return "";
  const row = headerRow || HEADER_ROW;
  const lastCol = Math.max(sheet.getLastColumn(), 1);
  return sheet.getSheetId() + ":" + row + ":" + lastCol;
}


function clearHeaderCacheForSheet_(sheet) {
  if (!sheet) return;
  const prefix = sheet.getSheetId() + ":";


  Object.keys(ML_HEADER_CACHE_).forEach(key => {
    if (key.indexOf(prefix) === 0) delete ML_HEADER_CACHE_[key];
  });


  Object.keys(ML_HEADER_MAP_CACHE_).forEach(key => {
    if (key.indexOf(prefix) === 0) delete ML_HEADER_MAP_CACHE_[key];
  });
}


function getHeaders_(sheet, headerRow) {
  headerRow = headerRow || HEADER_ROW;
  const key = getHeaderCacheKey_(sheet, headerRow);


  if (key && ML_HEADER_CACHE_[key]) {
    return ML_HEADER_CACHE_[key].slice();
  }


  const lastCol = Math.max(sheet.getLastColumn(), 1);
  const headers = sheet.getRange(headerRow, 1, 1, lastCol)
    .getValues()[0]
    .map(h => String(h || "").trim());


  if (key) ML_HEADER_CACHE_[key] = headers.slice();
  return headers;
}


function buildHeaderIndexMap_(headers) {
  const map = {};
  headers.forEach((header, idx) => {
    const clean = String(header || "").trim();
    if (clean && map[clean] === undefined) map[clean] = idx;
  });
  return map;
}


function getHeaderMap_(sheet, headerRow) {
  headerRow = headerRow || HEADER_ROW;
  const key = getHeaderCacheKey_(sheet, headerRow);


  if (key && ML_HEADER_MAP_CACHE_[key]) {
    return Object.assign({}, ML_HEADER_MAP_CACHE_[key]);
  }


  const map = buildHeaderIndexMap_(getHeaders_(sheet, headerRow));
  if (key) ML_HEADER_MAP_CACHE_[key] = Object.assign({}, map);
  return map;
}


function findHeaderIndex_(headerMap, possibleNames) {
  for (let i = 0; i < possibleNames.length; i++) {
    if (headerMap[possibleNames[i]] !== undefined) return headerMap[possibleNames[i]];
  }
  return -1;
}




function ensureHeaders_(sheet, headersToAdd, headerRow) {
  /*
   * v1.4.24:
   * Runtime processing may not add columns. Dashboard Section C - Sheet Headers
   * is the only column add/remove authority. This helper now reports existing
   * headers only; callers must skip writes when required columns are absent.
   */
  headerRow = headerRow || HEADER_ROW;
  clearSheetRuntimeCachesForSheet_(sheet);
  return getHeaders_(sheet, headerRow);
}




function normalizeKeyPart_(value) {
  if (value === null || value === undefined) return "";


  if (value instanceof Date && !isNaN(value.getTime())) {
    return Utilities.formatDate(value, Session.getScriptTimeZone(), "yyyyMMdd");
  }


  return String(value)
    .trim()
    .toLowerCase()
    .replace(/\s+/g, " ");
}


function normalizePMR_(value) {
  return String(value === null || value === undefined ? "" : value)
    .trim()
    .replace(/\s+/g, "")
    .replace(/\.0$/, "");
}


function getPMRIndex_(headerMap) {
  return findHeaderIndex_(headerMap, ["Participant PMR#", "PMR #", "PMR#", "Participant PMR"]);
}


function getDOBIndex_(headerMap) {
  return findHeaderIndex_(headerMap, ["Date of Birth", "DOB"]);
}


function buildRowsByPMR_(sheet, headerRow, dataStartRow) {
  headerRow = headerRow || HEADER_ROW;
  dataStartRow = dataStartRow || DATA_START_ROW;


  const data = getDataValues_(sheet, headerRow, dataStartRow);
  const result = new Map();


  if (!data.values.length) return result;


  const pmrIdx = getPMRIndex_(data.headerMap);


  if (pmrIdx === -1) throw new Error(`${sheet.getName()} is missing Participant PMR# / PMR # column.`);


  data.values.forEach((row, offset) => {
    const pmr = normalizePMR_(row[pmrIdx]);
    if (!pmr) return;


    if (!result.has(pmr)) result.set(pmr, []);
    result.get(pmr).push({
      rowNumber: dataStartRow + offset,
      values: row
    });
  });


  return result;
}






function getDataValues_(sheet, headerRow, dataStartRow) {
  headerRow = headerRow || HEADER_ROW;
  dataStartRow = dataStartRow || DATA_START_ROW;


  const dimensions = getSheetDimensions_(sheet);
  const lastRow = dimensions.lastRow;
  const lastCol = dimensions.lastCol;
  const headers = getHeaders_(sheet, headerRow);
  const headerMap = getHeaderMap_(sheet, headerRow);


  if (lastRow < dataStartRow || lastCol < 1) {
    return {
      headers: headers,
      headerMap: headerMap,
      values: [],
      range: null,
      lastRow: lastRow,
      lastCol: lastCol
    };
  }


  const range = sheet.getRange(dataStartRow, 1, lastRow - dataStartRow + 1, lastCol);


  return {
    headers: headers,
    headerMap: headerMap,
    values: range.getValues(),
    range: range,
    lastRow: lastRow,
    lastCol: lastCol
  };
}






function deleteRowNumberBatches_(sheet, rowNumbers) {
  if (!rowNumbers || rowNumbers.length === 0) return;


  const sorted = Array.from(new Set(rowNumbers)).sort((a, b) => b - a);


  let start = sorted[0];
  let end = sorted[0];


  for (let i = 1; i < sorted.length; i++) {
    const current = sorted[i];


    if (current === end - 1) {
      end = current;
      continue;
    }


    sheet.deleteRows(end, start - end + 1);
    start = current;
    end = current;
  }


  sheet.deleteRows(end, start - end + 1);
}


function deleteColumnNumberBatches_(sheet, columnNumbers) {
  /*
   * v1.4.25:
   * Runtime column deletion is restricted. Column additions/removals are governed
   * by Dashboard Section C and executed only by dashboard/template rebuild paths.
   */
  return 0;
}




function normalizeCompareValue_(value) {
  if (value instanceof Date && !isNaN(value.getTime())) {
    return Utilities.formatDate(value, Session.getScriptTimeZone(), "yyyy-MM-dd");
  }


  if (value === null || value === undefined) return "";


  const text = String(value).trim();
  if (text === "") return "";


  const parsed = coerceToValidDate_(text);
  if (parsed && /\d{1,2}[\/.\-]\d{1,2}[\/.\-]\d{2,4}/.test(text)) {
    return Utilities.formatDate(parsed, Session.getScriptTimeZone(), "yyyy-MM-dd");
  }


  return text
    .toLowerCase()
    .replace(/\s+/g, " ");
}


function valuesAreEqual_(a, b) {
  return normalizeCompareValue_(a) === normalizeCompareValue_(b);
}

function deleteBlankRowsAfter_(sheet, lastDataRowToKeep) {
  const maxRows = sheet.getMaxRows();
  const lastCol = Math.max(sheet.getMaxColumns(), sheet.getLastColumn(), 1);
  const startRow = (lastDataRowToKeep || FORMAT_DELETE_BLANK_ROWS_AFTER) + 1;


  if (maxRows < startRow) return;


  const numRows = maxRows - startRow + 1;
  const values = sheet.getRange(startRow, 1, numRows, lastCol).getDisplayValues();
  const blankRows = [];


  values.forEach((rowValues, idx) => {
    const hasData = rowValues.some(value => String(value || "").trim() !== "");
    if (!hasData) blankRows.push(startRow + idx);
  });


  deleteRowNumberBatches_(sheet, blankRows);
}

function ensureStandardTitleRows_(sheet) {
  sheet.getRange(1, 1, Math.max(sheet.getLastRow(), HEADER_ROW), Math.max(sheet.getLastColumn(), 1)).breakApart();


  if (hasStandardTitleRows_(sheet)) {
    return;
  }


  const headerRow = detectCurrentHeaderRow_(sheet);


  const rowsNeeded = Math.max(0, HEADER_ROW - headerRow);


  if (rowsNeeded > 0) {
    sheet.insertRowsBefore(1, rowsNeeded);
  }


  if (HEADER_ROW > 1) {
    sheet.getRange(1, 1, HEADER_ROW - 1, Math.max(sheet.getLastColumn(), 1))
      .clear({ contentsOnly: true });
  }
}


function hasStandardTitleRows_(sheet) {
  const a2 = String(sheet.getRange("A2").getDisplayValue() || "").trim().toLowerCase();
  const c2 = String(sheet.getRange("C2").getDisplayValue() || "").trim().toLowerCase();


  return a2 === "date" && c2 === "to";
}


function detectCurrentHeaderRow_(sheet) {
  const maxCheckRows = Math.min(10, sheet.getMaxRows());
  const maxCols = Math.max(sheet.getLastColumn(), 1);


  const values = sheet.getRange(1, 1, maxCheckRows, maxCols).getDisplayValues();


  for (let r = 0; r < values.length; r++) {
    const row = values[r].map(v => String(v || "").trim().toLowerCase());


    const matches =
      row.includes("participant pmr#") ||
      row.includes("participant name") ||
      row.includes("last name") ||
      row.includes("first name") ||
      row.includes("next care plan due") ||
      row.includes("enrollment status");


    if (matches) {
      return r + 1;
    }
  }


  return 1;
}


function collectCellTextWithSpaces_(sheet, a1List) {
  const parts = [];


  a1List.forEach(a1 => {
    try {
      const value = sheet.getRange(a1).getDisplayValue();
      if (String(value || "").trim()) {
        parts.push(String(value).trim());
      }
    } catch (err) {
      Logger.log("Could not read " + a1 + ": " + err.message);
    }
  });


  return parts.join(" ");
}


function safeBreakApart_(sheet, a1Notation) {
  try {
    sheet.getRange(a1Notation).breakApart();
  } catch (err) {
    Logger.log("Could not unmerge " + a1Notation + ": " + err.message);
  }
}


function createLocalDateOnly_(year, month, day) {
  return new Date(year, month, day, 12, 0, 0, 0);
}


function dateOnlyLocalClone_(date) {
  const d = coerceToValidDate_(date);
  if (!d) return null;
  return createLocalDateOnly_(d.getFullYear(), d.getMonth(), d.getDate());
}


function getStandardSheetTypeFromName_(sheetName) {
  const name = String(sheetName || "").toLowerCase();


  if (name.indexOf("care plan due") !== -1) return SHEET_TYPE.CARE_PLAN_DUE;
  if (name.indexOf("unlocked") !== -1) return SHEET_TYPE.UNLOCKED;
  if (name.indexOf("banner") !== -1) return SHEET_TYPE.BANNER;
  if (name.indexOf("demo p") !== -1) return SHEET_TYPE.DEMO_P;
  if (name.indexOf("monthly change") !== -1) return SHEET_TYPE.MONTHLY_CHANGE;
  if (name.indexOf("change log") !== -1) return SHEET_TYPE.MASTER_LIST_CHANGE_LOG;
  if (name.indexOf("disenrollment") !== -1 || name.indexOf("disenrolled") !== -1) return SHEET_TYPE.DISENROLLED_EXCLUSION;
  if (name.indexOf("master list") !== -1) return SHEET_TYPE.MASTER_LIST;


  return SHEET_TYPE.MASTER_LIST;
}


function getStandardSheetTypeFromPrefix_(prefix) {
  const value = String(prefix || "").toLowerCase();


  if (value.indexOf("care plan due") !== -1) return SHEET_TYPE.CARE_PLAN_DUE;
  if (value.indexOf("unlocked") !== -1) return SHEET_TYPE.UNLOCKED;
  if (value.indexOf("banner") !== -1) return SHEET_TYPE.BANNER;
  if (value.indexOf("demo p") !== -1) return SHEET_TYPE.DEMO_P;
  if (value.indexOf("monthly change") !== -1) return SHEET_TYPE.MONTHLY_CHANGE;
  if (value.indexOf("change log") !== -1) return SHEET_TYPE.MASTER_LIST_CHANGE_LOG;
  if (value.indexOf("disenrollment") !== -1 || value.indexOf("disenrolled") !== -1) return SHEET_TYPE.DISENROLLED_EXCLUSION;
  if (value.indexOf("master list") !== -1) return SHEET_TYPE.MASTER_LIST;


  return SHEET_TYPE.MASTER_LIST;
}

}function findDisenrolledExclusionHeaderRow_(sheet) {
  const maxRowsToCheck = Math.min(10, sheet.getLastRow());
  const maxCols = Math.max(sheet.getLastColumn(), 1);


  if (maxRowsToCheck < 1) return HEADER_ROW;


  const values = sheet.getRange(1, 1, maxRowsToCheck, maxCols).getDisplayValues();


  for (let r = 0; r < values.length; r++) {
    const row = values[r].map(v => String(v || "").trim());


    if (
      row.indexOf("Last Name") !== -1 &&
      row.indexOf("First Name") !== -1 &&
      (
        row.indexOf("Participant PMR#") !== -1 ||
        row.indexOf("PMR #") !== -1
      )
    ) {
      return r + 1;
    }
  }


  return HEADER_ROW;
}


function getExistingPMRsFromSheet_(sheet, startRow, pmrColumn) {
  const result = new Set();
  const lastRow = sheet.getLastRow();


  if (lastRow < startRow) return result;


  const values = sheet.getRange(startRow, pmrColumn, lastRow - startRow + 1, 1).getValues();


  values.forEach(row => {
    const pmr = normalizePMR_(row[0]);
    if (pmr) result.add(pmr);
  });


  return result;
}

function getTodayLocalDate_() {
  const now = new Date();
  return createLocalDateOnly_(now.getFullYear(), now.getMonth(), now.getDate());
}


function prepareMasterListChangeLogSheetForCreate_(sheet) {
  if (!sheet) return;


  const today = getTodayLocalDate_();


  moveChangeLogDataOutOfTitleRows_(sheet);


  sheet.getRange(1, 1, 3, Math.max(sheet.getMaxColumns(), MASTER_LIST_CHANGE_LOG_HEADERS.length))
    .clear({ contentsOnly: true });


  sheet.getRange(HEADER_ROW, 1, 1, MASTER_LIST_CHANGE_LOG_HEADERS.length)
    .setValues([MASTER_LIST_CHANGE_LOG_HEADERS]);
  clearHeaderCacheForSheet_(sheet);


  applyStandardFormattingAfterHeadersAndData_(
    sheet,
    SHEET_TYPE.MASTER_LIST_CHANGE_LOG,
    SHEET_TYPE.MASTER_LIST_CHANGE_LOG,
    today,
    today,
    ""
  );


  sheet.getRange("A1").setValue(MASTER_LIST_CHANGE_LOG_SHEET);
  sheet.getRange("A2").setValue("Creation Date");
  sheet.getRange("B2").setValue(today);
  sheet.getRange("C2").setValue("to");
  sheet.getRange("D2").setValue(today);


  sheet.getRange(HEADER_ROW, 1, 1, MASTER_LIST_CHANGE_LOG_HEADERS.length)
    .setValues([MASTER_LIST_CHANGE_LOG_HEADERS]);
  clearHeaderCacheForSheet_(sheet);


  applyStandardFreeze_(sheet);
  forceStandardTitleCellAlignment_(sheet);
}


function moveChangeLogDataOutOfTitleRows_(sheet) {
  const lastCol = Math.max(sheet.getLastColumn(), MASTER_LIST_CHANGE_LOG_HEADERS.length, 1);
  const rowsToMove = [];


  for (let row = 1; row <= 3; row++) {
    const values = sheet.getRange(row, 1, 1, lastCol).getValues()[0];
    const display = values.map(v => String(v || "").trim());
    const hasData = display.some(v => v !== "");


    if (!hasData) continue;


    const firstCell = display[0].toLowerCase();


    const isStandardTitleRow =
      row === 1 && firstCell === "master list change log" ||
      row === 2 && firstCell === "creation date" ||
      row === 3 && display.every(v => v === "");


    if (!isStandardTitleRow) {
      rowsToMove.push(values);
      sheet.getRange(row, 1, 1, lastCol).clearContent();
    }
  }


  if (rowsToMove.length > 0) {
    const appendRow = Math.max(sheet.getLastRow() + 1, DATA_START_ROW);
    sheet.getRange(appendRow, 1, rowsToMove.length, lastCol).setValues(rowsToMove);
  }
}


function appendMasterListChangeLogRows_(rows) {
  appendMasterListChangeLog_(rows);
}

  createIndexSheet();

  applyCurrentVsOlderTabColors_();
  organizeSheetTabs_();
}


function captureHiddenSheetNames_() {
  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  const hiddenNames = new Set();


  ss.getSheets().forEach(sheet => {
    try {
      if (sheet.isSheetHidden()) hiddenNames.add(sheet.getName());
    } catch (err) {
      Logger.log("Could not read hidden state for " + sheet.getName() + ": " + err.message);
    }
  });


  return hiddenNames;
}


function restorePreviouslyHiddenSheets_(hiddenNames, sheetToKeepVisible) {
  if (!hiddenNames || hiddenNames.size === 0) return;


  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  const keepVisibleName = sheetToKeepVisible ? String(sheetToKeepVisible.getName() || "") : "";


  try {
    if (sheetToKeepVisible && !sheetToKeepVisible.isSheetHidden()) {
      ss.setActiveSheet(sheetToKeepVisible);
    } else {
      activateSafeSheetBeforeHiding_(ss);
    }
  } catch (err) {
    Logger.log("Could not activate safe sheet before restoring hidden sheets: " + err.message);
  }


  hiddenNames.forEach(name => {
    if (!name) return;
    if (name === keepVisibleName) return;


    const sheet = ss.getSheetByName(name);
    if (!sheet) return;


    try {
      if (!sheet.isSheetHidden()) sheet.hideSheet();
    } catch (err) {
      Logger.log("Could not restore hidden sheet " + name + ": " + err.message);
    }
  });


  hideSystemSheets_();
}

  hideDecimalSortOrderRows_(sheet);
  enforceMasterListFinalDisplay_(sheet);


  notify_("Sort Order assigned. Primary rows remain visible and extra rows are hidden.");
}

function assignSortOrderByParticipant_(sheet) {
  sheet = sheet || SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSheet();


  const primaryCol = ensurePrimaryPMRRowColumn_(sheet);
  const sortCol = ensureSortOrderColumn_(sheet);
  if (sortCol < 1) {
    notify_("Sort Order skipped: Sort Order column is not defined in Dashboard Sheet Headers.");
    return;
  }
  const lastRow = sheet.getLastRow();
  const lastCol = sheet.getLastColumn();


  if (lastRow < DATA_START_ROW || lastCol < 1) return;


  const headers = getHeaders_(sheet, HEADER_ROW);
  const headerMap = buildHeaderIndexMap_(headers);
  const pmrIdx = getPMRIndex_(headerMap);
  const primaryIdx = headerMap["Primary PMR Row"];


  if (pmrIdx === -1) {
    notify_("Sort Order skipped: Participant PMR# / PMR # column not found.");
    return;
  }


  const sortIdx = sortCol - 1;
  const dataRange = sheet.getRange(DATA_START_ROW, 1, lastRow - DATA_START_ROW + 1, lastCol);
  const values = dataRange.getValues();


  const blankOrNoPMRRows = [];
  values.forEach((row, idx) => {
    const pmr = normalizePMR_(row[pmrIdx]);
    if (pmr) return;
    if (primaryIdx !== undefined) row[primaryIdx] = "";
    row[sortIdx] = "";
    blankOrNoPMRRows.push({ row: row, originalIndex: idx });
  });


  const blocks = buildParticipantBlocksForSortOrder_(values, headerMap, pmrIdx);


  blocks.forEach(block => {
    assignPrimaryRowForBlock_(block, headerMap, primaryIdx);
  });


  blocks.sort((a, b) => {
    const aLast = normalizeKeyPart_(a.lastName);
    const bLast = normalizeKeyPart_(b.lastName);
    if (aLast !== bLast) return aLast < bLast ? -1 : 1;


    const aFirst = normalizeKeyPart_(a.firstName);
    const bFirst = normalizeKeyPart_(b.firstName);
    if (aFirst !== bFirst) return aFirst < bFirst ? -1 : 1;


    const aPMR = normalizePMR_(a.pmr);
    const bPMR = normalizePMR_(b.pmr);
    if (aPMR !== bPMR) return aPMR < bPMR ? -1 : 1;


    return 0;
  });


  let participantNumber = 1;
  const outputRows = [];


  blocks.forEach(block => {
    block.rows.sort((a, b) => {
      const aPrimary = isPrimaryPMRRowValue_(a.row[primaryIdx]);
      const bPrimary = isPrimaryPMRRowValue_(b.row[primaryIdx]);


      if (aPrimary !== bPrimary) return aPrimary ? -1 : 1;


      return a.originalIndex - b.originalIndex;
    });


    block.rows.forEach((item, idx) => {
      item.row[sortIdx] = idx === 0 ? participantNumber : Number((participantNumber + (idx / 1000)).toFixed(3));
      outputRows.push(item.row);
    });


    participantNumber++;
  });


  blankOrNoPMRRows.sort((a, b) => a.originalIndex - b.originalIndex);
  blankOrNoPMRRows.forEach(item => outputRows.push(item.row));


  if (outputRows.length > 0) {
    dataRange.setValues(outputRows);
    sheet.getRange(DATA_START_ROW, sortCol, outputRows.length, 1);
    sheet.getRange(DATA_START_ROW, primaryCol, outputRows.length, 1);
  }
}
function ensurePrimaryPMRRowColumn_(sheet) {
  const headers = getHeaders_(sheet, HEADER_ROW);
  const idx = headers.indexOf("Primary PMR Row");
  if (idx !== -1) return idx + 1;


  const newCol = Math.max(headers.length, sheet.getLastColumn(), 1) + 1;
  if (sheet.getMaxColumns() < newCol) {
    sheet.insertColumnsAfter(sheet.getMaxColumns(), newCol - sheet.getMaxColumns());
  }
  sheet.getRange(HEADER_ROW, newCol).setValue("Primary PMR Row");
  clearSheetRuntimeCachesForSheet_(sheet);
  return newCol;
}


function assignPrimaryPMRRows_(sheet) {
  sheet = sheet || SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSheet();


  ensurePrimaryPMRRowColumn_(sheet);


  const lastRow = sheet.getLastRow();
  const lastCol = sheet.getLastColumn();
  if (lastRow < DATA_START_ROW || lastCol < 1) return;


  const headers = getHeaders_(sheet, HEADER_ROW);
  const headerMap = buildHeaderIndexMap_(headers);
  const pmrIdx = getPMRIndex_(headerMap);
  const primaryIdx = headerMap["Primary PMR Row"];
  if (pmrIdx === -1 || primaryIdx === undefined) return;


  const dataRange = sheet.getRange(DATA_START_ROW, 1, lastRow - DATA_START_ROW + 1, lastCol);
  const values = dataRange.getValues();


  values.forEach(row => {
    if (!normalizePMR_(row[pmrIdx])) row[primaryIdx] = "";
  });


  const blocks = buildParticipantBlocksForSortOrder_(values, headerMap, pmrIdx);


  blocks.forEach(block => assignPrimaryRowForBlock_(block, headerMap, primaryIdx));


  dataRange.setValues(values);
}
function assignPrimaryRowForBlock_(block, headerMap, primaryIdx) {
  if (!block || !block.rows || block.rows.length === 0 || primaryIdx === undefined) return;


  let primaryItem = block.rows.find(item => isPrimaryPMRRowValue_(item.row[primaryIdx]));


  if (!primaryItem) {
    primaryItem = block.rows.slice().sort((a, b) => {
      const scoreA = getPrimaryRowScoreForSortOrder_(a.row, headerMap);
      const scoreB = getPrimaryRowScoreForSortOrder_(b.row, headerMap);


      if (scoreA !== scoreB) return scoreB - scoreA;
      return a.originalIndex - b.originalIndex;
    })[0];
  }


  block.rows.forEach(item => {
    item.row[primaryIdx] = item === primaryItem ? "Yes" : "";
  });
}


function isPrimaryPMRRowValue_(value) {
  const text = String(value || "").trim().toLowerCase();
  return text === "yes" || text === "y" || text === "true" || text === "primary" || text === "1";
}


function isPrimaryPMRRow_(row, headerMap) {
  const primaryIdx = headerMap["Primary PMR Row"];
  if (primaryIdx === undefined) return false;
  return isPrimaryPMRRowValue_(row[primaryIdx]);
}


function ensureSortOrderColumn_(sheet) {
  /*
   * v1.4.24:
   * Do not create Sort Order at runtime. It must exist from the dashboard Sheet
   * Headers/template definition when a workflow requires it.
   */
  const headers = getHeaders_(sheet, HEADER_ROW);
  const idx = headers.indexOf("Sort Order");
  return idx !== -1 ? idx + 1 : -1;
}


function buildParticipantBlocksForSortOrder_(values, headerMap, pmrIdx) {
  const lastNameIdx = headerMap["Last Name"];
  const firstNameIdx = headerMap["First Name"];


  const blocksByPMR = new Map();


  values.forEach((row, idx) => {
    const pmr = normalizePMR_(row[pmrIdx]);


    if (!pmr) return;


    if (!blocksByPMR.has(pmr)) {
      blocksByPMR.set(pmr, {
        pmr: pmr,
        lastName: lastNameIdx !== undefined ? row[lastNameIdx] : "",
        firstName: firstNameIdx !== undefined ? row[firstNameIdx] : "",
        rows: []
      });
    }


    const block = blocksByPMR.get(pmr);


    if (!String(block.lastName || "").trim() && lastNameIdx !== undefined && String(row[lastNameIdx] || "").trim()) {
      block.lastName = row[lastNameIdx];
    }


    if (!String(block.firstName || "").trim() && firstNameIdx !== undefined && String(row[firstNameIdx] || "").trim()) {
      block.firstName = row[firstNameIdx];
    }


    block.rows.push({ row: row, originalIndex: idx });
  });


  return Array.from(blocksByPMR.values());
}
function getPrimaryRowScoreForSortOrder_(row, headerMap) {
  let score = 0;


  const checks = [
    ["Date of Birth", 1000],
    ["Enrollment Date", 250],
    ["Capitation Date", 200],
    ["Address Line 1", 100],
    ["Phone Number", 50],
    ["Primary Language", 25],
    ["Participant Name", 20],
    ["PMR #", 10]
  ];


  checks.forEach(pair => {
    const idx = headerMap[pair[0]];
    if (idx !== undefined && normalizeCompareValue_(row[idx]) !== "") {
      score += pair[1];
    }
  });


  return score;
}


function sortBySortOrder_(sheet) {
  sheet = sheet || SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSheet();


  const headers = getHeaders_(sheet, HEADER_ROW);
  const sortIdx = headers.indexOf("Sort Order");


  if (sortIdx === -1) return;


  const lastRow = sheet.getLastRow();
  const lastCol = sheet.getLastColumn();


  if (lastRow < DATA_START_ROW || lastCol < 1) return;


  sheet.getRange(DATA_START_ROW, 1, lastRow - DATA_START_ROW + 1, lastCol)
    .sort([{ column: sortIdx + 1, ascending: true }]);
}


function hideDecimalSortOrderRows_(sheet) {
  sheet = sheet || SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSheet();


  const headers = getHeaders_(sheet, HEADER_ROW);
  const sortIdx = headers.indexOf("Sort Order");


  if (sortIdx === -1) return;


  const lastRow = sheet.getLastRow();


  if (lastRow < DATA_START_ROW) return;


  sheet.showRows(DATA_START_ROW, lastRow - DATA_START_ROW + 1);


  const values = sheet.getRange(DATA_START_ROW, sortIdx + 1, lastRow - DATA_START_ROW + 1, 1).getValues();
  const rowsToHide = [];


  values.forEach((row, idx) => {
    if (isDecimalSortOrder_(row[0])) {
      rowsToHide.push(DATA_START_ROW + idx);
    }
  });


  hideRowNumberBatches_(sheet, rowsToHide);
}

function isDecimalSortOrder_(value) {
  const num = Number(value);
  if (isNaN(num)) return false;
  return Math.abs(num - Math.floor(num)) > 0.000001;
}


function getWholeSortOrderNumber_(value) {
  const num = Number(value);
  if (isNaN(num)) return 0;
  return Math.floor(num);
}

  if (sheet.getMaxRows() >= DATA_START_ROW) {
    sheet.showRows(DATA_START_ROW, sheet.getMaxRows() - DATA_START_ROW + 1);
  }


  notify_("All rows shown.");
}

function getSystemSheetCreationDate_(sheet) {
  const existing = coerceToValidDate_(sheet.getRange("B2").getValue()) ||
    coerceToValidDate_(sheet.getRange("B2").getDisplayValue());


  if (existing) return existing;


  return createLocalDateOnly_(new Date().getFullYear(), new Date().getMonth(), new Date().getDate());
}


function getSystemSheetLastUpdatedDate_() {
  return createLocalDateOnly_(new Date().getFullYear(), new Date().getMonth(), new Date().getDate());
}


function applySystemSheetStandardTitle_(sheet, sheetType, title) {
  const creationDate = getSystemSheetCreationDate_(sheet);
  const lastUpdatedDate = getSystemSheetLastUpdatedDate_();


  applyStandardFormatting_(sheet, {
    sheetType: sheetType,
    title: title,
    startDate: creationDate,
    endDate: lastUpdatedDate,
    titleInfoText: "",
    renameSheet: false
  });


  sheet.getRange("A2").setValue("Creation Date");
  sheet.getRange("B2").setValue(dateOnlyLocalClone_(creationDate));
  sheet.getRange("C2").setValue("to");
  sheet.getRange("D2").setValue(dateOnlyLocalClone_(lastUpdatedDate));


  forceStandardTitleCellAlignment_(sheet);
}function formatMasterListChangeLogStandardTitle() {
  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  const sheet = ss.getSheetByName(MASTER_LIST_CHANGE_LOG_SHEET) || SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSheet();


  applySystemSheetStandardTitle_(sheet, SHEET_TYPE.MASTER_LIST_CHANGE_LOG, SHEET_TYPE.MASTER_LIST_CHANGE_LOG);
  notify_("Master List Change Log standard title applied.");
}


function applySystemSheetStandardTitles_() {
  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  const exclusionSheet = ss.getSheetByName(DISENROLLED_EXCLUSION_SHEET);
  const logSheet = ss.getSheetByName(MASTER_LIST_CHANGE_LOG_SHEET);


  if (exclusionSheet) {
    applySystemSheetStandardTitle_(exclusionSheet, SHEET_TYPE.DISENROLLED_EXCLUSION, SHEET_TYPE.DISENROLLED_EXCLUSION);
  }


  if (logSheet) {
    applySystemSheetStandardTitle_(logSheet, SHEET_TYPE.MASTER_LIST_CHANGE_LOG, SHEET_TYPE.MASTER_LIST_CHANGE_LOG);
  }
}function applySystemSheetCreateFormattingOnly_(sheet, sheetType, title) {
  if (!sheet) return;


  if (hasStandardTitleRows_(sheet)) {
    applyStandardFreeze_(sheet);
    forceStandardTitleCellAlignment_(sheet);
    return;
  }


  applySystemSheetStandardTitle_(sheet, sheetType, title);
  applyStandardFreeze_(sheet);
  forceStandardTitleCellAlignment_(sheet);
}

}


function applyIndexSheetRowFills_(sheet) {
  if (!sheet) return;


  const lastRow = sheet.getLastRow();
  const lastCol = INDEX_HEADERS.length;


  if (lastRow < 2) return;


  const indexValues = sheet.getRange(2, 1, lastRow - 1, INDEX_HEADERS.length).getDisplayValues();


  const rowItems = indexValues.map(row => {
    return {
      monthText: String(row[0] || "").trim(),
      sheetName: String(row[1] || "").trim(),
      sheetTypeText: String(row[3] || "").trim(),
      date: parseIndexMonthDate_(row[0]) || extractFirstDateFromSheetName_(row[1])
    };
  });


  const newestDate = getNewestMonthlySheetDate_(rowItems);


  const backgrounds = rowItems.map(item => {
    const standardType = getStandardSheetTypeFromOrganizationType_(item.sheetTypeText);
    const baseColor = standardType ? SHEET_BASE_COLORS[standardType] : null;


    if (!baseColor) {
      return new Array(lastCol).fill("#ffffff");
    }


    const theme = getThemeColorsFromBase_(baseColor);
    const isCurrent = item.date && newestDate && item.date.getTime() === newestDate.getTime();


    const fillColor = isCurrent ? theme.level3 : theme.level2;


    return new Array(lastCol).fill(fillColor);
  });


  sheet.getRange(2, 1, backgrounds.length, lastCol);
}


function organizeSheetTabs_() {
  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  const categorized = ss.getSheets().map(sheet => {
    const name = sheet.getName();


    return {
      sheet: sheet,
      name: name,
      type: getSheetTypeForOrganization_(name),
      date: extractFirstDateFromSheetName_(name)
    };
  });


  const newestDate = getNewestMonthlySheetDate_(categorized);


  const indexItems = [];
  const currentSheets = [];
  const referenceSheets = [];
  const olderSheets = [];


  categorized.forEach(item => {
    if (item.name === "Index") {
      indexItems.push(item);
      return;
    }


    if (isReferenceSheetForOrganization_(item.name)) {
      referenceSheets.push(item);
      return;
    }


    if (item.date && newestDate && item.date.getTime() === newestDate.getTime()) {
      currentSheets.push(item);
    } else {
      olderSheets.push(item);
    }
  });


  indexItems.sort(compareSheetOrganization_);
  currentSheets.sort(compareSheetOrganization_);
  referenceSheets.sort(compareSheetOrganization_);
  olderSheets.sort(compareOlderSheetOrganization_);


  const ordered = indexItems.concat(currentSheets).concat(referenceSheets).concat(olderSheets);


  ordered.forEach((item, idx) => {
    ss.setActiveSheet(item.sheet);
    ss.moveActiveSheet(idx + 1);
  });
}


function getSheetTypeForOrganization_(name) {
  const lower = String(name || "").toLowerCase();


  if (lower === "index") return "Index";
  if (lower.indexOf("master list change log") !== -1 || lower.indexOf("change log") !== -1) return "Master List Change Log";
  if (lower.indexOf("disenrollment exclusion") !== -1 || lower.indexOf("disenrolled exclusion") !== -1) return "Disenrolled Exclusion List";
  if (lower.indexOf("monthly change") !== -1) return "Monthly Change Report";
  if (lower.indexOf("master list") !== -1) return "Master List";
  if (lower.indexOf("demo p") !== -1) return "Demo P";
  if (lower.indexOf("care plan due") !== -1) return "Care Plan Due Date Report";
  if (lower.indexOf("unlock") !== -1) return "Unlocked Care Plan Report";
  if (lower.indexOf("banner") !== -1) return "Banner Report";


  return "Other";
}


function isReferenceSheetForOrganization_(name) {
  const lower = String(name || "").toLowerCase();


  return (
    lower.indexOf("change log") !== -1 ||
    lower.indexOf("disenrollment exclusion") !== -1 ||
    lower.indexOf("disenrolled exclusion") !== -1
  );
}


function compareSheetOrganization_(a, b) {
  const aIndex = SHEET_TAB_ORDER.indexOf(a.type);
  const bIndex = SHEET_TAB_ORDER.indexOf(b.type);
  const aOrder = aIndex === -1 ? 999 : aIndex;
  const bOrder = bIndex === -1 ? 999 : bIndex;


  if (aOrder !== bOrder) return aOrder - bOrder;


  return String(a.name).localeCompare(String(b.name));
}


function compareOlderSheetOrganization_(a, b) {
  if (a.date && b.date && a.date.getTime() !== b.date.getTime()) {
    return b.date.getTime() - a.date.getTime();
  }


  return compareSheetOrganization_(a, b);
}


function getNewestMonthlySheetDate_(items) {
  const dates = items
    .map(item => item.date)
    .filter(Boolean)
    .sort((a, b) => b.getTime() - a.getTime());


  return dates.length ? dates[0] : null;
}


function applyCurrentVsOlderTabColors_(ss, currentMonthParts) {
  // v1.1.0: Runtime tab-color formatting removed. Dashboard templates are formatting authority.
  return;
}




function getStandardSheetTypeFromOrganizationType_(orgType) {
  switch (orgType) {
    case "Master List":
      return SHEET_TYPE.MASTER_LIST;
    case "Demo P":
      return SHEET_TYPE.DEMO_P;
    case "Care Plan Due Date Report":
      return SHEET_TYPE.CARE_PLAN_DUE;
    case "Unlocked Care Plan Report":
      return SHEET_TYPE.UNLOCKED;
    case "Banner Report":
      return SHEET_TYPE.BANNER;
    case "Monthly Change Report":
      return SHEET_TYPE.MONTHLY_CHANGE;
    case "Master List Change Log":
      return SHEET_TYPE.MASTER_LIST_CHANGE_LOG;
    case "Disenrolled Exclusion List":
      return SHEET_TYPE.DISENROLLED_EXCLUSION;
    default:
      return null;
  }
}


function moveCellTextToTargetAndClearSources_(sheet, sourceA1List, targetA1) {
  const text = collectCellTextWithSpaces_(sheet, sourceA1List);


  sheet.getRange(targetA1).setValue(text);


  sourceA1List.forEach(a1 => {
    try {
      sheet.getRange(a1).clearContent();
    } catch (err) {
      Logger.log("Could not clear moved source cell " + a1 + ": " + err.message);
    }
  });


  return text;
}
