function formatRawData() {
  const sourceSheet = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSheet();
  const monthParts = promptForLockedYearReportMonth_("Format Raw Data");
  if (!monthParts) return;


  const timing = startRuntimeTiming_("Format Raw Data", monthParts);


  try {
    if (!sourceSheet) {
      throw new Error("No active sheet found. Select the imported Raw Data sheet before running Format Raw Data.");
    }


    const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
    const dashboard = loadDashboardConfig_();
    const sheetDef = getSheetDefinitionByType_(dashboard, SHEET_TYPE.RAW_DATA);
    const outputName = buildRawDataSheetName_(monthParts);
    const sourceName = sourceSheet.getName();


    if (sourceName === sheetDef.templateName || sourceName === outputName) {
      throw new Error("The active sheet is not a Raw Data import sheet. Select the imported Raw Data source sheet before formatting.");
    }


    ensureRawDataHeaderRows_(sourceSheet);
    markRuntimeStep_(timing, "Ensure Raw Data title/header row structure");


    let headers = getRawDataCurrentHeadersOrDefaults_(sourceSheet);
    headers = prepareRawDataSourceSheetForDashboardFormat_(sourceSheet, headers);
    ensurePrimaryPMRRowColumn_(sourceSheet);
    headers = getHeaders_(sourceSheet, HEADER_ROW);
    markRuntimeStep_(timing, "Normalize Raw Data headers and ensure Primary PMR Row");


    const templateHeaders = getHeadersForSheetType_(dashboard, sheetDef.sheetType);
    const rawData = getDataValues_(sourceSheet, HEADER_ROW, DATA_START_ROW);
    const outputRows = mapRowsToHeaders_(rawData.values, rawData.headers, templateHeaders);


    deleteSheetIfExists_(ss, outputName, sourceName, sheetDef.templateName);
    const outputSheet = createRawDataOutputSheetFromTemplateFast_(
      sheetDef.sheetType,
      outputName,
      outputRows,
      monthParts.firstDay,
      monthParts.lastDay,
      sourceName
    );
    markRuntimeStep_(timing, "Create Raw Data output from template skeleton and paste values");


    processRawDataApprovedSyncColumns_(outputSheet, monthParts);
    markRuntimeStep_(timing, "Populate Raw Data approved sync column: Primary PMR Row");


    if (sourceSheet.getSheetId() !== outputSheet.getSheetId() && ss.getSheets().length > 1) {
      ss.setActiveSheet(outputSheet);
      ss.deleteSheet(sourceSheet);
      markRuntimeStep_(timing, "Delete source Raw Data import sheet");
    }


    lockFinalOutputRowHeights_(outputSheet, "Raw Data");
    markRuntimeStep_(timing, "Lock Raw Data final row heights");


    clearSheetRuntimeCachesForSheet_(outputSheet);
    writeRuntimeTimingReport_(timing);


    notify_(
      "Raw Data formatted as " + outputName + ".\n" +
      "Template-driven output created from Template - Raw Data.\n" +
      "Primary PMR Row was added/populated. Run Process Demo P next when ready."
    );


    return outputSheet;
  } catch (err) {
    markRuntimeStep_(timing, "ERROR - " + err.message);
    writeRuntimeTimingReport_(timing);
    notify_("Format Raw Data stopped: " + err.message + "\nTiming log updated: " + FORMAT_DEMO_P_TIMING_SHEET);
    throw err;
  }
}


function ensureRawDataHeaderRows_(sheet) {
  if (!sheet) return;


  const row4Headers = sheet.getRange(HEADER_ROW, 1, 1, Math.max(sheet.getLastColumn(), 1)).getValues()[0];
  if (rowLooksLikeParticipantHeader_(row4Headers)) return;


  const row1Headers = sheet.getRange(1, 1, 1, Math.max(sheet.getLastColumn(), 1)).getValues()[0];
  if (rowLooksLikeParticipantHeader_(row1Headers)) {
    sheet.insertRowsBefore(1, HEADER_ROW - 1);
    clearSheetRuntimeCachesForSheet_(sheet);
    return;
  }


  // If neither row clearly looks like the source header, do not destructively
  // move rows. The existing formatter will surface missing-header errors later.
}


function rowLooksLikeParticipantHeader_(row) {
  const normalized = (row || []).map(function(value) {
    return normalizeHeader_(value);
  });
  const required = ["Last Name", "First Name", "Participant PMR#"].map(normalizeHeader_);
  return required.every(function(header) {
    return normalized.indexOf(header) !== -1;
  });
}


function getRawDataCurrentHeadersOrDefaults_(sheet) {
  const current = getHeaders_(sheet, HEADER_ROW)
    .map(function(header) { return String(header || "").trim(); })
    .filter(function(header) { return header !== ""; });
  return current.length ? current : getRawDataDemoPSourceHeaders_();
}




function enforceDemoPStrictDashboardSchema_(sheet) {
  /*
   * v1.4.24:
   * This function no longer inserts or deletes columns. Dashboard Section C is
   * the column authority; Template Header Audit reports drift.
   */
  if (!sheet) return;


  const dashboard = loadDashboardConfig_();
  const expectedHeaders = getHeadersForSheetType_(dashboard, SHEET_TYPE.DEMO_P)
    .map(normalizeHeader_);
  const expectedSet = {};
  expectedHeaders.forEach(function(header) {
    if (header) expectedSet[header] = true;
  });


  const currentHeaders = getHeaders_(sheet, HEADER_ROW).map(normalizeHeader_);
  const currentSet = {};
  currentHeaders.forEach(function(header) {
    if (header) currentSet[header] = true;
  });


  const missing = expectedHeaders.filter(function(header) {
    return header && !currentSet[header];
  });
  const unexpected = currentHeaders.filter(function(header) {
    return header && !expectedSet[header];
  });


  if (missing.length || unexpected.length) {
    Logger.log(
      "Demo P header drift detected. Missing: " +
      missing.join(", ") +
      " Unexpected: " +
      unexpected.join(", ")
    );
  }


  clearSheetRuntimeCachesForSheet_(sheet);
}


function processDemoP() {
  const monthParts = promptForLockedYearReportMonth_("Process Demo P");
  if (!monthParts) return;


  const timing = startRuntimeTiming_("Process Demo P", monthParts);
  let movedResult = {
    pmrsRemoved: 0,
    rowsRemoved: 0,
    rowsCopied: 0
  };


  try {
    const buildResult = getOrCreateDemoPProcessingSheet_(monthParts, timing);
    const sheet = buildResult && buildResult.sheet ? buildResult.sheet : buildResult;


    if (buildResult && buildResult.movedResult) {
      movedResult = buildResult.movedResult;
    }


    ensureStandardTitleRows_(sheet);
    markRuntimeStep_(timing, "Prepare Demo P title/header rows");


    enforceDemoPStrictDashboardSchema_(sheet);
    clearSheetRuntimeCachesForSheet_(sheet);
    markRuntimeStep_(timing, "Enforce Demo P strict dashboard schema and clear caches");


    if (!buildResult || !buildResult.sourceWasRawData) {
      movedResult = moveDisenrolledPMRsFromDemoPToExclusion_(sheet, monthParts);
      markRuntimeStep_(
        timing,
        "Move disenrolled PMRs to exclusion list - PMRs removed: " + movedResult.pmrsRemoved +
          ", rows copied: " + movedResult.rowsCopied +
          ", rows removed: " + movedResult.rowsRemoved
      );


      processDemoPAsWorkingSource_(sheet, monthParts, timing);
    } else {
      markRuntimeStep_(
        timing,
        "Disenrolled exclusion built from Raw Data - PMRs excluded from Demo P: " + movedResult.pmrsRemoved +
          ", rows copied: " + movedResult.rowsCopied
      );


      if (buildResult.preProcessedWorkingSource) {
        markRuntimeStep_(timing, "Demo P Working Source processing skipped - already completed in optimized Raw Data single-pass build");
      } else {
        processDemoPAsWorkingSource_(sheet, monthParts, timing);
      }
    }


    if (buildResult && buildResult.createdFromDashboardTemplate) {
      markRuntimeStep_(timing, "Apply Demo P dashboard template formatting skipped - template copy already formatted");
    } else {
      applyDemoPTemplateToSheet_(sheet, monthParts);
      markRuntimeStep_(timing, "Apply Demo P dashboard template formatting");
    }


    setUniqueSheetName_(
      sheet,
      buildMonthlySheetNameNoDashAfterPrefix_(
        "Demo P",
        monthParts.firstDay,
        monthParts.lastDay
      )
    );
    markRuntimeStep_(timing, "Rename processed Demo P sheet");


    lockFinalOutputRowHeights_(sheet, "Demo P");
    markRuntimeStep_(timing, "Lock Demo P final row heights");


    writeRuntimeTimingReport_(timing);


    notify_(
      "Demo P processed as the working source.\n" +
      "Raw Data preserved when source sheet was Raw Data.\n" +
      "Demo P contains active participants only when built from Raw Data.\n" +
      "Disenrolled PMRs excluded from Demo P: " + movedResult.pmrsRemoved + "\n" +
      "Disenrolled primary rows copied to exclusion list: " + movedResult.rowsCopied + "\n" +
      "Contact, phone, address, language, notes, banner, and Primary PMR fields were processed on Demo P.\n" +
      "Care Plan Due and Unlocked Care Plan remain Master List sync functions.\n" +
      "Master List can now be created from Primary PMR rows only."
    );


    return sheet;
  } catch (err) {
    markRuntimeStep_(timing, "ERROR - " + err.message);
    writeRuntimeTimingReport_(timing);
    notify_("Process Demo P stopped: " + err.message + "\nTiming log updated: " + FORMAT_DEMO_P_TIMING_SHEET);
    throw err;
  }
}






function processDemoPAsWorkingSource_(sheet, monthParts, timing) {
  enforceDemoPStrictDashboardSchema_(sheet);
  markRuntimeStep_(timing, "Demo P Working Source - verify strict working-source headers");


  const data = getDataValues_(sheet, HEADER_ROW, DATA_START_ROW);
  markRuntimeStep_(timing, "Demo P Working Source - read Demo P data range");
  if (!data.values.length) return;


  /*
   * v1.4.23:
   * Primary PMR Row is assigned during Format Raw Data and copied into Demo P.
   * Do not verify, rescan, or reassign Primary PMR ownership here.
   * Banner values are also sourced from Raw Data; do not sync a newest Banners sheet
   * into Demo P memory during this process.
   */


  updateBannerColumnData_(data, null);
  markRuntimeStep_(timing, "Demo P Working Source - build Banner Summary");


  combineAddressesData_(data, null);
  markRuntimeStep_(timing, "Demo P Working Source - combine address fields");


  handleLanguageData_(data, null);
  markRuntimeStep_(timing, "Demo P Working Source - process language fields");


  splitPhoneNumbersData_(data, null);
  markRuntimeStep_(timing, "Demo P Working Source - split phone fields");


  runMasterContactProcessData_(data, null);
  markRuntimeStep_(timing, "Demo P Working Source - process contacts");


  combineNotesSummaryData_(data, null);
  markRuntimeStep_(timing, "Demo P Working Source - combine Notes Summary");


  if (data.range) data.range.setValues(data.values);
  markRuntimeStep_(timing, "Demo P Working Source - single write processed Demo P data");


  clearSheetRuntimeCachesForSheet_(sheet);
}


function markPrimaryPMRRowsForSequentialData_(data) {
  if (!data || !data.values || !data.values.length || !data.headerMap) return;


  const headerMap = data.headerMap;
  const pmrIdx = getPMRIndex_(headerMap);
  const primaryIdx = headerMap["Primary PMR Row"];


  if (pmrIdx === -1 || primaryIdx === undefined) return;


  let previousPMR = "";


  data.values.forEach(row => {
    const pmr = normalizePMR_(row[pmrIdx]);


    if (!pmr) {
      row[primaryIdx] = "";
      return;
    }


    row[primaryIdx] = pmr !== previousPMR ? "Yes" : "";
    previousPMR = pmr;
  });
}




function assignPrimaryPMRRowsInData_(data) {
  if (!data || !data.values || !data.values.length || !data.headerMap) return;


  const headerMap = data.headerMap;
  const pmrIdx = getPMRIndex_(headerMap);
  const primaryIdx = headerMap["Primary PMR Row"];


  if (pmrIdx === -1 || primaryIdx === undefined) return;


  data.values.forEach(row => {
    if (!normalizePMR_(row[pmrIdx])) row[primaryIdx] = "";
  });


  const blocks = buildParticipantBlocksForSortOrder_(data.values, headerMap, pmrIdx);
  blocks.forEach(block => assignPrimaryRowForBlock_(block, headerMap, primaryIdx));
}






function formatDemoPStructure() {
  return processDemoP();
}


function buildRawDataSheetName_(monthParts) {
  return "Raw Data " + Utilities.formatDate(monthParts.firstDay, Session.getScriptTimeZone(), "MM.yy");
}


function buildRawDataSourceArchiveName_(monthParts) {
  return "Raw Data - Source " + Utilities.formatDate(monthParts.firstDay, Session.getScriptTimeZone(), "MM.yy");
}


function getOrCreateDemoPProcessingSheet_(monthParts, timing) {
  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  const active = ss.getActiveSheet();
  const rawName = buildRawDataSheetName_(monthParts);
  const targetName = buildMonthlySheetNameNoDashAfterPrefix_("Demo P", monthParts.firstDay, monthParts.lastDay);


  if (!active) {
    throw new Error("No active sheet found. Select the Raw Data sheet or existing Demo P sheet before running Process Demo P.");
  }


  const activeName = String(active.getName() || "").trim();
  const activeLower = activeName.toLowerCase();


  if (activeName === targetName || activeLower.indexOf("demo p") === 0) {
    markRuntimeStep_(timing, "Using active Demo P sheet: " + activeName);
    return {
      sheet: active,
      sourceWasRawData: false,
      movedResult: {
        pmrsRemoved: 0,
        rowsRemoved: 0,
        rowsCopied: 0
      },
      preProcessedWorkingSource: false
    };
  }


  let rawSheet = null;


  if (activeName === rawName || activeLower.indexOf("raw data") === 0) {
    rawSheet = active;
  } else {
    rawSheet = ss.getSheetByName(rawName);
  }


  if (!rawSheet) {
    throw new Error("Raw Data sheet was not found for " + Utilities.formatDate(monthParts.firstDay, Session.getScriptTimeZone(), "MM.yy") + ". Run Format Raw Data first.");
  }


  deleteSheetIfExistsForDemoPProcess_(ss, targetName, rawSheet.getName());


  const buildResult = createActiveDemoPFromRawData_(rawSheet, targetName, monthParts, timing);
  const demoSheet = buildResult && buildResult.sheet ? buildResult.sheet : buildResult;


  ss.setActiveSheet(demoSheet);
  clearSheetRuntimeCachesForSheet_(demoSheet);
  markRuntimeStep_(timing, "Active-only processed Demo P built from protected Raw Data: " + targetName);


  return {
    sheet: demoSheet,
    sourceWasRawData: true,
    createdFromDashboardTemplate: true,
    preProcessedWorkingSource: !!(buildResult && buildResult.preProcessedWorkingSource),
    movedResult: (buildResult && buildResult.movedResult) ? buildResult.movedResult : getLastRawDataDisenrolledBuildResult_()
  };
}






function deleteSheetIfExistsForDemoPProcess_(ss, sheetName, protectedSheetName) {
  const existing = ss.getSheetByName(sheetName);
  if (!existing) return;


  if (existing.getName() === protectedSheetName) {
    throw new Error("Cannot replace Demo P processing sheet because it is also the protected Raw Data sheet.");
  }


  ss.deleteSheet(existing);
  clearMonthlySheetLookupCache_();
}




const ML_LAST_RAW_DATA_DISENROLLED_BUILD_RESULT_ = {
  pmrsRemoved: 0,
  rowsRemoved: 0,
  rowsCopied: 0
};


function getLastRawDataDisenrolledBuildResult_() {
  return {
    pmrsRemoved: ML_LAST_RAW_DATA_DISENROLLED_BUILD_RESULT_.pmrsRemoved || 0,
    rowsRemoved: ML_LAST_RAW_DATA_DISENROLLED_BUILD_RESULT_.rowsRemoved || 0,
    rowsCopied: ML_LAST_RAW_DATA_DISENROLLED_BUILD_RESULT_.rowsCopied || 0
  };
}


function setLastRawDataDisenrolledBuildResult_(result) {
  result = result || {};
  ML_LAST_RAW_DATA_DISENROLLED_BUILD_RESULT_.pmrsRemoved = result.pmrsRemoved || 0;
  ML_LAST_RAW_DATA_DISENROLLED_BUILD_RESULT_.rowsRemoved = result.rowsRemoved || 0;
  ML_LAST_RAW_DATA_DISENROLLED_BUILD_RESULT_.rowsCopied = result.rowsCopied || 0;
}




function createDisenrolledList() {
  const monthParts = promptForLockedYearReportMonth_("Create Disenrolled List");
  if (!monthParts) return;


  const timing = startRuntimeTiming_("Create Disenrolled List", monthParts);


  try {
    const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
    const rawName = buildRawDataSheetName_(monthParts);
    const rawSheet = ss.getSheetByName(rawName);


    if (!rawSheet) {
      throw new Error("Raw Data sheet was not found for " + Utilities.formatDate(monthParts.firstDay, Session.getScriptTimeZone(), "MM.yy") + ". Expected sheet: " + rawName);
    }
    markRuntimeStep_(timing, "Locate Raw Data source sheet: " + rawName);


    const rawData = getDataValues_(rawSheet, HEADER_ROW, DATA_START_ROW);
    if (!rawData.values.length) {
      throw new Error("Raw Data sheet has no participant rows: " + rawName);
    }
    markRuntimeStep_(timing, "Read Raw Data values");


    const split = splitRawDataRowsIntoActiveAndDisenrolled_(rawData);
    markRuntimeStep_(timing, "Identify disenrolled PMRs by sequential block scan");


    const rowsCopied = appendDisenrolledRowsFromRawDataToExclusion_(
      rawSheet,
      rawData.headers,
      split.disenrolledRowsByPMR,
      monthParts
    );
    markRuntimeStep_(timing, "Write Disenrolled Exclusion primary rows only: " + rowsCopied);


    const result = {
      pmrsRemoved: split.disenrolledPMRs.size,
      rowsRemoved: 0,
      rowsCopied: rowsCopied,
      primaryRowsOnly: true
    };
    setLastRawDataDisenrolledBuildResult_(result);


    writeRuntimeTimingReport_(timing);


    notify_(
      "Disenrolled List created from " + rawName + " as " + buildDatedDisenrolledOutputName_(monthParts) + ".\n" +
      "PMRs identified: " + split.disenrolledPMRs.size + "\n" +
      "Primary rows written: " + rowsCopied + "\n" +
      "Process Demo P no longer rebuilds this list automatically."
    );


    return result;
  } catch (err) {
    markRuntimeStep_(timing, "ERROR - " + err.message);
    writeRuntimeTimingReport_(timing);
    notify_("Create Disenrolled List stopped: " + err.message);
    throw err;
  }
}


function createDisenrollmentList() {
  return createDisenrolledList();
}


function createActiveDemoPFromRawData_(rawSheet, targetName, monthParts, timing) {
  const rawData = getDataValues_(rawSheet, HEADER_ROW, DATA_START_ROW);

  if (!rawData.values.length) {
    throw new Error("Raw Data has no participant rows to process.");
  }

  const pmrIdx = getPMRIndex_(rawData.headerMap);
  if (pmrIdx === -1) {
    throw new Error("Raw Data is missing Participant PMR# / PMR # column.");
  }

  const disenrolledPMRSet = loadDisenrolledPMRSetForMonth_(monthParts);
  const split = splitRawDataRowsIntoActiveAndDisenrolled_(rawData, disenrolledPMRSet);
  const movedResult = {
    pmrsRemoved: split.disenrolledPMRs.size,
    rowsRemoved: 0,
    rowsCopied: split.disenrolledRows.length,
    primaryRowsOnly: true
  };

  setLastRawDataDisenrolledBuildResult_(movedResult);

  movedResult.outputRowsWritten = 0;
  markRuntimeStep_(timing, "Disenrolled PMRs identified and excluded from Demo P - " +
    (disenrolledPMRSet && disenrolledPMRSet.size ? "used Disenrolled List PMR set" : "used Raw Data disenrollment fields") +
    " | Rows Read: " + rawData.values.length +
    "; Rows Processed: " + split.activeRows.length +
    "; Rows Excluded: " + split.disenrolledRows.length);

  const dashboard = loadDashboardConfig_();
  const sheetDef = getSheetDefinitionByType_(dashboard, SHEET_TYPE.DEMO_P);
  const headers = getHeadersForSheetType_(dashboard, SHEET_TYPE.DEMO_P);
  const outputRows = mapRowsToHeaders_(split.activeRows, rawData.headers, headers);

  const workingData = {
    headers: headers,
    headerMap: buildHeaderIndexMap_(headers),
    values: outputRows,
    range: null
  };

  populateDemoPUpdateColumns_(workingData, monthParts, rawSheet.getName(), "Created");
  markRuntimeStep_(timing, "Demo P Working Source - populate Demo P update tracking columns | Rows Processed: " + workingData.values.length + "; Write Mode: in-memory only");

  const demoSheet = createOutputSheetFromDashboardTemplate_(
    SHEET_TYPE.DEMO_P,
    targetName,
    workingData.values,
    monthParts.firstDay,
    monthParts.lastDay
  );
  markRuntimeStep_(timing, "Demo P Working Source - copy active Raw Data rows to Demo P template | Rows Read: " + rawData.values.length + "; Rows Written: " + workingData.values.length + "; Write Mode: single output write");

  try {
    demoSheet.getRange("A1").setValue(sheetDef.reportTitle || "Demo P");
  } catch (err) {
    Logger.log("Could not set Demo P title: " + err.message);
  }

  clearSheetRuntimeCachesForSheet_(demoSheet);

  processDemoPAsWorkingSource_(demoSheet, monthParts, timing);

  return {
    sheet: demoSheet,
    movedResult: movedResult,
    createdFromDashboardTemplate: true,
    sourceWasRawData: true,
    preProcessedWorkingSource: true
  };
}





function populateDemoPUpdateColumns_(data, monthParts, sourceSheetName, status) {
  if (!data || !data.headerMap || !data.values) return;
  const statusIdx = data.headerMap["Demo P Update Status"];
  const monthIdx = data.headerMap["Demo P Update Month"];
  const sourceIdx = data.headerMap["Demo P Source Sheet"];
  if (statusIdx === undefined && monthIdx === undefined && sourceIdx === undefined) return;


  const monthText = monthParts && monthParts.firstDay
    ? Utilities.formatDate(monthParts.firstDay, Session.getScriptTimeZone(), "MM.yy")
    : "";
  data.values.forEach(function(row) {
    if (statusIdx !== undefined) row[statusIdx] = status || "Created";
    if (monthIdx !== undefined) row[monthIdx] = monthText;
    if (sourceIdx !== undefined) row[sourceIdx] = sourceSheetName || "";
  });
}


function verifyPrimaryPMRColumnFromRawData_(data) {
  if (!data || !data.headerMap) return;
  const idx = data.headerMap["Primary PMR Row"];
  if (idx === undefined) {
    throw new Error("Demo P requires Primary PMR Row from Raw Data. Run Format Raw Data first.");
  }
  // Do not rescan or reassign PMR blocks here. Raw Data is the source of truth.
}




function splitRawDataRowsIntoActiveAndDisenrolled_(rawData, disenrolledPMRSet) {
  const headerMap = rawData.headerMap;
  const pmrIdx = getPMRIndex_(headerMap);
  const statusIdx = headerMap["Enrollment Status"];
  const disenrollmentDateIdx = findHeaderIndex_(headerMap, ["Disenrollment Effective Date", "Disenrollment Date", "Date of Death"]);
  const useExternalDisenrolledSet = !!(disenrolledPMRSet && disenrolledPMRSet.size);


  const activeRows = [];
  const disenrolledRows = [];
  const disenrolledRowsByPMR = new Map();
  const disenrolledPMRs = new Set();


  const values = rawData.values || [];
  let i = 0;


  while (i < values.length) {
    const firstRow = values[i];
    const pmr = normalizePMR_(firstRow[pmrIdx]);


    if (!pmr) {
      i++;
      continue;
    }


    const block = [];
    let blockIsDisenrolled = useExternalDisenrolledSet && disenrolledPMRSet.has(pmr);


    while (i < values.length && normalizePMR_(values[i][pmrIdx]) === pmr) {
      const row = values[i];
      block.push(row);


      if (!useExternalDisenrolledSet) {
        const status = statusIdx === undefined ? "" : String(row[statusIdx] || "").trim().toLowerCase();
        const disenrollmentValue = disenrollmentDateIdx === -1 ? "" : row[disenrollmentDateIdx];


        if (status === "disenrolled" || normalizeCompareValue_(disenrollmentValue) !== "") {
          blockIsDisenrolled = true;
        }
      }


      i++;
    }


    if (blockIsDisenrolled) {
      disenrolledPMRs.add(pmr);
      const primaryRow = block[0];
      disenrolledRows.push(primaryRow);
      disenrolledRowsByPMR.set(pmr, [primaryRow]);
    } else {
      for (let b = 0; b < block.length; b++) {
        activeRows.push(block[b]);
      }
    }
  }


  return {
    activeRows: activeRows,
    disenrolledRows: disenrolledRows,
    disenrolledRowsByPMR: disenrolledRowsByPMR,
    disenrolledPMRs: disenrolledPMRs
  };
}


function loadDisenrolledPMRSetForMonth_(monthParts) {
  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  const set = new Set();
  const candidates = [];


  if (monthParts && monthParts.firstDay) {
    candidates.push(buildDatedDisenrolledOutputName_(monthParts));
  }


  candidates.push(DISENROLLED_EXCLUSION_SHEET);


  for (let c = 0; c < candidates.length; c++) {
    const name = candidates[c];
    const sheet = ss.getSheetByName(name);
    if (!sheet) continue;


    const data = getDataValues_(sheet, HEADER_ROW, DATA_START_ROW);
    const pmrIdx = getPMRIndex_(data.headerMap);
    if (pmrIdx === -1) continue;


    (data.values || []).forEach(function(row) {
      const pmr = normalizePMR_(row[pmrIdx]);
      if (pmr) set.add(pmr);
    });


    if (set.size) return set;
  }


  return set;
}


function mapRowsToHeaders_(sourceRows, sourceHeaders, targetHeaders) {
  const sourceHeaderMap = buildHeaderIndexMap_(sourceHeaders || []);


  return (sourceRows || []).map(row => {
    return (targetHeaders || []).map(header => {
      const sourceIdx = sourceHeaderMap[header];
      return sourceIdx === undefined ? "" : row[sourceIdx];
    });
  });
}



function createOutputSheetFromDashboardTemplate_(sheetType, outputName, outputRows, firstDay, endDate) {
  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  const dashboard = loadDashboardConfig_();
  const normalizedSheetType = normalizeDashboardSheetTypeKey_(sheetType);
  const sheetDef = getSheetDefinitionByType_(dashboard, normalizedSheetType);
  const headers = getHeadersForSheetType_(dashboard, normalizedSheetType);
  const template = ss.getSheetByName(sheetDef.templateName);

  if (!template) {
    throw new Error("Template not found: " + sheetDef.templateName + ". Run Create / Refresh All Templates first.");
  }

  deleteSheetIfExists_(ss, outputName, sheetDef.templateName);
  const sheet = template.copyTo(ss);
  sheet.showSheet();
  setUniqueSheetName_(sheet, outputName);
  ss.setActiveSheet(sheet);

  const width = Math.max(headers.length, 1);
  const rows = outputRows || [];
  const requiredRows = rows.length ? DATA_START_ROW + rows.length - 1 : Math.max(sheet.getLastRow(), DATA_START_ROW);

  ensureOutputSheetHasFormattedRows_(sheet, requiredRows, width);

  try {
    sheet.getRange("A1").setValue(sheetDef.reportTitle || normalizedSheetType || outputName);
    if (firstDay) sheet.getRange("B2").setValue(firstDay);
    if (endDate) sheet.getRange("D2").setValue(endDate);
    if (headers.length) sheet.getRange(HEADER_ROW, 1, 1, width).setValues([headers]);
  } catch (err) {
    Logger.log("Dashboard-template output metadata skipped for " + outputName + ": " + err.message);
  }

  if (rows.length) {
    sheet.getRange(DATA_START_ROW, 1, rows.length, width).setValues(rows.map(function(row) {
      const out = (row || []).slice(0, width);
      while (out.length < width) out.push("");
      return out;
    }));
  }

  clearSheetRuntimeCachesForSheet_(sheet);
  return sheet;
}



function createRawDataOutputSheetFromTemplateFast_(sheetType, outputName, outputRows, firstDay, endDate, sourceName) {
  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  const dashboard = loadDashboardConfig_();
  const normalizedSheetType = normalizeDashboardSheetTypeKey_(sheetType);
  const sheetDef = getSheetDefinitionByType_(dashboard, normalizedSheetType);
  const headers = getHeadersForSheetType_(dashboard, normalizedSheetType);
  const template = ss.getSheetByName(sheetDef.templateName);

  if (!template) {
    throw new Error("Template not found: " + sheetDef.templateName + ". Run Create / Refresh All Templates first.");
  }

  deleteSheetIfExists_(ss, outputName, sourceName, sheetDef.templateName);
  const sheet = ss.insertSheet(outputName);
  sheet.showSheet();
  ss.setActiveSheet(sheet);

  const width = Math.max(headers.length, 1);
  const rows = outputRows || [];
  const requiredRows = rows.length ? DATA_START_ROW + rows.length - 1 : DATA_START_ROW;

  resizeSheetColumns_(sheet, width);
  if (sheet.getMaxRows() < requiredRows) {
    sheet.insertRowsAfter(sheet.getMaxRows(), requiredRows - sheet.getMaxRows());
  }

  const templateTopRows = Math.max(DATA_START_ROW - 1, HEADER_ROW);
  try {
    template.getRange(1, 1, templateTopRows, width)
      .copyTo(sheet.getRange(1, 1, templateTopRows, width), { contentsOnly: false });
  } catch (err) {
    Logger.log("Raw Data template title/header copy skipped for " + outputName + ": " + err.message);
  }

  const dataRows = Math.max(requiredRows - DATA_START_ROW + 1, 1);
  try {
    template.getRange(DATA_START_ROW, 1, 1, width)
      .copyTo(sheet.getRange(DATA_START_ROW, 1, dataRows, width), { formatOnly: true });
  } catch (err) {
    Logger.log("Raw Data template data-row formatting copy skipped for " + outputName + ": " + err.message);
  }

  try {
    for (let col = 1; col <= width; col++) {
      sheet.setColumnWidth(col, template.getColumnWidth(col));
    }
    sheet.setFrozenRows(template.getFrozenRows());
    sheet.setFrozenColumns(template.getFrozenColumns());
    if (template.getTabColor()) sheet.setTabColor(template.getTabColor());
  } catch (err) {
    Logger.log("Raw Data template sheet settings copy skipped for " + outputName + ": " + err.message);
  }

  try {
    sheet.getRange("A1").setValue(sheetDef.reportTitle || normalizedSheetType || outputName);
    if (firstDay) sheet.getRange("B2").setValue(firstDay);
    if (endDate) sheet.getRange("D2").setValue(endDate);
    if (headers.length) sheet.getRange(HEADER_ROW, 1, 1, width).setValues([headers]);
  } catch (err) {
    Logger.log("Raw Data output metadata skipped for " + outputName + ": " + err.message);
  }

  if (rows.length) {
    sheet.getRange(DATA_START_ROW, 1, rows.length, width).setValues(rows.map(function(row) {
      const out = (row || []).slice(0, width);
      while (out.length < width) out.push("");
      return out;
    }));
  }

  try {
    const existingFilter = sheet.getFilter && sheet.getFilter();
    if (existingFilter) existingFilter.remove();
    sheet.getRange(HEADER_ROW, 1, Math.max(sheet.getMaxRows() - HEADER_ROW + 1, 1), width).createFilter();
  } catch (err) {
    Logger.log("Raw Data output filter creation skipped for " + outputName + ": " + err.message);
  }

  clearSheetRuntimeCachesForSheet_(sheet);
  return sheet;
}


function ensureOutputSheetHasFormattedRows_(sheet, requiredRows, width) {
  if (!sheet) return;

  requiredRows = Math.max(Number(requiredRows || 1), DATA_START_ROW);
  width = Math.max(Number(width || 1), 1);

  const currentRows = sheet.getMaxRows();
  if (currentRows < requiredRows) {
    sheet.insertRowsAfter(currentRows, requiredRows - currentRows);
  }

  if (!RFF_OUTPUT_EXTEND_TEMPLATE_FORMATTING) return;

  const dataRows = Math.max(requiredRows - DATA_START_ROW + 1, 1);
  try {
    sheet.getRange(DATA_START_ROW, 1, 1, width)
      .copyTo(sheet.getRange(DATA_START_ROW, 1, dataRows, width), { formatOnly: true });
  } catch (err) {
    Logger.log("Output template formatting extension skipped for " + sheet.getName() + ": " + err.message);
  }
}


function appendDisenrolledRowsFromRawDataToExclusion_(rawSheet, rawHeaders, rowsByPMR, monthParts) {
  if (!rowsByPMR || rowsByPMR.size === 0) return 0;
  return appendDisenrolledPMRBlocksToExclusion_(rawSheet, rawHeaders, rowsByPMR, monthParts);
}




function moveDisenrolledPMRsFromDemoPToExclusion_(demoSheet, monthParts) {
  const result = {
    pmrsRemoved: 0,
    rowsRemoved: 0,
    rowsCopied: 0
  };


  if (!demoSheet) return result;


  const lastRow = demoSheet.getLastRow();
  const lastCol = demoSheet.getLastColumn();


  if (lastRow < DATA_START_ROW || lastCol < 1) return result;


  const headers = getHeaders_(demoSheet, HEADER_ROW);
  const headerMap = buildHeaderIndexMap_(headers);
  const pmrIdx = getPMRIndex_(headerMap);
  const statusIdx = headerMap["Enrollment Status"];


  if (pmrIdx === -1 || statusIdx === undefined) {
    Logger.log("Demo P disenrolled split skipped: missing PMR or Enrollment Status header.");
    return result;
  }


  const dataRange = demoSheet.getRange(DATA_START_ROW, 1, lastRow - DATA_START_ROW + 1, lastCol);
  const values = dataRange.getValues();
  const disenrolledPMRs = new Set();


  values.forEach(row => {
    const pmr = normalizePMR_(row[pmrIdx]);
    if (!pmr) return;


    const status = String(row[statusIdx] || "").trim().toLowerCase();
    if (status === "disenrolled") disenrolledPMRs.add(pmr);
  });


  if (disenrolledPMRs.size === 0) return result;


  const rowsToRemove = [];
  const rowsByPMR = new Map();


  values.forEach((row, idx) => {
    const pmr = normalizePMR_(row[pmrIdx]);
    if (!pmr || !disenrolledPMRs.has(pmr)) return;


    rowsToRemove.push(DATA_START_ROW + idx);
    if (!rowsByPMR.has(pmr)) rowsByPMR.set(pmr, []);
    rowsByPMR.get(pmr).push(row);
  });


  result.pmrsRemoved = disenrolledPMRs.size;
  result.rowsRemoved = rowsToRemove.length;
  result.rowsCopied = appendDisenrolledPMRBlocksToExclusion_(demoSheet, headers, rowsByPMR, monthParts);


  deleteRowNumberBatches_(demoSheet, rowsToRemove);
  clearSheetRuntimeCachesForSheet_(demoSheet);


  return result;
}


function appendDisenrolledPMRBlocksToExclusion_(sourceSheet, sourceHeaders, rowsByPMR, monthParts) {
  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  const dashboard = loadDashboardConfig_();
  const sheetDef = getSheetDefinitionByType_(dashboard, SHEET_TYPE.DISENROLLED_EXCLUSION);
  const template = ss.getSheetByName(sheetDef.templateName);
  if (!template) {
    throw new Error("Template not found: " + sheetDef.templateName + ". Run Create / Refresh Disenrolled Exclusion List Template first.");
  }

  const exclusionHeaders = getHeadersForSheetType_(dashboard, SHEET_TYPE.DISENROLLED_EXCLUSION);
  const sourceHeaderMap = buildHeaderIndexMap_(sourceHeaders || []);
  const sourcePMRIdx = getPMRIndex_(sourceHeaderMap);
  const exclusionHeaderMap = buildHeaderIndexMap_(exclusionHeaders);
  const exclusionPMRIdx = getPMRIndex_(exclusionHeaderMap);

  const sourceIndexes = exclusionHeaders.map(function(header) {
    return Object.prototype.hasOwnProperty.call(sourceHeaderMap, header) ? sourceHeaderMap[header] : -1;
  });

  const rowsToWrite = [];
  if (rowsByPMR && rowsByPMR.size) {
    rowsByPMR.forEach(function(rows) {
      const sourceRow = rows && rows.length ? rows[0] : null;
      if (!sourceRow) return;

      const output = sourceIndexes.map(function(sourceIdx) {
        return sourceIdx === -1 ? "" : sourceRow[sourceIdx];
      });

      if (exclusionPMRIdx >= 0 && sourcePMRIdx >= 0 && !normalizePMR_(output[exclusionPMRIdx])) {
        output[exclusionPMRIdx] = sourceRow[sourcePMRIdx];
      }
      rowsToWrite.push(output);
    });
  }

  const outputSheetName = buildDatedDisenrolledOutputName_(monthParts);
  const legacy = ss.getSheetByName(DISENROLLED_EXCLUSION_SHEET);
  if (legacy && ss.getSheets().length > 1) ss.deleteSheet(legacy);
  const existing = ss.getSheetByName(outputSheetName);
  if (existing && ss.getSheets().length > 1) ss.deleteSheet(existing);

  const sheet = template.copyTo(ss);
  sheet.showSheet();
  setUniqueSheetName_(sheet, outputSheetName);

  const width = Math.max(exclusionHeaders.length, 1);
  const startDate = monthParts && monthParts.firstDay ? monthParts.firstDay : getTodayLocalDate_();
  const endDate = monthParts && monthParts.lastDay ? monthParts.lastDay : startDate;

  // v1.5: The copied dashboard template already owns headers, row count, column count, and formatting.
  // Do not force row count or clear blank data rows before the first output write.
  sheet.getRange("A1").setValue(DISENROLLED_EXCLUSION_SHEET);
  sheet.getRange("A2:D2").setValues([["Date:", startDate, "to", endDate]]);
  sheet.getRange(HEADER_ROW, 1, 1, width).setValues([exclusionHeaders]);

  if (rowsToWrite.length) {
    sheet.getRange(DATA_START_ROW, 1, rowsToWrite.length, width).setValues(rowsToWrite);
  }

  applyFinalRowHeightLock_(sheet, 25);

  try {
    sheet.getRange("A1").setNote(
      "Rows Processed: " + (rowsByPMR ? rowsByPMR.size : 0) + "\\n" +
      "Rows Written: " + rowsToWrite.length + "\\n" +
      "v1.5 Disenrolled single-write output"
    );
  } catch (err) {
    Logger.log("Disenrolled output note skipped: " + err.message);
  }

  clearSheetRuntimeCachesForSheet_(sheet);
  return rowsToWrite.length;
}



function createDisenrolledExclusionSheetFromDashboardTemplate_(ss, monthParts) {
  ss = ss || SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();


  const dashboard = loadDashboardConfig_();
  const sheetDef = getSheetDefinitionByType_(dashboard, SHEET_TYPE.DISENROLLED_EXCLUSION);
  const template = ss.getSheetByName(sheetDef.templateName);


  if (!template) {
    throw new Error("Template not found: " + sheetDef.templateName + ". Run Create / Refresh All Templates first.");
  }


  const existing = ss.getSheetByName(DISENROLLED_EXCLUSION_SHEET);
  if (existing) ss.deleteSheet(existing);


  const sheet = template.copyTo(ss);
  sheet.showSheet();
  setUniqueSheetName_(sheet, DISENROLLED_EXCLUSION_SHEET);


  const startDate = monthParts && monthParts.firstDay ? monthParts.firstDay : getTodayLocalDate_();
  const endDate = monthParts && monthParts.lastDay ? monthParts.lastDay : startDate;


  sheet.getRange("A1").setValue(DISENROLLED_EXCLUSION_SHEET);
  sheet.getRange("A2").setValue("Date");
  sheet.getRange("B2").setValue(startDate);
  sheet.getRange("C2").setValue("to");
  sheet.getRange("D2").setValue(endDate);


  clearSheetRuntimeCachesForSheet_(sheet);
  return sheet;
}

  /*
   * v1.4.25:

   * Demo P, must build through the shared dashboard template pipeline.
   */
  const dashboard = loadDashboardConfig_();
  const sheetDef = getSheetDefinitionByType_(dashboard, SHEET_TYPE.DEMO_P);
  return createOrRefreshTemplateFromDashboard_(dashboard, sheetDef, null);
}

  ss = ss || SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  let template = ss.getSheetByName(DEMO_P_TEMPLATE_SHEET);
  if (!template) template = createOrRefreshDemoPTemplate_(ss);
  return template;
}


function initializeDemoPTemplateTitleRows_(sheet, monthParts) {
  if (!sheet) return;


  if (sheet.getMaxColumns() < 4) {
    sheet.insertColumnsAfter(sheet.getMaxColumns(), 4 - sheet.getMaxColumns());
  }


  sheet.getRange("A1").setValue("Demographics - Participants");
  sheet.getRange("A2").setValue("Date");
  sheet.getRange("B2").setValue(monthParts.firstDay);
  sheet.getRange("C2").setValue("to");
  sheet.getRange("D2").setValue(monthParts.lastDay);
}


function applyDemoPTemplateFormatting_(sheet, monthParts) {
  if (!sheet) return;


  monthParts = monthParts || getMonthPartsFromTitleRows_(sheet) || getMonthDateParts_(new Date());


  applyStandardFormatting_(sheet, {
    sheetType: SHEET_TYPE.DEMO_P,
    title: "Demographics - Participants",
    startDate: monthParts.firstDay,
    endDate: monthParts.lastDay,
    titleInfoText: "",
    renameSheet: false,
    skipAlternatingColors: true,
    promptDate: monthParts.firstDay
  });


  applyDemoPDateFormattingByHeader_(sheet);
  applyStandardRowHeights_(sheet);
}


function applyDemoPTemplateToSheet_(targetSheet, monthParts) {
  if (!targetSheet) return;


  const dashboard = loadDashboardConfig_();
  const sheetDef = getSheetDefinitionByType_(dashboard, SHEET_TYPE.DEMO_P);
  const headers = getHeadersForSheetType_(dashboard, SHEET_TYPE.DEMO_P);
  const behavior = dashboard.behaviors[sheetDef.sheetType] || getDefaultBehavior_();


  enforceDemoPStrictDashboardSchema_(targetSheet);


  applyDashboardTemplateFormattingToActiveReportSheet_(
    targetSheet,
    dashboard,
    sheetDef,
    headers,
    behavior,
    monthParts || {
      firstDay: new Date(),
      lastDay: new Date()
    },
    monthParts ? monthParts.lastDay : new Date(),
    "",
    null
  );


  try {
    targetSheet.getRange("A1").setValue(sheetDef.reportTitle || "Demo P");
  } catch (err) {
    Logger.log("Could not refresh Demo P title after dashboard template apply: " + err.message);
  }


  applyDemoPDateFormattingByHeader_(targetSheet);
  clearSheetRuntimeCachesForSheet_(targetSheet);
}


function applyDemoPDateFormattingByHeader_(sheet) {
  if (!sheet) return;


  const lastRow = Math.max(sheet.getLastRow(), DATA_START_ROW);
  const headers = getHeaders_(sheet, HEADER_ROW);


  DEMO_P_TEMPLATE_DATE_HEADERS.forEach(headerName => {
    const idx = headers.indexOf(headerName);
    if (idx === -1) return;


    try {
      sheet.getRange(DATA_START_ROW, idx + 1, Math.max(lastRow - DATA_START_ROW + 1, 1), 1);
    } catch (err) {
      Logger.log("Could not apply Demo P date format for " + headerName + ": " + err.message);
    }
  });


  try {
    sheet.getRange("B2");
    sheet.getRange("D2");
  } catch (err) {
    Logger.log("Could not apply Demo P title date format: " + err.message);
  }
}


function syncDemoPBannerColumns_(demoSheet, monthParts) {
  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  const bannerSheet = getCurrentBannersSheet_(monthParts);


  if (!bannerSheet) {
    notify_("Banners sheet was not found. Demo P Banner sync skipped.");
    return;
  }


  const demoLastRow = demoSheet.getLastRow();
  const demoLastCol = demoSheet.getLastColumn();


  if (demoLastRow < DATA_START_ROW || demoLastCol < 1) return;


  const demoHeaders = getHeaders_(demoSheet, HEADER_ROW);
  const demoHeaderMap = buildHeaderIndexMap_(demoHeaders);


  const demoPMRIdx = getPMRIndex_(demoHeaderMap);
  const demoLastNameIdx = demoHeaderMap["Last Name"];
  const demoFirstNameIdx = demoHeaderMap["First Name"];


  if (demoPMRIdx === -1 || demoLastNameIdx === undefined || demoFirstNameIdx === undefined) {
    notify_("Demo P Banner sync skipped: missing Participant PMR#, Last Name, or First Name.");
    return;
  }


  const bannerMap = buildSourceMapByCompositeKeyForDemoPBanner_(
    bannerSheet,
    HEADER_ROW,
    DATA_START_ROW,
    ["Participant PMR#", "Last Name", "First Name"]
  );


  if (bannerMap.size === 0) {
    notify_("Demo P Banner sync skipped: no matching Banner records were found.");
    return;
  }


  const range = demoSheet.getRange(DATA_START_ROW, 1, demoLastRow - DATA_START_ROW + 1, demoLastCol);
  const values = range.getValues();


  values.forEach(row => {
    const demoDOBIdx = getDOBIndex_(demoHeaderMap);
    if (demoDOBIdx !== -1 && normalizeCompareValue_(row[demoDOBIdx]) === "") return;


    const key = [
      normalizeKeyPart_(row[demoPMRIdx]),
      normalizeKeyPart_(row[demoLastNameIdx]),
      normalizeKeyPart_(row[demoFirstNameIdx])
    ].join("|||");


    if (!bannerMap.has(key)) return;


    const source = bannerMap.get(key);


    DEMO_P_BANNER_SYNC_HEADERS.forEach(header => {
      const targetIdx = demoHeaderMap[header];
      if (targetIdx === undefined) return;
      if (!Object.prototype.hasOwnProperty.call(source, header)) return;
      row[targetIdx] = source[header];
    });
  });


  range.setValues(values);
}


function buildSourceMapByCompositeKeyForDemoPBanner_(sheet, headerRow, dataStartRow, keyHeaders) {
  const lastRow = sheet.getLastRow();
  const lastCol = sheet.getLastColumn();
  const map = new Map();


  if (lastRow < dataStartRow || lastCol < 1) return map;


  const headers = getHeaders_(sheet, headerRow);
  const headerMap = buildHeaderIndexMap_(headers);


  if (keyHeaders.some(header => headerMap[header] === undefined)) return map;


  const data = sheet.getRange(dataStartRow, 1, lastRow - dataStartRow + 1, lastCol).getValues();


  data.forEach(row => {
    const key = keyHeaders
      .map(header => normalizeKeyPart_(row[headerMap[header]]))
      .join("|||");


    if (key.replace(/\|/g, "") === "") return;


    const record = {};
    headers.forEach((header, idx) => {
      if (header) record[header] = row[idx];
    });


    map.set(key, record);
  });


  return map;
}

    RFF_SHEET_TYPES.UNLOCKED,
    "Format Unlocked Care Plan Report",
    "G3"
  );

function formatCarePlanDueOrUnlockedFromDashboard_(sheetType, promptTitle, endDateCellA1) {
  return runFrameworkTimed_(promptTitle, function(timing) {
    const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
    const sourceSheetOriginal = ss.getActiveSheet();


    if (!sourceSheetOriginal) {
      throw new Error("No active sheet found. Select the raw " + sheetType + " import sheet before running " + promptTitle + ".");
    }


    const monthParts = promptForLockedYearReportMonth_(promptTitle);
    if (!monthParts) return null;


    const dashboard = loadDashboardConfig_();
    const sheetDef = getSheetDefinitionByType_(dashboard, sheetType);
    const headers = getHeadersForSheetType_(dashboard, sheetType);
    const outputName = buildDashboardOutputSheetName_(sheetDef, monthParts);
    const rawName = buildRawArchiveNameForSheetType_(sheetType, monthParts);


    const activeName = String(sourceSheetOriginal.getName() || "").trim();
    if (activeName === sheetDef.templateName || activeName === outputName) {
      throw new Error("The active sheet is not a raw " + sheetType + " import sheet. Select the imported source sheet.");
    }


    const originalEndDate =
      coerceToValidDate_(sourceSheetOriginal.getRange(endDateCellA1).getValue()) ||
      coerceToValidDate_(sourceSheetOriginal.getRange(endDateCellA1).getDisplayValue()) ||
      monthParts.lastDay;


    const titleInfoText = collectAndClearMovedTitleInfoCells_(sourceSheetOriginal, sheetType);
    markFrameworkStep_(timing, "Move source title/date cells into dashboard title info");


    /*
     * v1.5.47:
     * Read the active raw import without a local rename, create the governed
     * formatted output, then archive/delete the raw source only after output
     * creation succeeds. Formatting is owned by the verified hidden template.
     */
    prepareCarePlanSourceSheetForDashboardFormat_(sourceSheetOriginal, sheetType, headers);
    markFrameworkStep_(timing, "Prepare raw source structure");


    const rawSheet = sourceSheetOriginal;
    markFrameworkStep_(timing, "Raw source preserved for read without local rename: " + rawSheet.getName());


    const rawData = getDataValues_(rawSheet, HEADER_ROW, DATA_START_ROW);
    const outputRows = mapRowsToHeaders_(rawData.values, rawData.headers, headers);
    markFrameworkStep_(timing, "Raw data mapped to dashboard headers");


    deleteSheetIfExists_(ss, outputName, rawSheet.getName(), sheetDef.templateName);
    const outputSheet = createOutputSheetFromDashboardTemplate_(
      sheetType,
      outputName,
      outputRows,
      monthParts.firstDay,
      originalEndDate || monthParts.lastDay
    );
    markFrameworkStep_(timing, "Template duplicated and raw data pasted: " + outputSheet.getName());


    try {
      outputSheet.getRange("A1").setValue(sheetDef.reportTitle || sheetType);
      if (titleInfoText) outputSheet.getRange("A3").setValue(titleInfoText);
    } catch (err) {
      Logger.log("Could not write " + sheetType + " title info: " + err.message);
    }


    lockFinalOutputRowHeights_(outputSheet, sheetType);
    markFrameworkStep_(timing, "Lock final row heights");


    archiveRawSourceAndDeleteLocal_(ss, rawSheet, rawName, outputSheet, timing);


    clearSheetRuntimeCachesForSheet_(outputSheet);
    markFrameworkStep_(timing, "Clear runtime caches");


    notify_(sheetDef.reportTitle + " formatted using template-copy pattern.\nSheet created: " + outputSheet.getName());
    return outputSheet;
  });
}


function buildRawArchiveNameForSheetType_(sheetType, monthParts) {
  const suffix = Utilities.formatDate(monthParts.firstDay, Session.getScriptTimeZone(), "MM.yy");


  if (sheetType === SHEET_TYPE.CARE_PLAN_DUE || sheetType === RFF_SHEET_TYPES.CARE_PLAN_DUE) {
    return "Raw Data - CP Due " + suffix;
  }


  if (sheetType === SHEET_TYPE.UNLOCKED || sheetType === RFF_SHEET_TYPES.UNLOCKED) {
    return "Raw Data - Unlocked CP " + suffix;
  }


  if (sheetType === SHEET_TYPE.DEMO_P || sheetType === RFF_SHEET_TYPES.DEMO_P) {
    return "Raw Data " + suffix;
  }


  if (sheetType === SHEET_TYPE.DISENROLLED_EXCLUSION || sheetType === RFF_SHEET_TYPES.DISENROLLED) {
    return "Raw Data - Disenrolled " + suffix;
  }


  return "Raw Data - " + String(sheetType || "Report") + " " + suffix;
}




function collectAndClearMovedTitleInfoCells_(sheet, sheetType) {
  const cells = TITLE_INFO_MOVE_CELLS[sheetType] || [];
  const parts = [];


  cells.forEach(function(a1) {
    try {
      const value = String(sheet.getRange(a1).getDisplayValue() || "").trim();
      if (value) parts.push(value);
    } catch (err) {
      Logger.log("Could not read moved source cell " + a1 + ": " + err.message);
    }
  });


  cells.forEach(function(a1) {
    try {
      sheet.getRange(a1).clearContent();
    } catch (err) {
      Logger.log("Could not clear moved source cell " + a1 + ": " + err.message);
    }
  });


  return parts.join(" ");
}


function prepareCarePlanSourceSheetForDashboardFormat_(sheet, sheetType, headers) {
  /*
   * v1.4.25:
   * Source sheet structural cleanup is restricted. This function may no longer
   * unmerge, show columns, delete cells, or delete empty columns. Care Plan
   * source/template column structure must come from Dashboard Section C.
   */
  if (!sheet) return;
  clearSheetRuntimeCachesForSheet_(sheet);
}


function prepareRawDataSourceSheetForDashboardFormat_(sheet, headers) {
  /*
   * v1.4.24:
   * Raw Data column additions/removals are dashboard-governed. Do not append
   * approved columns here; the Format Dashboard Sheet Headers must define them.
   */
  if (!sheet) return headers || [];


  const effectiveHeaders = getHeaders_(sheet, HEADER_ROW)
    .map(function(header) { return String(header || "").trim(); })
    .filter(function(header) { return header !== ""; });


  return effectiveHeaders.length ? effectiveHeaders : (headers || []);
}






function buildRawDataHeadersForFormatting_(sheet, fallbackHeaders) {
  /*
   * v1.4.24:
   * Return current/template headers only. Do not append columns outside the
   * dashboard Sheet Headers table.
   */
  const currentHeaders = getHeaders_(sheet, HEADER_ROW)
    .map(function(header) { return String(header || "").trim(); })
    .filter(function(header) { return header !== ""; });


  return currentHeaders.length ? currentHeaders.slice() : (fallbackHeaders || []).slice();
}


function getRawDataApprovedAddedColumns_() {
  return [
    "Primary PMR Row"
  ];
}


function processRawDataApprovedSyncColumns_(sheet, monthParts) {
  if (!sheet) return;


  const data = getDataValues_(sheet, HEADER_ROW, DATA_START_ROW);
  if (!data.values.length) return;


  const headerMap = data.headerMap || {};
  const beforeValues = {};
  getRawDataApprovedAddedColumns_().forEach(function(header) {
    const idx = headerMap[header];
    if (idx === undefined) return;
    beforeValues[idx] = data.values.map(function(row) { return row[idx]; });
  });


  markPrimaryPMRRowsForSequentialData_(data);


  /*
   * v1.5.47 correction:
   * Format Raw Data only owns Primary PMR Row. Banner safety fields are no
   * longer populated from this formatter, so do not look up or notify on a
   * Banners sheet during Raw Data formatting.
   */
  writeChangedColumnsOnly_(sheet, data, beforeValues);
  clearSheetRuntimeCachesForSheet_(sheet);
}


function writeChangedColumnsOnly_(sheet, data, beforeValues) {
  if (!sheet || !data || !data.values || !data.values.length) return 0;


  const indexes = Object.keys(beforeValues || {})
    .map(function(key) { return Number(key); })
    .filter(function(idx) {
      return idx >= 0 && data.values.some(function(row, r) {
        return !valuesAreEqual_(row[idx], beforeValues[idx][r]);
      });
    })
    .sort(function(a, b) { return a - b; });


  if (!indexes.length) return 0;


  const groups = [];
  let current = [indexes[0]];


  for (let i = 1; i < indexes.length; i++) {
    if (indexes[i] === current[current.length - 1] + 1) {
      current.push(indexes[i]);
    } else {
      groups.push(current);
      current = [indexes[i]];
    }
  }
  groups.push(current);


  groups.forEach(function(group) {
    const startIdx = group[0];
    const width = group.length;
    const values = data.values.map(function(row) {
      return row.slice(startIdx, startIdx + width);
    });


    sheet.getRange(DATA_START_ROW, startIdx + 1, values.length, width).setValues(values);
  });


  return indexes.length;
}

function applyDashboardTemplateFormattingToActiveReportSheet_(sheet, dashboard, sheetDef, headers, behavior, monthParts, endDate, titleInfoText, timing) {
  /*
   * v1.4.25:
   * Runtime report formatting is restricted. Verified dashboard-built templates
   * are the formatting authority. Normal sheet processes may write data,
   * metadata/date cells, and final row heights only; they may not reapply
   * dashboard formatting, hidden columns, filters, freezes, widths, or
   * date/number formatting outside the template builder.
   */
  if (!sheet || !sheetDef) return sheet;


  try {
    const globals = dashboard && dashboard.globals ? dashboard.globals : RFF_DEFAULTS;
    if (sheetDef.reportTitle) sheet.getRange("A1").setValue(sheetDef.reportTitle);
    if (monthParts && monthParts.firstDay) {
      sheet.getRange("B2").setValue(monthParts.firstDay);
    }
    if (endDate || (monthParts && monthParts.lastDay)) {
      sheet.getRange("D2").setValue(endDate || monthParts.lastDay);
    }
    if (titleInfoText !== undefined && titleInfoText !== null) {
      sheet.getRange("C1").setValue(titleInfoText);
    }
  } catch (err) {
    Logger.log("Dashboard-template runtime metadata update skipped for " + sheet.getName() + ": " + err.message);
  }


  applyFinalRowHeightLockForSheetType_(sheet, sheetDef.sheetType);
  clearSheetRuntimeCachesForSheet_(sheet);
  return sheet;
}


function resizeSheetMinimum_(sheet, rowCount, colCount) {
  const currentRows = sheet.getMaxRows();
  const currentCols = sheet.getMaxColumns();


  if (currentRows < rowCount) {
    sheet.insertRowsAfter(currentRows, rowCount - currentRows);
  }


  if (currentCols < colCount) {
    sheet.insertColumnsAfter(currentCols, colCount - currentCols);
  }
}


function buildDashboardOutputSheetName_(sheetDef, monthParts) {
  const pattern = String(sheetDef.outputNamingPattern || sheetDef.reportTitle || sheetDef.sheetType || "").trim();
  const monthText = Utilities.formatDate(monthParts.firstDay, Session.getScriptTimeZone(), "MM.yy");
  const monthTextNoLeading = Utilities.formatDate(monthParts.firstDay, Session.getScriptTimeZone(), "M.yy");
  const fullStart = formatDateForSheetName_(monthParts.firstDay);
  const fullEnd = formatDateForSheetName_(monthParts.lastDay);


  let name = pattern || String(sheetDef.reportTitle || sheetDef.sheetType || "Report").trim();


  name = name
    .replace(/mm\.yy/g, monthText)
    .replace(/MM\.yy/g, monthText)
    .replace(/m\.yy/g, monthTextNoLeading)
    .replace(/M\.yy/g, monthTextNoLeading)
    .replace(/start/gi, fullStart)
    .replace(/end/gi, fullEnd);


  if (name === pattern && name.toLowerCase().indexOf(monthText.toLowerCase()) === -1 && sheetDef.usePromptDate) {
    name = name + " " + monthText;
  }


  return safeSheetName_(name);
}




function getReportMonthFromSheetOrPrompt_(sheet, promptTitle, possibleDateCells) {
  const foundDate = getFirstValidDateFromCells_(sheet, possibleDateCells || []);
  if (foundDate) return getMonthDateParts_(foundDate);


  return promptForLockedYearReportMonth_(promptTitle);
}


function getReportMonthFromB3D3NoPrompt_(sheet, reportName) {
  const startDate = coerceToValidDate_(sheet.getRange("B3").getValue()) ||
    coerceToValidDate_(sheet.getRange("B3").getDisplayValue());


  const endDate = coerceToValidDate_(sheet.getRange("D3").getValue()) ||
    coerceToValidDate_(sheet.getRange("D3").getDisplayValue());


  if (!startDate) {
    notify_(`${reportName}: B3 does not contain a valid report start date. The sheet was formatted but not renamed.`);
    return null;
  }


  const firstDay = new Date(startDate.getFullYear(), startDate.getMonth(), startDate.getDate());
  const lastDay = endDate || new Date(firstDay.getFullYear(), firstDay.getMonth() + 1, 0);


  return {
    inputDate: firstDay,
    firstDay: firstDay,
    lastDay: lastDay,
    previousMonthFirstDay: new Date(firstDay.getFullYear(), firstDay.getMonth() - 1, 1),
    previousMonthLastDay: new Date(firstDay.getFullYear(), firstDay.getMonth(), 0),
    firstDayName: formatDateForSheetName_(firstDay),
    lastDayName: formatDateForSheetName_(lastDay),
    previousFirstDayName: formatDateForSheetName_(new Date(firstDay.getFullYear(), firstDay.getMonth() - 1, 1)),
    previousLastDayName: formatDateForSheetName_(new Date(firstDay.getFullYear(), firstDay.getMonth(), 0)),
    monthKey: Utilities.formatDate(firstDay, Session.getScriptTimeZone(), "yyyy-MM")
  };
}


function getFirstValidDateFromCells_(sheet, cellList) {
  for (let i = 0; i < cellList.length; i++) {
    try {
      const range = sheet.getRange(cellList[i]);
      const value = range.getValue();
      const display = range.getDisplayValue();


      const parsedValue = coerceToValidDate_(value);
      if (parsedValue) return parsedValue;


      const parsedDisplay = coerceToValidDate_(display);
      if (parsedDisplay) return parsedDisplay;
    } catch (err) {
      Logger.log("Date read skipped for " + cellList[i] + ": " + err.message);
    }
  }


  return null;
}


function buildDisenrolledPMRSetFromDemoPValues_(demoValues, demoHeaderMap) {
  const result = new Set();


  const pmrIdx = getPMRIndex_(demoHeaderMap);
  const disenrollEffectiveIdx = findHeaderIndex_(demoHeaderMap, ["Disenrollment Effective Date", "Disenrollment Date"]);


  if (pmrIdx === -1 || disenrollEffectiveIdx === -1) {
    return result;
  }


  demoValues.forEach(row => {
    const pmr = normalizePMR_(row[pmrIdx]);
    if (!pmr) return;


    const disenrollDate = row[disenrollEffectiveIdx];


    if (normalizeCompareValue_(disenrollDate) !== "") {
      result.add(pmr);
    }
  });


  return result;
}


function removeDisenrolledPMRBlocksFromMasterUsingDemoP_(masterSheet, demoSheet) {
  if (!masterSheet || !demoSheet) return 0;


  const demoHeaders = getHeaders_(demoSheet, HEADER_ROW);
  const demoHeaderMap = buildHeaderIndexMap_(demoHeaders);
  const demoLastRow = demoSheet.getLastRow();
  const demoLastCol = demoSheet.getLastColumn();


  if (demoLastRow < DATA_START_ROW || demoLastCol < 1) return 0;


  const demoValues = demoSheet.getRange(DATA_START_ROW, 1, demoLastRow - DATA_START_ROW + 1, demoLastCol).getValues();
  const disenrolledPMRs = buildDisenrolledPMRSetFromDemoPValues_(demoValues, demoHeaderMap);


  const exclusionPMRs = loadDisenrolledExclusionPMRsForPart3_();
  exclusionPMRs.forEach(pmr => disenrolledPMRs.add(pmr));


  if (disenrolledPMRs.size === 0) return 0;


  const masterHeaders = getHeaders_(masterSheet, HEADER_ROW);
  const masterHeaderMap = buildHeaderIndexMap_(masterHeaders);
  const masterPMRIdx = getPMRIndex_(masterHeaderMap);


  if (masterPMRIdx === -1) return 0;


  const masterLastRow = masterSheet.getLastRow();
  const masterLastCol = masterSheet.getLastColumn();


  if (masterLastRow < DATA_START_ROW || masterLastCol < 1) return 0;


  const range = masterSheet.getRange(DATA_START_ROW, 1, masterLastRow - DATA_START_ROW + 1, masterLastCol);
  const values = range.getValues();


  const keepRows = [];
  let removed = 0;


  values.forEach(row => {
    const pmr = normalizePMR_(row[masterPMRIdx]);
    if (pmr && disenrolledPMRs.has(pmr)) {
      removed++;
      return;
    }
    keepRows.push(row);
  });


  if (removed === 0) return 0;


  range.clearContent();


  if (keepRows.length > 0) {
    masterSheet.getRange(DATA_START_ROW, 1, keepRows.length, masterLastCol).setValues(keepRows);
  }


  return removed;
}

function formatDateColumnsForHeaderRowOne_(sheet) {
  const lastRow = sheet.getLastRow();
  const lastCol = sheet.getLastColumn();
  if (lastRow < 2 || lastCol < 1) return;


  const headers = sheet.getRange(1, 1, 1, lastCol)
    .getValues()[0]
    .map(h => String(h || "").trim());


  GLOBAL_DATE_FORMAT_HEADERS.forEach(headerName => {
    const colIdx = headers.indexOf(headerName);
    if (colIdx === -1) return;


    normalizeAndFormatDateRange_(sheet.getRange(2, colIdx + 1, lastRow - 1, 1));
  });
}


function buildMasterListHeadersBeforeDataCopy_(demoSheet, masterSheet) {
  /*
   * v1.4.24:
   * The Master List template/dashboard Sheet Headers are the only header
   * authority. Do not add Master List columns during monthly processing.
   */
  const existingHeaders = getHeaders_(masterSheet, HEADER_ROW)
    .map(function(header) { return String(header || "").trim(); })
    .filter(function(header) { return header !== ""; });


  return existingHeaders;
}




function copyDemoPDataToMasterListByHeader_(demoSheet, masterSheet, monthParts) {
  const demoData = getDataValues_(demoSheet, HEADER_ROW, DATA_START_ROW);


  if (!demoData.values.length) return 0;


  const demoHeaders = demoData.headers;
  const demoHeaderMap = demoData.headerMap;
  const masterHeaders = getHeaders_(masterSheet, HEADER_ROW);
  const masterHeaderMap = getHeaderMap_(masterSheet, HEADER_ROW);


  const pmrIdx = getPMRIndex_(demoHeaderMap);
  if (pmrIdx === -1) {
    throw new Error("Demo P is missing Participant PMR# / PMR # column.");
  }


  const demoValues = demoData.values;


  const disenrolledPMRs = buildDisenrolledPMRSetFromDemoPValues_(demoValues, demoHeaderMap);


  const exclusionPMRs = loadDisenrolledExclusionPMRsForPart3_();
  exclusionPMRs.forEach(pmr => disenrolledPMRs.add(pmr));


  const output = [];


  demoValues.forEach(row => {
    const pmr = normalizePMR_(row[pmrIdx]);
    if (!pmr) return;


    if (disenrolledPMRs.has(pmr)) return;


    const out = new Array(masterHeaders.length).fill("");


    demoHeaders.forEach((header, sourceIdx) => {
      if (!header) return;
      const targetIdx = masterHeaderMap[header];
      if (targetIdx !== undefined) {
        out[targetIdx] = row[sourceIdx];
      }
    });


    output.push(out);
  });


  if (output.length > 0) {
    masterSheet.getRange(DATA_START_ROW, 1, output.length, masterHeaders.length).setValues(output);
    clearSheetRuntimeCachesForSheet_(masterSheet);
  }


  return output.length;
}

  // v1.1.0: Runtime column-width copying removed. Dashboard templates are formatting authority.
  return;
}

function getExpiredPhoneHighlightColor_() {
  return "#E0A3C1";
}


function isDateExpiredBeforeToday_(value) {
  const d = coerceToValidDate_(value);
  if (!d) return false;


  const today = new Date();
  const todayOnly = new Date(today.getFullYear(), today.getMonth(), today.getDate());
  const testOnly = new Date(d.getFullYear(), d.getMonth(), d.getDate());


  return testOnly < todayOnly;
}


function highlightAndStrikeExpiredADPhones_(sheet) {
  // v1.1.0: Runtime highlight/strike formatting removed. Dashboard templates are formatting authority.
  return;
}




function isExpiredADPhoneCell_(row, headers, phoneIdx) {
  const header = headers[phoneIdx];
  if (!header) return false;


  const match = String(header).match(/^(AD[123]) - Phone$/);
  if (!match) return false;


  const validToHeader = `${match[1]} - Phone Valid Dates To`;
  const validToIdx = headers.indexOf(validToHeader);


  if (validToIdx === -1) return false;


  return isDateExpiredBeforeToday_(row[validToIdx]);
}


function createMasterList() {
  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  const monthParts = promptForLockedYearReportMonth_("Create Master List");
  if (!monthParts) return;


  const timing = startRuntimeTiming_("Create Master List", monthParts);
  let masterSheet = null;
  let copiedRowCount = 0;


  try {
    markRuntimeStep_(timing, "Start");


    const demoSheet = getCurrentDemoPSheet_(monthParts);
    markRuntimeStep_(timing, "Locate current processed Demo P sheet");


    if (!demoSheet) {
      notify_("Demo P sheet for that month was not found. Run Process Demo P first.");
      markRuntimeStep_(timing, "Stopped - missing Demo P");
      writeRuntimeTimingReport_(timing);
      return;
    }


    const masterName = buildMonthlySheetName_(MASTER_LIST_PREFIX, monthParts.firstDay, monthParts.lastDay);


    masterSheet = ss.getSheetByName(masterName);
    if (masterSheet) {
      const ui = SpreadsheetApp.getUi();
      const response = ui.alert(
        "Master List Exists",
        `${masterName} already exists. Replace it?`,
        ui.ButtonSet.YES_NO
      );


      if (response !== ui.Button.YES) {
        notify_("Create Master List cancelled.");
        markRuntimeStep_(timing, "Cancelled - existing Master List not replaced");
        writeRuntimeTimingReport_(timing);
        return;
      }


      ss.deleteSheet(masterSheet);
      markRuntimeStep_(timing, "Delete existing Master List sheet");
    }


    masterSheet = createMasterListSheetFromTemplate_(ss, masterName, monthParts);
    markRuntimeStep_(timing, "Copy Template - Master List as output sheet");


    buildMasterListHeadersBeforeDataCopy_(demoSheet, masterSheet);
    markRuntimeStep_(timing, "Build Master List headers");


    copiedRowCount = copyPrimaryDemoPRowsToMasterListByHeader_(demoSheet, masterSheet, monthParts);
    markRuntimeStep_(timing, "Copy Primary PMR rows from processed Demo P to Master List");


    markRuntimeStep_(timing, "Master List output row trimming skipped - template controls sheet size");


    fillMasterListMetadataColumns_(masterSheet, monthParts, demoSheet.getName(), "Created from processed Demo P primary rows");
    markRuntimeStep_(timing, "Fill Master List metadata columns");


    syncMasterListFromUnlockedCarePlan_(masterSheet, monthParts, null);
    markRuntimeStep_(timing, "Sync Unlocked CP to Master List primary rows");


    syncMasterListFromCarePlanDue_(masterSheet, monthParts, null);
    markRuntimeStep_(timing, "Sync Care Plan Due to Master List primary rows");


    setUniqueSheetName_(masterSheet, masterName);
    markRuntimeStep_(timing, "Set final Master List sheet name");


    enforceMasterListFinalDisplay_(masterSheet);
    markRuntimeStep_(timing, "Final Master List display enforcement");


    lockFinalOutputRowHeights_(masterSheet, "Master List");
    markRuntimeStep_(timing, "Lock Master List final row heights");


    writeRuntimeTimingReport_(timing);


    notify_(
      `Master List created. Copied ${copiedRowCount} Primary PMR row(s) from processed Demo P.\n\n` +
      `Runtime: ${formatSeconds_((new Date().getTime() - timing.startMs) / 1000)}`
    );


    return masterSheet;
  } catch (err) {
    markRuntimeStep_(timing, "ERROR - " + err.message);
    try {
      writeRuntimeTimingReport_(timing);
    } catch (reportErr) {
      Logger.log("Could not write timing report: " + reportErr.message);
    }
    throw err;
  }
}




function copyPrimaryDemoPRowsToMasterListByHeader_(demoSheet, masterSheet, monthParts) {
  const demoData = getDataValues_(demoSheet, HEADER_ROW, DATA_START_ROW);

  if (!demoData.values.length) return 0;

  const demoHeaders = demoData.headers;
  const demoHeaderMap = demoData.headerMap;
  const masterHeaders = getHeaders_(masterSheet, HEADER_ROW);
  const masterHeaderMap = getHeaderMap_(masterSheet, HEADER_ROW);

  const pmrIdx = getPMRIndex_(demoHeaderMap);
  if (pmrIdx === -1) {
    throw new Error("Demo P is missing Participant PMR# / PMR # column.");
  }

  const primaryIdx = demoHeaderMap["Primary PMR Row"];
  const dobIdx = getDOBIndex_(demoHeaderMap);

  function getMasterTargetIndex_(header) {
    if (masterHeaderMap[header] !== undefined) return masterHeaderMap[header];

    const aliases = {
      "Participant PMR#": ["PMR #", "PMR#", "Participant PMR"],
      "PMR #": ["Participant PMR#", "PMR#", "Participant PMR"],
      "PMR#": ["Participant PMR#", "PMR #", "Participant PMR"],
      "Participant PMR": ["Participant PMR#", "PMR #", "PMR#"]
    };

    const candidates = aliases[header] || [];
    for (let i = 0; i < candidates.length; i++) {
      if (masterHeaderMap[candidates[i]] !== undefined) return masterHeaderMap[candidates[i]];
    }

    return undefined;
  }

  function buildOutputRows_(mode) {
    const output = [];
    const seenPMRs = new Set();

    demoData.values.forEach(row => {
      const pmr = normalizePMR_(row[pmrIdx]);
      if (!pmr) return;

      let includeRow = false;

      if (mode === "primary") {
        includeRow = primaryIdx !== undefined && isPrimaryPMRRowValue_(row[primaryIdx]);
      } else if (mode === "dob") {
        includeRow = dobIdx !== -1 && normalizeCompareValue_(row[dobIdx]) !== "" && !seenPMRs.has(pmr);
      } else if (mode === "first") {
        includeRow = !seenPMRs.has(pmr);
      }

      if (!includeRow) return;
      seenPMRs.add(pmr);

      const out = new Array(masterHeaders.length).fill("");

      demoHeaders.forEach((header, sourceIdx) => {
        if (!header) return;
        const targetIdx = getMasterTargetIndex_(header);
        if (targetIdx !== undefined) {
          out[targetIdx] = row[sourceIdx];
        }
      });

      output.push(out);
    });

    return output;
  }

  let output = buildOutputRows_("primary");

  /*
   * v1.5.1:
   * Master List creation depends on Primary PMR Row when available. Some v1.5
   * runs produced processed Demo P sheets where the Primary PMR Row column existed
   * but was blank, which caused an empty Master List. Preserve Primary PMR
   * governance first, then fall back to one row per PMR using DOB/first-row
   * selection only when no primary rows are detected.
   */
  if (output.length === 0) output = buildOutputRows_("dob");
  if (output.length === 0) output = buildOutputRows_("first");

  if (output.length > 0) {
    masterSheet.getRange(DATA_START_ROW, 1, output.length, masterHeaders.length).setValues(output);
    clearSheetRuntimeCachesForSheet_(masterSheet);
  }

  return output.length;
}





function getMasterListTemplateHeaders_() {
  /*
   * v1.4.24:
   * Legacy Master List template helper now defers to Dashboard/App C header
   * defaults instead of COLUMN_FORMATS or MASTER_LIST_ADDED_HEADERS.
   */
  return (getDefaultHeaderSets_()[RFF_SHEET_TYPES.MASTER_LIST] || [])
    .map(function(item) { return item.header; });
}

function createOrRefreshMasterListTemplate_(ss) {
  /*
   * v1.4.25:
   * Legacy Master List template builder is restricted. All templates, including
   * Master List, must build through the shared dashboard template pipeline.
   */
  const dashboard = loadDashboardConfig_();
  const sheetDef = getSheetDefinitionByType_(dashboard, SHEET_TYPE.MASTER_LIST);
  return createOrRefreshTemplateFromDashboard_(dashboard, sheetDef, null);
}


function getOrCreateMasterListTemplate_(ss) {
  ss = ss || SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  let template = ss.getSheetByName(MASTER_LIST_TEMPLATE_SHEET);
  if (!template) template = createOrRefreshMasterListTemplate_(ss);
  return template;
}


function createMasterListSheetFromTemplate_(ss, targetName, monthParts) {
  ss = ss || SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  const existing = ss.getSheetByName(targetName);
  if (existing && ss.getSheets().length > 1) ss.deleteSheet(existing);


  const dashboard = loadDashboardConfig_();
  const sheetDef = getSheetDefinitionByType_(dashboard, SHEET_TYPE.MASTER_LIST);
  const template = ss.getSheetByName(sheetDef.templateName);
  if (!template) {
    throw new Error("Template not found: " + sheetDef.templateName + ". Run Create / Refresh Master List Template first.");
  }


  // v1.4.19: monthly Master List creation must copy the verified template only.
  // Do not rebuild dashboard formatting during monthly processing.
  const sheet = template.copyTo(ss);
  sheet.showSheet();
  setMonthlySheetNameFast_(sheet, targetName);


  try {
    sheet.getRange("A1:D2").setValues([
      ["Master List", "", "", ""],
      ["Date:", monthParts.firstDay, "to", monthParts.lastDay]
    ]);
    const lastRow = sheet.getMaxRows();
    const lastCol = sheet.getMaxColumns();
    if (lastRow >= DATA_START_ROW && lastCol > 0) {
      sheet.getRange(DATA_START_ROW, 1, lastRow - DATA_START_ROW + 1, lastCol).clearContent();
    }
  } catch (err) {
    Logger.log("Master List template copy initialization skipped: " + err.message);
  }


  clearSheetRuntimeCachesForSheet_(sheet);
  return sheet;
}

  // v1.1.0: Legacy Master List template formatting removed. Dashboard template builder owns formatting.
  return;

    ["Master List", "", "", ""],
    ["Date:", monthParts.firstDay, "to", monthParts.lastDay]
  ]);
}

  masterSheet.clearContents();


  if (masterSheet.getMaxColumns() < 4) {
    masterSheet.insertColumnsAfter(masterSheet.getMaxColumns(), 4 - masterSheet.getMaxColumns());
  }


  writeMasterListTitleDateBlock_(masterSheet, monthParts);


  clearSheetRuntimeCachesForSheet_(masterSheet);
}


function copyDemoPHeaderRowsToMasterList_(demoSheet, masterSheet, monthParts) {
  const demoLastCol = Math.max(demoSheet.getLastColumn(), 1);


  masterSheet.clear();


  demoSheet.getRange(1, 1, HEADER_ROW, demoLastCol)
    .copyTo(masterSheet.getRange(1, 1, HEADER_ROW, demoLastCol), { contentsOnly: false });
  clearHeaderCacheForSheet_(masterSheet);


  writeMasterListTitleDateBlock_(masterSheet, monthParts);


  try {
    const missingColumns = demoLastCol - masterSheet.getMaxColumns();
    if (missingColumns > 0) {
      masterSheet.insertColumnsAfter(masterSheet.getMaxColumns(), missingColumns);
    }
// v1.1.0 removed orphaned legacy formatting statement.
  } catch (err) {
    Logger.log("Column growth skipped while copying Demo P headers: " + err.message);
  }
}


function copyQualifyingDemoPRowsToMasterList_(demoSheet, masterSheet, monthParts) {
  const demoLastRow = demoSheet.getLastRow();
  const demoLastCol = demoSheet.getLastColumn();


  if (demoLastRow < DATA_START_ROW) return;


  const headers = getHeaders_(demoSheet, HEADER_ROW);
  const headerMap = buildHeaderIndexMap_(headers);
  const pmrIdx = getPMRIndex_(headerMap);


  if (pmrIdx === -1) {
    throw new Error("Demo P is missing Participant PMR# / PMR # column.");
  }


  const data = demoSheet.getRange(DATA_START_ROW, 1, demoLastRow - DATA_START_ROW + 1, demoLastCol).getValues();


  const disenrolledPMRs = buildDisenrolledPMRSetFromDemoPValues_(data, headerMap);
  const exclusionPMRs = loadDisenrolledExclusionPMRsForPart3_();
  exclusionPMRs.forEach(pmr => disenrolledPMRs.add(pmr));


  const qualifyingRows = [];


  data.forEach(row => {
    const pmr = normalizePMR_(row[pmrIdx]);
    if (!pmr) return;
    if (disenrolledPMRs.has(pmr)) return;


    qualifyingRows.push(row);
  });


  if (qualifyingRows.length > 0) {
    masterSheet.getRange(DATA_START_ROW, 1, qualifyingRows.length, demoLastCol).setValues(qualifyingRows);
  }
}


function fillMasterListMetadataColumns_(sheet, monthParts, sourceSheetName, statusText) {
  const lastRow = sheet.getLastRow();
  if (lastRow < DATA_START_ROW) return;


  const headers = getHeaders_(sheet, HEADER_ROW);
  const headerMap = buildHeaderIndexMap_(headers);


  const required = ["Master List Update Status", "Master List Update Month", "Master List Source Sheet"];
  const missing = required.filter(function(header) { return headerMap[header] === undefined; });
  if (missing.length) {
    Logger.log("Master List metadata write skipped for missing dashboard-defined columns: " + missing.join(", "));
  }


  const rowCount = lastRow - DATA_START_ROW + 1;
  const metadata = {
    "Master List Update Status": statusText || "Created",
    "Master List Update Month": monthParts.firstDay,
    "Master List Source Sheet": sourceSheetName || ""
  };


  const indexes = required
    .map(function(header) { return headerMap[header]; })
    .filter(function(idx) { return idx !== undefined; })
    .sort(function(a, b) { return a - b; });


  if (!indexes.length) return;


  if (indexes[indexes.length - 1] - indexes[0] + 1 === indexes.length) {
    const startIdx = indexes[0];
    const width = indexes.length;
    const rowTemplate = [];
    for (let c = startIdx; c <= indexes[indexes.length - 1]; c++) {
      const header = headers[c];
      rowTemplate.push(Object.prototype.hasOwnProperty.call(metadata, header) ? metadata[header] : "");
    }
    const values = Array.from({ length: rowCount }, function() { return rowTemplate.slice(); });
    sheet.getRange(DATA_START_ROW, startIdx + 1, rowCount, width).setValues(values);
    return;
  }


  indexes.forEach(function(idx) {
    const header = headers[idx];
    const value = Object.prototype.hasOwnProperty.call(metadata, header) ? metadata[header] : "";
    const values = Array.from({ length: rowCount }, function() { return [value]; });
    sheet.getRange(DATA_START_ROW, idx + 1, rowCount, 1).setValues(values);
  });
}

  };

}

function getMonthPartsFromTitleRows_(sheet) {
  const firstDay = coerceToValidDate_(sheet.getRange("B2").getValue()) ||
    coerceToValidDate_(sheet.getRange("B2").getDisplayValue());
  const lastDay = coerceToValidDate_(sheet.getRange("D2").getValue()) ||
    coerceToValidDate_(sheet.getRange("D2").getDisplayValue());


  if (!firstDay || !lastDay) return null;


  return {
    firstDay: firstDay,
    lastDay: lastDay
  };
}


function loadDisenrolledExclusionPMRsForPart3_() {
  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  const sheet = ss.getSheetByName(DISENROLLED_EXCLUSION_SHEET);
  const pmrs = new Set();


  if (!sheet || sheet.getLastRow() < 2) return pmrs;


  const headers = sheet.getRange(1, 1, 1, sheet.getLastColumn())
    .getValues()[0]
    .map(h => String(h || "").trim());


  const headerMap = buildHeaderIndexMap_(headers);
  const pmrIdx = getPMRIndex_(headerMap);


  if (pmrIdx === -1) return pmrs;


  const values = sheet.getRange(2, 1, sheet.getLastRow() - 1, sheet.getLastColumn()).getValues();


  values.forEach(row => {
    const pmr = normalizePMR_(row[pmrIdx]);
    if (pmr) pmrs.add(pmr);
  });


  return pmrs;
}
