function extractFirstDateFromSheetName_(sheetName) {
  const text = String(sheetName || "").trim();
  const match = text.match(/(\d{1,2})\.(\d{1,2})\.(\d{2}|\d{4})/);
  if (!match) return null;


  const month = Number(match[1]);
  const day = Number(match[2]);
  let year = Number(match[3]);
  if (year < 100) year += 2000;


  const date = createLocalDateOnly_(year, month - 1, day);
  if (
    date.getFullYear() !== year ||
    date.getMonth() !== month - 1 ||
    date.getDate() !== day
  ) {
    return null;
  }


  return date;
}


function parseIndexMonthDate_(value) {
  if (value instanceof Date && !isNaN(value.getTime())) {
    return createLocalDateOnly_(value.getFullYear(), value.getMonth(), value.getDate());
  }


  const text = String(value || "").trim();
  if (!text) return null;


  const dotMatch = text.match(/^(\d{1,2})\.(\d{1,2})\.(\d{2}|\d{4})$/);
  if (dotMatch) {
    const month = Number(dotMatch[1]);
    const day = Number(dotMatch[2]);
    let year = Number(dotMatch[3]);
    if (year < 100) year += 2000;


    const date = createLocalDateOnly_(year, month - 1, day);
    if (
      date.getFullYear() === year &&
      date.getMonth() === month - 1 &&
      date.getDate() === day
    ) {
      return date;
    }
  }


  return coerceToValidDate_(text);
}


function createIndexSheet() {
  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  let sheet = ss.getSheetByName("Index");


  if (!sheet) {
    sheet = ss.insertSheet("Index", 0);
  } else {
    sheet.clear();
  }


  sheet;


  const rows = [];


  ss.getSheets().forEach(sh => {
    const sheetName = sh.getName();
    if (sheetName === "Index") return;


    const monthDate = extractFirstDateFromSheetName_(sheetName);
    const monthText = monthDate ? formatDateForSheetName_(monthDate) : "";
    const sheetType = getSheetTypeForOrganization_(sheetName);
    const hidden = sh.isSheetHidden() ? "Yes" : "No";


    rows.push([
      monthText,
      sheetName,
      `=HYPERLINK("#gid=${sh.getSheetId()}","Open")`,
      sheetType,
      hidden
    ]);
  });


  rows.sort((a, b) => {
    const aDate = parseIndexMonthDate_(a[0]);
    const bDate = parseIndexMonthDate_(b[0]);


    if (aDate && bDate && aDate.getTime() !== bDate.getTime()) {
      return bDate.getTime() - aDate.getTime();
    }


    const aType = SHEET_TAB_ORDER.indexOf(a[3]);
    const bType = SHEET_TAB_ORDER.indexOf(b[3]);
    const aOrder = aType === -1 ? 999 : aType;
    const bOrder = bType === -1 ? 999 : bType;


    if (aOrder !== bOrder) return aOrder - bOrder;


    return String(a[1]).localeCompare(String(b[1]));
  });


  sheet.getRange(1, 1, 1, INDEX_HEADERS.length)
    .setValues([INDEX_HEADERS]);


  if (rows.length > 0) {
    sheet.getRange(2, 1, rows.length, INDEX_HEADERS.length)
      .setValues(rows);
  }


  applyIndexSheetRowFills_(sheet);


  sheet;
  sheet;
  sheet;
  sheet;
  sheet;
  sheet;


  if (sheet.getFilter()) {
    sheet;
  }


  sheet.getRange(1, 1, Math.max(sheet.getLastRow(), 1), INDEX_HEADERS.length);


  applyCurrentVsOlderTabColors_();
  organizeSheetTabs_();
  applyCurrentVsOlderTabColors_();


  return sheet;


  applyStandardRowHeights_(sheet);
}

function buildMonthlyChangeReportFromDemoP() {
  const monthParts = promptForLockedYearReportMonth_("Build Monthly Change Report");
  if (!monthParts) return;


  buildMonthlyChangeReportFromDemoPForMonth_(monthParts);
}


function buildMonthlyChangeReportFromDemoPForMonth_(monthParts) {
  if (!monthParts) return null;


  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  const currentDemo = getCurrentDemoPSheet_(monthParts);
  const previousDemo = getPreviousDemoPSheet_(monthParts);


  if (!currentDemo) {
    notify_(
      "Current month Demo P was not found.\n\n" +
      `Expected current month start date: ${formatDateForSheetName_(monthParts.firstDay)}\n` +
      "Example accepted name:\n" +
      `Demo P ${formatDateForSheetName_(monthParts.firstDay)} - ${formatDateForSheetName_(monthParts.lastDay)}`
    );
    return null;
  }


  if (!previousDemo) {
    notify_(
      "Previous month Demo P was not found.\n\n" +
      "The Monthly Change Report compares previous month Demo P to current month Demo P.\n\n" +
      `Current source found: ${currentDemo.getName()}\n` +
      `Expected previous month start date: ${formatDateForSheetName_(monthParts.previousMonthFirstDay)}\n` +
      "Example accepted name:\n" +
      `Demo P ${formatDateForSheetName_(monthParts.previousMonthFirstDay)} - ${formatDateForSheetName_(monthParts.previousMonthLastDay)}`
    );
    return null;
  }


  formatDateColumnsByHeader_(currentDemo, HEADER_ROW, DATA_START_ROW);
  formatDateColumnsByHeader_(previousDemo, HEADER_ROW, DATA_START_ROW);


  const sectionData = compareRawDemoPForSectionReport_(previousDemo, currentDemo, monthParts);
  const totalPMRs =
    sectionData.enrollmentPMRs.size +
    sectionData.disenrollmentPMRs.size +
    sectionData.demographicPMRs.size +
    sectionData.caseloadPMRs.size +
    sectionData.contactPMRs.size;


  if (totalPMRs === 0) {
    notify_(
      "No raw Demo P changes found. Monthly Change Report was not created.\n\n" +
      `Current source: ${currentDemo.getName()}\n` +
      `Previous source: ${previousDemo.getName()}\n\n` +
      `Current Demo P rows read: ${sectionData.currentData.values.length}\n` +
      `Previous Demo P rows read: ${sectionData.previousData.values.length}\n` +
      `Current PMRs found: ${sectionData.currentData.rowsByPMR.size}\n` +
      `Previous PMRs found: ${sectionData.previousData.rowsByPMR.size}\n\n` +
      "For enrollments, Capitation Date must equal the report date. " +
      "For disenrollments, Disenrollment Effective Date must be between the previous month first day and the report date."
    );
    return null;
  }


  const reportName = buildMonthlySheetName_(MONTHLY_CHANGE_REPORT_PREFIX, monthParts.firstDay, monthParts.lastDay);
  let reportSheet = ss.getSheetByName(reportName);


  if (reportSheet) ss.deleteSheet(reportSheet);


  reportSheet = ss.insertSheet(reportName);
  reportSheet;


  buildMonthlyChangeReportSectionLayout_(reportSheet, currentDemo, sectionData.currentData.headers, monthParts);
  populateMonthlyChangeReportSections_(reportSheet, sectionData, monthParts);
  formatMonthlyChangeReportSectionSheet_(reportSheet, sectionData.currentData.headers);


  setUniqueSheetName_(reportSheet, reportName);
  formatDateColumnsOnAllSheets_();
  createIndexSheet();


    applyStandardRowHeights_(reportSheet);


notify_(
    "Monthly Change Report created.\n\n" +
    `Current source: ${currentDemo.getName()}\n` +
    `Previous source: ${previousDemo.getName()}\n\n` +
    `Enrollments: ${sectionData.enrollmentPMRs.size}\n` +
    `Disenrollments: ${sectionData.disenrollmentPMRs.size}\n` +
    `Demographic Changes: ${sectionData.demographicPMRs.size}\n` +
    `Caseload Changes: ${sectionData.caseloadPMRs.size}\n` +
    `Contact Changes: ${sectionData.contactPMRs.size}`
  );


  return reportSheet;
}




function compareRawDemoPForSectionReport_(previousDemo, currentDemo, monthParts) {
  const previousData = getRawDemoPDataForCompare_(previousDemo);
  const currentData = getRawDemoPDataForCompare_(currentDemo);


  const enrollmentPMRs = new Set();
  const disenrollmentPMRs = new Set();
  const demographicPMRs = new Set();
  const caseloadPMRs = new Set();
  const contactPMRs = new Set();


  const demographicChangedColumnsByPMR = new Map();
  const caseloadChangedColumnsByPMR = new Map();
  const contactChangedColumnsByPMR = new Map();


  currentData.rowsByPMR.forEach((currentRows, pmr) => {
    const previousRows = previousData.rowsByPMR.get(pmr) || [];


    const capitationHeader = "Capitation Date";
    const disenrollEffectiveHeader = "Disenrollment Effective Date";


    const mostRecentCapitationDate = getMostRecentDateFromRowsByHeader_(
      currentRows,
      currentData.headerMap,
      capitationHeader
    );


    const isEnrollmentPMR = isSameDate_(mostRecentCapitationDate, monthParts.firstDay);


    const isDisenrollmentPMR =
      currentRows.some(item => {
        const effectiveDate = getFieldValueFromRow_(
          item.values,
          currentData.headerMap,
          disenrollEffectiveHeader
        );


        return isDateInStrictLocalRangeInclusive_(
          effectiveDate,
          monthParts.previousMonthFirstDay,
          monthParts.firstDay
        );
      });


    if (isEnrollmentPMR) enrollmentPMRs.add(pmr);
    if (isDisenrollmentPMR) disenrollmentPMRs.add(pmr);


    if (isEnrollmentPMR || isDisenrollmentPMR) return;


    if (isParticipantEnrollmentStatusDisenrolled_(currentRows, currentData.headerMap)) return;


    const currentDobRows = rowsWithDOBOnlyForSection_(currentRows, currentData.headerMap);
    const previousDobRows = rowsWithDOBOnlyForSection_(previousRows, previousData.headerMap);


    const demographicChangedColumns = getChangedColumnsForSectionRows_(
      currentDobRows,
      previousDobRows,
      currentData.headers,
      previousData.headers,
      RAW_DEMO_P_DEMOGRAPHIC_FIELDS
    );


    if (demographicChangedColumns.size > 0) {
      demographicPMRs.add(pmr);
      demographicChangedColumnsByPMR.set(pmr, demographicChangedColumns);
    }


    const caseloadChangedColumns = getChangedColumnsForSectionRows_(
      currentDobRows,
      previousDobRows,
      currentData.headers,
      previousData.headers,
      RAW_DEMO_P_CASELOAD_FIELDS
    );


    if (caseloadChangedColumns.size > 0) {
      caseloadPMRs.add(pmr);
      caseloadChangedColumnsByPMR.set(pmr, caseloadChangedColumns);
    }


    const contactChangedColumns = getChangedColumnsForSectionRows_(
      currentRows,
      previousRows,
      currentData.headers,
      previousData.headers,
      RAW_DEMO_P_CONTACT_FIELDS
    );


    if (contactChangedColumns.size > 0) {
      contactPMRs.add(pmr);
      contactChangedColumnsByPMR.set(pmr, contactChangedColumns);
    }
  });


  enrollmentPMRs.forEach(pmr => {
    demographicPMRs.delete(pmr);
    caseloadPMRs.delete(pmr);
    contactPMRs.delete(pmr);
  });


  disenrollmentPMRs.forEach(pmr => {
    demographicPMRs.delete(pmr);
    caseloadPMRs.delete(pmr);
    contactPMRs.delete(pmr);
  });


  return {
    previousData: previousData,
    currentData: currentData,
    enrollmentPMRs: enrollmentPMRs,
    disenrollmentPMRs: disenrollmentPMRs,
    demographicPMRs: demographicPMRs,
    caseloadPMRs: caseloadPMRs,
    contactPMRs: contactPMRs,
    demographicChangedColumnsByPMR: demographicChangedColumnsByPMR,
    caseloadChangedColumnsByPMR: caseloadChangedColumnsByPMR,
    contactChangedColumnsByPMR: contactChangedColumnsByPMR
  };
}


function rowsWithDOBOnlyForSection_(items, headerMap) {
  const dobIdx = getDOBIndex_(headerMap);
  if (dobIdx === -1) return [];
  return (items || []).filter(item => normalizeCompareValue_(item.values[dobIdx]) !== "");
}


function getChangedColumnsForSectionRows_(currentItems, previousItems, currentHeaders, previousHeaders, columnsToCompare) {
  const changed = new Set();


  if (!currentItems || currentItems.length === 0) return changed;


  if (!previousItems || previousItems.length === 0) return changed;


  columnsToCompare.forEach(header => {


    if (currentHeaders.indexOf(header) === -1 || previousHeaders.indexOf(header) === -1) return;


    const currentSig = buildColumnSignatureForSection_(currentItems, currentHeaders, [header]);
    const previousSig = buildColumnSignatureForSection_(previousItems, previousHeaders, [header]);


    if (currentSig !== previousSig) changed.add(header);
  });


  return changed;
}


function buildColumnSignatureForSection_(items, headers, columnsToCompare) {
  const headerMap = buildHeaderIndexMap_(headers);


  return (items || [])
    .map(item => {
      return columnsToCompare.map(header => {
        const idx = headerMap[header];
        if (idx === undefined || idx === -1) return "";
        return normalizeCompareValue_(item.values[idx]);
      }).join("~");
    })
    .sort()
    .join("||");
}


function buildMonthlyChangeReportSectionLayout_(reportSheet, sourceSheet, headers, monthParts) {
  const reportHeaders = getMonthlyChangeReportHeaders_(headers);
  const lastCol = reportHeaders.length;


  reportSheet.clear();


  reportSheet.getRange("A1").setValue("Monthly Change Report");
  reportSheet.getRange("A2").setValue("Date");
  reportSheet.getRange("B2").setValue(monthParts.firstDay);
  reportSheet.getRange("C2").setValue("to");
  reportSheet.getRange("D2").setValue(monthParts.lastDay);
  reportSheet.getRange(HEADER_ROW, 1, 1, lastCol).setValues([reportHeaders]);


  applyMonthlyChangeStandardTopRows_(reportSheet, lastCol);


  setupMonthlyChangeSectionLayout_(reportSheet, sourceSheet, reportHeaders, 5, "Enrollments");
  setupMonthlyChangeSectionLayout_(reportSheet, sourceSheet, reportHeaders, 12, "Disenrollments");
  setupMonthlyChangeSectionLayout_(reportSheet, sourceSheet, reportHeaders, 19, "Demographic Changes");
  setupMonthlyChangeSectionLayout_(reportSheet, sourceSheet, reportHeaders, 26, "Caseload Changes");
  setupMonthlyChangeSectionLayout_(reportSheet, sourceSheet, reportHeaders, 33, "Contact Changes");


  if (lastCol > 0) {
    reportSheet.getRange(1, 1, 40, lastCol);
  }


  applyMonthlyChangeStandardTopRows_(reportSheet, lastCol);
  applyMonthlyChangeAllSubsectionFormats_(reportSheet, lastCol);


  reportSheet;
  reportSheet;


  for (let col = 1; col <= lastCol; col++) {
    try {
      if (col <= sourceSheet.getLastColumn()) {
// v1.1.0 removed orphaned legacy formatting statement.
      } else {
        reportSheet;
      }
    } catch (err) {
      Logger.log("Monthly Change Report column width skipped for col " + col + ": " + err.message);
    }
  }
}


function setupMonthlyChangeSectionLayout_(reportSheet, sourceSheet, headers, titleRow, titleText) {
  const lastCol = headers.length;
  const spacerRow = titleRow + 1;
  const headerRow = titleRow + 2;


  reportSheet.getRange(titleRow, 1).setValue(titleText);
  reportSheet.getRange(headerRow, 1, 1, lastCol).setValues([headers]);


  applyMonthlyChangeSubsectionFormat_(
    reportSheet,
    titleRow,
    headerRow,
    lastCol,
    SHEET_BASE_COLORS[SHEET_TYPE.MONTHLY_CHANGE]
  );
}


function insertMonthlyDisenrollmentRowsStrict_(reportSheet, currentData, pmrSet, monthParts) {


  if (!monthParts) return;


  const sectionTitle = "Disenrollments";
  const titleRow = findMonthlyChangeSectionTitleRow_(reportSheet, sectionTitle);
  if (titleRow === -1) return;


  const headerRow = titleRow + 2;
  const insertAt = headerRow + 1;
  const reportHeaders = getMonthlyChangeReportHeaders_(currentData.headers);
  const lastCol = reportHeaders.length;


  const effectiveIdx = currentData.headerMap["Disenrollment Effective Date"];
  const pmrIdx = getPMRIndex_(currentData.headerMap);


  if (effectiveIdx === undefined || effectiveIdx === -1 || pmrIdx === -1) return;


  const rowsToInsert = [];
  const usedPMRs = new Set();


  currentData.values.forEach(row => {
    const pmr = normalizePMR_(row[pmrIdx]);
    if (!pmr || usedPMRs.has(pmr)) return;


    const effectiveDate = row[effectiveIdx];


    if (!isDateDisplayInReportWindow_(
      effectiveDate,
      monthParts.previousMonthFirstDay,
      monthParts.firstDay
    )) {
      return;
    }


    rowsToInsert.push(buildMonthlyChangeReportRow_(
      row,
      currentData.headers,
      reportHeaders,
      new Set()
    ));


    usedPMRs.add(pmr);
  });


  if (rowsToInsert.length === 0) return;


  reportSheet.insertRowsBefore(insertAt, rowsToInsert.length);


  const dataRange = reportSheet.getRange(insertAt, 1, rowsToInsert.length, lastCol);
  dataRange.setValues(rowsToInsert);
  dataRange;


  try {
    reportSheet.getRange(headerRow, 1, 1, lastCol)
      .copyTo(dataRange, SpreadsheetApp.CopyPasteType.PASTE_FORMAT, false);
  } catch (err) {
    Logger.log("Monthly Change disenrollment data format copy skipped: " + err.message);
  }


  dataRange;


  reportSheet;
}


function populateMonthlyChangeReportSections_(reportSheet, sectionData, monthParts) {
  insertMonthlyChangeSectionRows_(
    reportSheet,
    sectionData.currentData,
    sectionData.enrollmentPMRs,
    "Enrollments",
    "dobOnly",
    new Map(),
    monthParts
  );


  insertMonthlyDisenrollmentRowsStrict_(
    reportSheet,
    sectionData.currentData,
    sectionData.disenrollmentPMRs,
    monthParts
  );


  insertMonthlyChangeSectionRows_(
    reportSheet,
    sectionData.currentData,
    sectionData.demographicPMRs,
    "Demographic Changes",
    "dobOnly",
    sectionData.demographicChangedColumnsByPMR,
    monthParts
  );


  insertMonthlyChangeSectionRows_(
    reportSheet,
    sectionData.currentData,
    sectionData.caseloadPMRs,
    "Caseload Changes",
    "dobOnly",
    sectionData.caseloadChangedColumnsByPMR,
    monthParts
  );


  insertMonthlyChangeSectionRows_(
    reportSheet,
    sectionData.currentData,
    sectionData.contactPMRs,
    "Contact Changes",
    "allRows",
    sectionData.contactChangedColumnsByPMR,
    monthParts
  );
}


function insertMonthlyChangeSectionRows_(reportSheet, currentData, pmrSet, sectionTitle, rowMode, changedColumnsByPMR, monthParts) {
  if (!pmrSet || pmrSet.size === 0) return;


  const titleRow = findMonthlyChangeSectionTitleRow_(reportSheet, sectionTitle);
  if (titleRow === -1) return;


  const headerRow = titleRow + 2;
  const insertAt = headerRow + 1;
  const reportHeaders = getMonthlyChangeReportHeaders_(currentData.headers);
  const lastCol = reportHeaders.length;
  const dobIdx = getDOBIndex_(currentData.headerMap);
  const disenrollEffectiveIdx = currentData.headerMap["Disenrollment Effective Date"];


  const allowDuplicateRowsForPMR = sectionTitle === "Contact Changes";


  const rowsToInsert = [];
  const pmrForEachInsertedRow = [];


  Array.from(pmrSet).sort().forEach(pmr => {
    const items = currentData.rowsByPMR.get(pmr) || [];
    let insertedForThisPMR = false;


    items.forEach(item => {
      if (!allowDuplicateRowsForPMR && insertedForThisPMR) return;


      if (rowMode === "dobOnly" && (dobIdx === -1 || normalizeCompareValue_(item.values[dobIdx]) === "")) return;


      if (rowMode === "disenrollmentEffectiveRange") {
        if (disenrollEffectiveIdx === undefined || disenrollEffectiveIdx === -1 || !monthParts) return;


        const effectiveDate = item.values[disenrollEffectiveIdx];


        if (!isDateInStrictLocalRangeInclusive_(
          effectiveDate,
          monthParts.previousMonthFirstDay,
          monthParts.firstDay
        )) {
          return;
        }
      }


      const changedColumns = changedColumnsByPMR && changedColumnsByPMR.has(pmr)
        ? changedColumnsByPMR.get(pmr)
        : new Set();


      rowsToInsert.push(buildMonthlyChangeReportRow_(item.values, currentData.headers, reportHeaders, changedColumns));
      pmrForEachInsertedRow.push(pmr);


      if (!allowDuplicateRowsForPMR) insertedForThisPMR = true;
    });
  });


  if (rowsToInsert.length === 0) return;


  reportSheet.insertRowsBefore(insertAt, rowsToInsert.length);


  const dataRange = reportSheet.getRange(insertAt, 1, rowsToInsert.length, lastCol);
  dataRange.setValues(rowsToInsert);
  dataRange;


  const headerFormatRange = reportSheet.getRange(headerRow, 1, 1, lastCol);
  try {
    headerFormatRange.copyTo(dataRange, SpreadsheetApp.CopyPasteType.PASTE_FORMAT, false);
  } catch (err) {
    Logger.log("Monthly Change data format copy skipped: " + err.message);
  }


  dataRange;


  dataRange;


  if (changedColumnsByPMR && changedColumnsByPMR.size > 0) {
    const backgrounds = dataRange.getBackgrounds();


    for (let r = 0; r < backgrounds.length; r++) {
      const pmr = pmrForEachInsertedRow[r];
      const changedColumns = changedColumnsByPMR.get(pmr);


      if (!changedColumns || changedColumns.size === 0) continue;


      reportHeaders.forEach((header, colIndex) => {
        if (changedColumns.has(header)) {
          backgrounds[r][colIndex] = "#f3ffc7";
        }
      });
    }


    dataRange;
  }


  reportSheet;
}


function findMonthlyChangeSectionTitleRow_(sheet, title) {
  const lastRow = sheet.getLastRow();
  if (lastRow < 1) return -1;


  const values = sheet.getRange(1, 1, lastRow, 1).getValues();


  for (let i = 0; i < values.length; i++) {
    if (String(values[i][0] || "").trim() === title) return i + 1;
  }


  return -1;
}


function findNextMonthlyChangeSectionTitleRow_(sheet, afterRow) {
  const titles = new Set(["Enrollments", "Disenrollments", "Demographic Changes", "Caseload Changes", "Contact Changes"]);
  const lastRow = sheet.getLastRow();


  if (afterRow >= lastRow) return -1;


  const values = sheet.getRange(afterRow + 1, 1, lastRow - afterRow, 1).getValues();


  for (let i = 0; i < values.length; i++) {
    const value = String(values[i][0] || "").trim();
    if (titles.has(value)) return afterRow + 1 + i;
  }


  return -1;
}

  // v1.1.0: Runtime Monthly Change formatting removed. Dashboard templates are formatting authority.
  return;
}

  // v1.1.0: Runtime date formatting removed. Dashboard templates are formatting authority.
  return;
}




function compareRawDemoPForChanges_(previousDemo, currentDemo, monthParts) {
  const previousData = getRawDemoPDataForCompare_(previousDemo);
  const currentData = getRawDemoPDataForCompare_(currentDemo);


  const outputRows = [];
  const changedPMRs = new Map();


  currentData.participantRows.forEach((currentMain, pmr) => {
    const previousMain = previousData.participantRows.get(pmr);


    const capitationIdx = currentData.headerMap["Capitation Date"];
    const currentCapitation = capitationIdx !== undefined ? currentMain.values[capitationIdx] : "";


    const isNewPMR = !previousData.allPMRs.has(pmr);
    const isReportMonthCapitation = isSameMonth_(currentCapitation, monthParts.firstDay);


    if (isNewPMR || isReportMonthCapitation) {
      RAW_DEMO_P_ENROLLMENT_FIELDS.forEach(field => {
        const currentValue = getFieldValueFromRow_(currentMain.values, currentData.headerMap, field);
        if (normalizeCompareValue_(currentValue) !== "") {
          addMCRRow_(
            outputRows,
            changedPMRs,
            CHANGE_SECTION_ENROLLMENTS,
            pmr,
            currentMain,
            null,
            currentData,
            previousData,
            field,
            "",
            currentValue,
            monthParts
          );
        }
      });
    }
  });


  currentData.participantRows.forEach((currentMain, pmr) => {
    const effective = getFieldValueFromRow_(currentMain.values, currentData.headerMap, "Disenrollment Effective Date");
    const disenrollDate = getFieldValueFromRow_(currentMain.values, currentData.headerMap, "Disenrollment Date");
    const deathDate = getFieldValueFromRow_(currentMain.values, currentData.headerMap, "Date of Death");


    const isCurrentEffective = isSameDate_(effective, monthParts.firstDay);
    const isPriorMonthDisenroll = isSameMonth_(disenrollDate, monthParts.previousMonthFirstDay);
    const isPriorMonthDeath = isSameMonth_(deathDate, monthParts.previousMonthFirstDay);


    if (isCurrentEffective || isPriorMonthDisenroll || isPriorMonthDeath) {
      RAW_DEMO_P_DISENROLLMENT_FIELDS.forEach(field => {
        const currentValue = getFieldValueFromRow_(currentMain.values, currentData.headerMap, field);
        if (normalizeCompareValue_(currentValue) !== "") {
          addMCRRow_(
            outputRows,
            changedPMRs,
            CHANGE_SECTION_DISENROLLMENTS,
            pmr,
            currentMain,
            null,
            currentData,
            previousData,
            field,
            "",
            currentValue,
            monthParts
          );
        }
      });
    }
  });


  currentData.participantRows.forEach((currentMain, pmr) => {
    const previousMain = previousData.participantRows.get(pmr);
    if (!previousMain) return;


    RAW_DEMO_P_DEMOGRAPHIC_FIELDS.forEach(field => {
      compareSingleFieldAndAdd_(
        outputRows,
        changedPMRs,
        CHANGE_SECTION_DEMOGRAPHIC,
        pmr,
        previousMain,
        currentMain,
        previousData,
        currentData,
        field,
        monthParts,
        true
      );
    });


    RAW_DEMO_P_CASELOAD_FIELDS.forEach(field => {
      compareSingleFieldAndAdd_(
        outputRows,
        changedPMRs,
        CHANGE_SECTION_CASELOAD,
        pmr,
        previousMain,
        currentMain,
        previousData,
        currentData,
        field,
        monthParts,
        true
      );
    });
  });


  const allCurrentPMRs = Array.from(currentData.allPMRs);
  allCurrentPMRs.forEach(pmr => {
    if (!previousData.allPMRs.has(pmr)) return;


    const previousRows = previousData.rowsByPMR.get(pmr) || [];
    const currentRows = currentData.rowsByPMR.get(pmr) || [];


    const maxLength = Math.max(previousRows.length, currentRows.length);


    for (let i = 0; i < maxLength; i++) {
      const previousItem = previousRows[i] || null;
      const currentItem = currentRows[i] || null;


      RAW_DEMO_P_CONTACT_FIELDS.forEach(field => {
        const previousValue = previousItem ? getFieldValueFromRow_(previousItem.values, previousData.headerMap, field) : "";
        const currentValue = currentItem ? getFieldValueFromRow_(currentItem.values, currentData.headerMap, field) : "";


        if (!valuesAreEqual_(previousValue, currentValue)) {
          addMCRRow_(
            outputRows,
            changedPMRs,
            CHANGE_SECTION_CONTACT,
            pmr,
            currentItem,
            previousItem,
            currentData,
            previousData,
            field,
            previousValue,
            currentValue,
            monthParts
          );
        }
      });
    }
  });


  return {
    rows: outputRows,
    changedPMRs: changedPMRs
  };
}


function getRawDemoPDataForCompare_(sheet) {
  const data = getDataValues_(sheet, HEADER_ROW, DATA_START_ROW);


  const headers = data.headers;
  const headerMap = data.headerMap;
  const pmrIdx = getPMRIndex_(headerMap);
  const dobIdx = getDOBIndex_(headerMap);


  if (pmrIdx === -1) {
    throw new Error(`${sheet.getName()} is missing Participant PMR# / PMR # column.`);
  }


  const values = data.values;


  const rowsByPMR = new Map();
  const participantRows = new Map();
  const allPMRs = new Set();


  values.forEach((row, idx) => {
    const pmr = normalizePMR_(row[pmrIdx]);
    if (!pmr) return;


    allPMRs.add(pmr);


    const item = {
      rowNumber: DATA_START_ROW + idx,
      values: row
    };


    if (!rowsByPMR.has(pmr)) rowsByPMR.set(pmr, []);
    rowsByPMR.get(pmr).push(item);


    if (!participantRows.has(pmr)) {
      if (dobIdx === -1 || normalizeCompareValue_(row[dobIdx]) !== "") {
        participantRows.set(pmr, item);
      }
    }
  });


  rowsByPMR.forEach((items, pmr) => {
    if (!participantRows.has(pmr) && items.length > 0) {
      participantRows.set(pmr, items[0]);
    }
  });


  return {
    sheet: sheet,
    sheetName: sheet.getName(),
    headers: headers,
    headerMap: headerMap,
    values: values,
    rowsByPMR: rowsByPMR,
    participantRows: participantRows,
    allPMRs: allPMRs
  };
}




function compareSingleFieldAndAdd_(
  outputRows,
  changedPMRs,
  section,
  pmr,
  previousItem,
  currentItem,
  previousData,
  currentData,
  field,
  monthParts,
  skipIfCurrentDOBBlank
) {
  if (!previousItem || !currentItem) return;


  if (skipIfCurrentDOBBlank) {
    const currentDOBIdx = getDOBIndex_(currentData.headerMap);
    if (currentDOBIdx !== -1 && normalizeCompareValue_(currentItem.values[currentDOBIdx]) === "") return;
  }


  if (field !== "Participant PMR#" && currentData.headerMap[field] === undefined && previousData.headerMap[field] === undefined) {
    return;
  }


  const previousValue = getFieldValueFromRow_(previousItem.values, previousData.headerMap, field);
  const currentValue = getFieldValueFromRow_(currentItem.values, currentData.headerMap, field);


  if (!valuesAreEqual_(previousValue, currentValue)) {
    addMCRRow_(
      outputRows,
      changedPMRs,
      section,
      pmr,
      currentItem,
      previousItem,
      currentData,
      previousData,
      field,
      previousValue,
      currentValue,
      monthParts
    );
  }
}


function addMCRRow_(
  outputRows,
  changedPMRs,
  section,
  pmr,
  currentItem,
  previousItem,
  currentData,
  previousData,
  field,
  previousValue,
  currentValue,
  monthParts
) {
  const mainItem = currentItem || previousItem;
  const currentValues = currentItem ? currentItem.values : (mainItem ? mainItem.values : []);
  const currentMap = currentData.headerMap;


  const lastName = getFieldValueFromRow_(currentValues, currentMap, "Last Name");
  const firstName = getFieldValueFromRow_(currentValues, currentMap, "First Name");
  const participantName = buildParticipantName_(currentValues, currentMap);


  outputRows.push([
    section,
    pmr,
    participantName,
    lastName,
    firstName,
    field,
    displayValueForReport_(previousValue),
    displayValueForReport_(currentValue),
    previousItem ? previousItem.rowNumber : "",
    currentItem ? currentItem.rowNumber : "",
    monthParts.firstDay
  ]);


  if (!changedPMRs.has(pmr)) changedPMRs.set(pmr, new Set());
  changedPMRs.get(pmr).add(section);
}


function getFieldValueFromRow_(row, headerMap, field) {
  const idx = headerMap[field];
  if (idx === undefined || idx < 0) return "";
  return row[idx];
}


function buildParticipantName_(row, headerMap) {
  const participantName = getFieldValueFromRow_(row, headerMap, "Participant Name");
  if (normalizeCompareValue_(participantName) !== "") return participantName;


  const last = getFieldValueFromRow_(row, headerMap, "Last Name");
  const first = getFieldValueFromRow_(row, headerMap, "First Name");


  const lastText = String(last || "").trim();
  const firstText = String(first || "").trim();


  if (lastText && firstText) return `${lastText}, ${firstText}`;
  return lastText || firstText || "";
}


function displayValueForReport_(value) {
  if (value instanceof Date && !isNaN(value.getTime())) {
    return formatDateDisplay_(value);
  }
  return value === null || value === undefined ? "" : String(value);
}


function rebuildChangedPMRsFromDemoP_(currentDemo, currentMaster, reportSheet, changedInfo, monthParts, runProcessing) {


  return rebuildChangedPMRsOnExistingMaster_(
    currentDemo,
    currentMaster,
    reportSheet,
    monthParts,
    runProcessing !== false
  );
}


function getOrBuildMonthlyChangeReport_(ss, monthParts, currentDemo, previousDemo) {
  let reportSheet = getMonthlySheetByPrefixAndDate_(ss, MONTHLY_CHANGE_REPORT_PREFIX, monthParts.firstDay, monthParts.lastDay);


  if (reportSheet) return reportSheet;


  if (!currentDemo) {
    throw new Error("Current month Demo P was not found. Format Demo P first.");
  }


  if (!previousDemo) {
    throw new Error("Previous month Demo P was not found. Format the previous Demo P first.");
  }


  formatDateColumnsByHeader_(currentDemo, HEADER_ROW, DATA_START_ROW);
  formatDateColumnsByHeader_(previousDemo, HEADER_ROW, DATA_START_ROW);


  const sectionData = compareRawDemoPForSectionReport_(previousDemo, currentDemo, monthParts);
  const totalPMRs =
    sectionData.enrollmentPMRs.size +
    sectionData.disenrollmentPMRs.size +
    sectionData.demographicPMRs.size +
    sectionData.caseloadPMRs.size +
    sectionData.contactPMRs.size;


  if (totalPMRs === 0) return null;


  const reportName = buildMonthlySheetName_(MONTHLY_CHANGE_REPORT_PREFIX, monthParts.firstDay, monthParts.lastDay);
  reportSheet = ss.insertSheet(reportName);
  reportSheet;


  buildMonthlyChangeReportSectionLayout_(reportSheet, currentDemo, sectionData.currentData.headers, monthParts);
  populateMonthlyChangeReportSections_(reportSheet, sectionData, monthParts);
  formatMonthlyChangeReportSectionSheet_(reportSheet, sectionData.currentData.headers);
  setUniqueSheetName_(reportSheet, reportName);


  return reportSheet;
}


function copyPreviousMasterListToCurrentMonth_(previousMaster, monthParts) {
  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  const targetName = buildMonthlySheetName_(MASTER_LIST_PREFIX, monthParts.firstDay, monthParts.lastDay);
  const existing = ss.getSheetByName(targetName);


  if (existing) {
    ss.deleteSheet(existing);
  }


  const currentMaster = createMasterListSheetFromTemplate_(ss, targetName, monthParts);


  const lastRow = Math.max(previousMaster.getLastRow(), HEADER_ROW);
  const lastCol = Math.max(previousMaster.getLastColumn(), 1);


  if (lastCol > currentMaster.getMaxColumns()) {
    currentMaster.insertColumnsAfter(currentMaster.getMaxColumns(), lastCol - currentMaster.getMaxColumns());
  }


  if (lastRow > currentMaster.getMaxRows()) {
    currentMaster.insertRowsAfter(currentMaster.getMaxRows(), lastRow - currentMaster.getMaxRows());
  }


  const values = previousMaster.getRange(1, 1, lastRow, lastCol).getValues();
  currentMaster.getRange(1, 1, lastRow, lastCol).setValues(values);


  updateCopiedMasterListHeader_(currentMaster, monthParts);
  applyMasterListTemplateHeaderFormatting_(currentMaster, monthParts);


  ensureHeaders_(currentMaster, MASTER_LIST_ADDED_HEADERS, HEADER_ROW);
  ensureBannerSummaryOutputHeaders_(currentMaster);
  ensureContactOutputHeaders_(currentMaster);
  clearSheetRuntimeCachesForSheet_(currentMaster);


  return currentMaster;
}


function sortMasterListByParticipantNameAndPMR_(sheet) {
  sheet = sheet || SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSheet();


  const lastRow = sheet.getLastRow();
  const lastCol = sheet.getLastColumn();
  if (lastRow < DATA_START_ROW || lastCol < 1) return;


  clearAllRowGroupsIfPossible_(sheet);
  sheet.showRows(DATA_START_ROW, lastRow - DATA_START_ROW + 1);


  const headers = getHeaders_(sheet, HEADER_ROW);
  const headerMap = buildHeaderIndexMap_(headers);
  const pmrIdx = getPMRIndex_(headerMap);
  const lastNameIdx = headerMap["Last Name"];
  const firstNameIdx = headerMap["First Name"];


  if (pmrIdx === -1 || lastNameIdx === undefined || firstNameIdx === undefined) {
    notify_("Sort skipped: missing Last Name, First Name, or Participant PMR#.");
    return;
  }


  const range = sheet.getRange(DATA_START_ROW, 1, lastRow - DATA_START_ROW + 1, lastCol);
  const values = range.getValues();
  const blocksByPMR = new Map();


  values.forEach((row, idx) => {
    const pmr = normalizePMR_(row[pmrIdx]);
    if (!pmr) return;


    if (!blocksByPMR.has(pmr)) {
      blocksByPMR.set(pmr, {
        pmr: pmr,
        lastName: row[lastNameIdx],
        firstName: row[firstNameIdx],
        rows: []
      });
    }


    const block = blocksByPMR.get(pmr);
    if (!String(block.lastName || "").trim() && String(row[lastNameIdx] || "").trim()) block.lastName = row[lastNameIdx];
    if (!String(block.firstName || "").trim() && String(row[firstNameIdx] || "").trim()) block.firstName = row[firstNameIdx];


    block.rows.push({ row: row, originalIndex: idx });
  });


  const blocks = Array.from(blocksByPMR.values());


  blocks.sort((a, b) => {
    const aLast = normalizeKeyPart_(a.lastName);
    const bLast = normalizeKeyPart_(b.lastName);
    if (aLast !== bLast) return aLast < bLast ? -1 : 1;


    const aFirst = normalizeKeyPart_(a.firstName);
    const bFirst = normalizeKeyPart_(b.firstName);
    if (aFirst !== bFirst) return aFirst < bFirst ? -1 : 1;


    return normalizePMR_(a.pmr) < normalizePMR_(b.pmr) ? -1 : 1;
  });


  const sortedRows = [];


  blocks.forEach(block => {
    block.rows.sort((a, b) => {
      const aScore = getPrimaryRowScore_(a.row, headerMap);
      const bScore = getPrimaryRowScore_(b.row, headerMap);
      if (aScore !== bScore) return bScore - aScore;
      return a.originalIndex - b.originalIndex;
    });


    block.rows.forEach(item => sortedRows.push(item.row));
  });


  if (sortedRows.length > 0) {
    range.setValues(sortedRows);
  }
}


function getPrimaryRowScore_(row, headerMap) {
  let score = 0;
  const checks = [
    ["Date of Birth", 1000],
    ["Enrollment Date", 250],
    ["Capitation Date", 200],
    ["Address Line 1", 100],
    ["Phone Number", 50],
    ["Primary Language", 25],
    ["Participant Name", 20],
    ["PMR #", 10]
  ];


  checks.forEach(item => {
    const idx = headerMap[item[0]];
    if (idx !== undefined && normalizeCompareValue_(row[idx]) !== "") score += item[1];
  });


  return score;
}


function hideNonPrimaryPMRRows_(sheet) {
  sheet = sheet || SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSheet();


  const lastRow = sheet.getLastRow();
  const lastCol = sheet.getLastColumn();
  if (lastRow < DATA_START_ROW || lastCol < 1) return;


  sheet.showRows(DATA_START_ROW, lastRow - DATA_START_ROW + 1);


  const headers = getHeaders_(sheet, HEADER_ROW);
  const headerMap = buildHeaderIndexMap_(headers);
  const pmrIdx = getPMRIndex_(headerMap);
  if (pmrIdx === -1) return;


  const values = sheet.getRange(DATA_START_ROW, 1, lastRow - DATA_START_ROW + 1, lastCol).getValues();
  const seenPMRs = new Set();
  const rowsToHide = [];


  values.forEach((row, offset) => {
    const pmr = normalizePMR_(row[pmrIdx]);
    if (!pmr) return;


    if (!seenPMRs.has(pmr)) {
      seenPMRs.add(pmr);
      return;
    }


    rowsToHide.push(DATA_START_ROW + offset);
  });


  hideRowNumberBatches_(sheet, rowsToHide);
}


function hideRowNumberBatches_(sheet, rowNumbers) {
  if (!rowNumbers || rowNumbers.length === 0) return;


  const sorted = Array.from(new Set(rowNumbers)).sort((a, b) => a - b);
  let start = sorted[0];
  let previous = sorted[0];


  for (let i = 1; i < sorted.length; i++) {
    const current = sorted[i];
    if (current === previous + 1) {
      previous = current;
      continue;
    }


    sheet.hideRows(start, previous - start + 1);
    start = current;
    previous = current;
  }


  sheet.hideRows(start, previous - start + 1);
}


function clearAllRowGroupsIfPossible_(sheet) {
  const maxRows = sheet.getMaxRows();
  if (maxRows < DATA_START_ROW) return;


  for (let i = 0; i < 8; i++) {
    try {
      sheet.shiftRowGroupDepth(DATA_START_ROW, maxRows - DATA_START_ROW + 1, -1);
    } catch (err) {
      break;
    }
  }
}


function processMasterListFull_(masterSheet, monthParts, pmrFilter, timing) {
  ensureHeaders_(masterSheet, MASTER_LIST_ADDED_HEADERS, HEADER_ROW);
  ensureBannerSummaryOutputHeaders_(masterSheet);
  ensureContactOutputHeaders_(masterSheet);
  markRuntimeStep_(timing, "Process Full - ensure Master List headers");


  processMasterListSingleDataPass_(masterSheet, monthParts, pmrFilter || null, true, timing);
}


function processMasterListDataOnly_(masterSheet, pmrFilter, timing) {
  processMasterListSingleDataPass_(masterSheet, null, pmrFilter || null, false, timing);
}


function processMasterListSingleDataPass_(masterSheet, monthParts, pmrFilter, includeMonthlySyncs, timing) {
  ensureHeaders_(masterSheet, MASTER_LIST_ADDED_HEADERS, HEADER_ROW);
  ensureBannerSummaryOutputHeaders_(masterSheet);
  ensureContactOutputHeaders_(masterSheet);
  ensureHeaders_(masterSheet, ["Notes"], HEADER_ROW);
  markRuntimeStep_(timing, "Single Pass - ensure processing headers");


  assignPrimaryPMRRows_(masterSheet);
  markRuntimeStep_(timing, "Single Pass - assign Primary PMR Row");


  const data = getDataValues_(masterSheet, HEADER_ROW, DATA_START_ROW);
  markRuntimeStep_(timing, "Single Pass - read Master List data range");
  if (!data.values.length) return;


  if (includeMonthlySyncs && monthParts) {
    syncMasterListMonthlySourcesIntoData_(data, monthParts, pmrFilter || null);
    markRuntimeStep_(timing, "Single Pass - sync monthly source data into memory");
  }


  updateBannerColumnData_(data, pmrFilter || null);
  markRuntimeStep_(timing, "Single Pass - build Banner Summary");


  combineAddressesData_(data, pmrFilter || null);
  markRuntimeStep_(timing, "Single Pass - combine address fields");


  handleLanguageData_(data, pmrFilter || null);
  markRuntimeStep_(timing, "Single Pass - process language fields");


  splitPhoneNumbersData_(data, pmrFilter || null);
  markRuntimeStep_(timing, "Single Pass - split phone fields");


  runMasterContactProcessData_(data, pmrFilter || null);
  markRuntimeStep_(timing, "Single Pass - process contacts");


  combineNotesSummaryData_(data, pmrFilter || null);
  markRuntimeStep_(timing, "Single Pass - combine Notes Summary");


  if (data.range) data.range.setValues(data.values);
  markRuntimeStep_(timing, "Single Pass - write processed Master List data");


  highlightAndStrikeExpiredADPhones_(masterSheet, pmrFilter || null);
  markRuntimeStep_(timing, "Single Pass - highlight expired AD phones");


  lockMasterListRowHeightsAndClip_(masterSheet);
  markRuntimeStep_(timing, "Single Pass - row height/wrap lock");
}


function syncMasterListMonthlySourcesIntoData_(data, monthParts, pmrFilter) {
  syncBannerSourceIntoData_(data, monthParts, pmrFilter || null);
  syncUnlockedCarePlanSourceIntoData_(data, monthParts, pmrFilter || null);
  syncCarePlanDueSourceIntoData_(data, monthParts, pmrFilter || null);
}


function syncBannerSourceIntoData_(data, monthParts, pmrFilter) {
  const sourceSheet = getCurrentBannersSheet_(monthParts);


  if (!sourceSheet) {
    notify_("Newest Banners mm.yy sheet was not found. Banner sync skipped.");
    return;
  }


  const sourceMap = buildSourceMapBySingleKeyForPart5_(
    sourceSheet,
    HEADER_ROW,
    DATA_START_ROW,
    "Participant PMR#"
  );


  syncRowsFromSourceMapData_(
    data,
    sourceMap,
    {
      masterKeyHeaders: ["Participant PMR#"],
      fields: BANNER_SYNC_FIELDS
    },
    pmrFilter || null
  );
}




function syncUnlockedCarePlanSourceIntoData_(data, monthParts, pmrFilter) {
  const sourceSheet = getCurrentUnlockedCarePlanSheet_(monthParts);


  if (!sourceSheet) {
    notify_("Unlocked Care Plan Report was not found. Unlocked sync skipped.");
    return;
  }


  const sourceMap = buildSourceMapBySingleKeyForPart5_(
    sourceSheet,
    HEADER_ROW,
    DATA_START_ROW,
    "PMR #"
  );


  syncRowsFromSourceMapData_(
    data,
    sourceMap,
    {
      masterKeyHeaders: ["Participant PMR#"],
      sourceKeyHeaders: ["PMR #"],
      fields: [
        ["Participant Name", "Participant Name"],
        ["PMR #", "PMR #"],
        ["IDT Meeting Date", "IDT Meeting Date"],
        ["Care Plan Start Date", "Care Plan Start Date"]
      ]
    },
    pmrFilter || null
  );
}


function syncCarePlanDueSourceIntoData_(data, monthParts, pmrFilter) {
  const sourceSheet = getCurrentCarePlanDueSheet_(monthParts);


  if (!sourceSheet) {
    notify_("Care Plan Due Report was not found. Care Plan Due sync skipped.");
    return;
  }


  const sourceMap = buildSourceMapBySingleKeyForPart5_(
    sourceSheet,
    HEADER_ROW,
    DATA_START_ROW,
    "Participant Name"
  );


  syncRowsFromSourceMapData_(
    data,
    sourceMap,
    {
      masterKeyHeaders: ["Participant Name"],
      fields: [
        ["Enrollment Date", "Enrollment Date"],
        ["Last Care Plan", "Last Care Plan"],
        ["Next Care Plan Due", "Next Care Plan Due"],
        ["CP Type", "CP Type"]
      ]
    },
    pmrFilter || null
  );
}


function syncRowsFromSourceMapData_(data, sourceMap, config, pmrFilter) {
  if (!data || !data.values || !data.values.length) return;


  const headerMap = data.headerMap;
  const fields = normalizeSyncFieldPairs_(config.fields);


  data.values.forEach(row => {
    if (!shouldProcessRowByPMR_(row, headerMap, pmrFilter)) return;


    const key = config.masterKeyHeaders
      .map(header => normalizeKeyPart_(row[headerMap[header]]))
      .join("|||");


    if (key.replace(/\|/g, "") === "") return;
    if (!sourceMap.has(key)) return;


    const source = sourceMap.get(key);


    fields.forEach(pair => {
      const destHeader = pair[0];
      const sourceHeader = pair[1];
      const destIdx = headerMap[destHeader];


      if (destIdx === undefined) return;
      if (!Object.prototype.hasOwnProperty.call(source, sourceHeader)) return;


      row[destIdx] = source[sourceHeader];
    });
  });
}


function updateBannerColumnData_(data, pmrFilter) {
  const headerMap = data.headerMap;
  const bIdx = headerMap["Banner Summary"];


  if (bIdx === undefined) return;


  const bannerHeaders = [
    "Safety - 2 Person",
    "Wanderer",
    "Interpreter Needed",
    "Fall Risk",
    "DPOA or Guardian Active",
    "Palliative Care"
  ];


  data.values.forEach(row => {
    if (!shouldProcessRowByPMR_(row, headerMap, pmrFilter)) return;


    const parts = [];


    bannerHeaders.forEach(header => {
      const idx = headerMap[header];
      if (idx === undefined) return;


      const value = String(row[idx] || "").trim();
      if (value !== "") parts.push(header);
    });


    row[bIdx] = parts.join(" | ");
  });
}


function combineAddressesData_(data, pmrFilter) {
  const headerMap = data.headerMap;
  const a1Idx = headerMap["Address Line 1"];
  const a2Idx = headerMap["Address Line 2"];
  const targetIdx = headerMap["Address 1 - Street"];


  if (a1Idx === undefined || targetIdx === undefined) return;


  data.values.forEach(row => {
    if (!shouldProcessRowByPMR_(row, headerMap, pmrFilter)) return;


    const p1 = String(row[a1Idx] || "").trim();
    const p2 = a2Idx !== undefined ? String(row[a2Idx] || "").trim() : "";


    row[targetIdx] = p1 && p2 ? `${p1} ${p2}` : (p1 || p2);
  });
}


function handleLanguageData_(data, pmrFilter) {
  const headerMap = data.headerMap;
  const labelIdx = headerMap["Custom Field 1 - Label"];
  const valueIdx = headerMap["Custom Field 1 - Value"];
  const langIdx = headerMap["Primary Language"];


  if (labelIdx === undefined || valueIdx === undefined || langIdx === undefined) return;


  data.values.forEach(row => {
    if (!shouldProcessRowByPMR_(row, headerMap, pmrFilter)) return;


    const lang = String(row[langIdx] || "").trim();
    const existingValue = String(row[valueIdx] || "").trim();


    if (lang && lang.toLowerCase() !== "english") {
      row[labelIdx] = "Language";
      row[valueIdx] = lang;
    } else if (existingValue) {
      row[labelIdx] = "Language";
    } else {
      row[labelIdx] = "";
      row[valueIdx] = "";
    }
  });
}


function splitPhoneNumbersData_(data, pmrFilter) {
  const headerMap = data.headerMap;
  const phoneIdx = headerMap["Phone Number"];


  if (phoneIdx === undefined) return;


  const labelHeaders = ["Phone 1 - Label", "Phone 2 - Label", "Phone 3 - Label", "Phone 4 - Label"];
  const valueHeaders = ["Phone 1 - Value", "Phone 2 - Value", "Phone 3 - Value", "Phone 4 - Value"];
  const labels = ["Home", "Mobile", "Other", "Other"];


  data.values.forEach(row => {
    if (!shouldProcessRowByPMR_(row, headerMap, pmrFilter)) return;


    const phoneText = String(row[phoneIdx] || "").trim();


    for (let i = 0; i < 4; i++) {
      const labelIdx = headerMap[labelHeaders[i]];
      const valueIdx = headerMap[valueHeaders[i]];


      if (labelIdx !== undefined) row[labelIdx] = "";
      if (valueIdx !== undefined) row[valueIdx] = "";
    }


    if (!phoneText) return;


    const parts = phoneText.split("_").map(part => part.trim()).filter(Boolean);


    parts.slice(0, 4).forEach((phone, idx) => {
      const labelIdx = headerMap[labelHeaders[idx]];
      const valueIdx = headerMap[valueHeaders[idx]];


      if (labelIdx !== undefined) row[labelIdx] = labels[idx];
      if (valueIdx !== undefined) row[valueIdx] = phone;
    });
  });
}


function runMasterContactProcessData_(data, pmrFilter) {
  if (!data || !data.values || !data.values.length) return;


  writePMRContactsToParticipantRows_(null, data.values, data.headers, data.headerMap, pmrFilter || null);
}


function combineNotesSummaryData_(data, pmrFilter) {
  if (!data || !data.values || !data.values.length) return;


  const headerMap = data.headerMap;
  const notesIdx = headerMap["Notes"];
  if (notesIdx === undefined) return;


  const sourceHeaders = [
    "Banner Summary",
    "Contact - Summary",
    "Additional Important Information"
  ];


  data.values.forEach(row => {
    if (!shouldProcessRowByPMR_(row, headerMap, pmrFilter)) return;


    const parts = [];


    sourceHeaders.forEach(header => {
      const idx = headerMap[header];
      if (idx === undefined) return;


      const value = String(row[idx] || "").trim();
      if (value) parts.push(value);
    });


    row[notesIdx] = parts.join("\n\n");
  });
}




function rebuildChangedPMRsOnExistingMaster_(currentDemo, currentMaster, reportSheet, monthParts, runFullProcessing, timing) {
  const changedInfo = getChangedPMRsFromMonthlyChangeReport_(reportSheet);
  const changedPMRs = Array.from(changedInfo.keys());
  markRuntimeStep_(timing, "Update - read PMRs from Monthly Change Report (" + changedPMRs.length + " PMRs)");


  if (changedPMRs.length === 0) {
    return 0;
  }


  const result = updateMasterListFromMonthlyChangeActions_(currentDemo, currentMaster, reportSheet, monthParts, changedInfo, timing);
  const affectedPMRFilter = result.affectedPMRs || new Set(changedPMRs);
  markRuntimeStep_(timing, "Update - build affected PMR filter (" + affectedPMRFilter.size + " PMRs)");


  if (runFullProcessing) {
    processMasterListFull_(currentMaster, monthParts, affectedPMRFilter, timing);
  } else {
    processMasterListDataOnly_(currentMaster, affectedPMRFilter, timing);
    markRuntimeStep_(timing, "Update - process affected PMRs data-only");
    formatMasterListSheet_(currentMaster);
    markRuntimeStep_(timing, "Update - format Master List");
    groupMasterListRowsByPMR_(currentMaster);
    markRuntimeStep_(timing, "Update - group/sort Master List rows");
    hideRowsWithBlankDOB_(currentMaster);
    markRuntimeStep_(timing, "Update - hide non-primary rows");
  }


  removeDisenrolledPMRBlocksFromMasterUsingDemoP_(currentMaster, currentDemo);
  markRuntimeStep_(timing, "Update - remove disenrolled PMR blocks after update actions");


  return changedPMRs.length;
}


function updateMasterListFromMonthlyChangeActions_(currentDemo, currentMaster, reportSheet, monthParts, changedInfo, timing) {
  const enrollmentPMRs = getPMRsForMonthlyChangeSections_(changedInfo, ["Enrollments"]);
  const disenrollmentPMRs = getPMRsForMonthlyChangeSections_(changedInfo, ["Disenrollments"]);
  const primaryUpdatePMRs = getPMRsForMonthlyChangeSections_(changedInfo, ["Demographic Changes", "Caseload Changes", "Banner Changes"]);
  const contactChangePMRs = getPMRsForMonthlyChangeSections_(changedInfo, ["Contact Changes"]);
  const affectedPMRs = new Set();


  disenrollmentPMRs.forEach(pmr => affectedPMRs.add(pmr));
  enrollmentPMRs.forEach(pmr => affectedPMRs.add(pmr));
  primaryUpdatePMRs.forEach(pmr => affectedPMRs.add(pmr));
  contactChangePMRs.forEach(pmr => affectedPMRs.add(pmr));


  deletePMRBlocksFromMasterListBySet_(currentMaster, disenrollmentPMRs, reportSheet, monthParts, "Disenrollments - remove PMR block");
  markRuntimeStep_(timing, "Update - remove Disenrollment PMR blocks (" + disenrollmentPMRs.size + " PMRs)");


  deletePMRBlocksFromMasterListBySet_(currentMaster, enrollmentPMRs, reportSheet, monthParts, "Enrollments - replace/add PMR block");
  const addedRows = copyChangedPMRsFromDemoPToMasterList_(currentDemo, currentMaster, enrollmentPMRs, monthParts);
  markRuntimeStep_(timing, "Update - add Enrollment PMR blocks (" + enrollmentPMRs.size + " PMRs, " + addedRows + " rows)");


  const primaryResult = updatePrimaryRowsFromDemoPForPMRs_(currentDemo, currentMaster, primaryUpdatePMRs, monthParts);
  markRuntimeStep_(timing, "Update - primary row updates (" + primaryResult.rowsUpdated + " rows, " + primaryResult.columnsUpdated + " columns)");


  const contactResult = mergeSecondaryRowsFromDemoPForPMRs_(currentDemo, currentMaster, contactChangePMRs, monthParts);
  markRuntimeStep_(timing, "Update - contact row merge (" + contactResult.rowsUpdated + " updates, " + contactResult.rowsAdded + " adds, " + contactResult.rowsRemoved + " removes)");


  return {
    affectedPMRs: affectedPMRs,
    enrollmentPMRs: enrollmentPMRs,
    disenrollmentPMRs: disenrollmentPMRs,
    primaryUpdatePMRs: primaryUpdatePMRs,
    contactChangePMRs: contactChangePMRs,
    primaryResult: primaryResult,
    contactResult: contactResult
  };
}


function getPMRsForMonthlyChangeSections_(changedInfo, sectionsToMatch) {
  const targets = new Set(sectionsToMatch || []);
  const result = new Set();


  (changedInfo || new Map()).forEach((sections, pmr) => {
    if (!sections) return;
    const hasMatch = Array.from(sections).some(section => targets.has(section));
    if (hasMatch) result.add(pmr);
  });


  return result;
}


function deletePMRBlocksFromMasterListBySet_(masterSheet, pmrSet, reportSheet, monthParts, reasonText) {
  if (!masterSheet || !pmrSet || pmrSet.size === 0) return 0;


  const rowsByPMR = buildRowsByPMR_(masterSheet, HEADER_ROW, DATA_START_ROW);
  const headers = getHeaders_(masterSheet, HEADER_ROW);
  const logRows = [];
  const rowsToDelete = [];
  const timestamp = new Date();


  pmrSet.forEach(pmr => {
    const items = rowsByPMR.get(pmr) || [];
    items.forEach(item => {
      logRows.push([
        timestamp,
        monthParts.firstDay,
        pmr,
        reasonText || "Monthly Change action",
        masterSheet.getName(),
        item.rowNumber,
        reportSheet ? reportSheet.getName() : "",
        JSON.stringify(rowObjectFromHeaders_(headers, item.values))
      ]);
      rowsToDelete.push(item.rowNumber);
    });
  });


  appendMasterListChangeLog_(logRows);
  deleteRowNumberBatches_(masterSheet, rowsToDelete);
  clearSheetRuntimeCachesForSheet_(masterSheet);
  return rowsToDelete.length;
}


function updatePrimaryRowsFromDemoPForPMRs_(demoSheet, masterSheet, pmrSet, monthParts) {
  const result = { rowsUpdated: 0, columnsUpdated: 0, missingInMaster: 0, missingInDemo: 0 };
  if (!demoSheet || !masterSheet || !pmrSet || pmrSet.size === 0) return result;


  const demoData = getDataValues_(demoSheet, HEADER_ROW, DATA_START_ROW);
  const masterData = getDataValues_(masterSheet, HEADER_ROW, DATA_START_ROW);
  const demoBlocks = buildMergeRowsByPMRFromData_(demoData);
  const masterBlocks = buildMergeRowsByPMRFromData_(masterData);
  const masterHeaders = masterData.headers;
  const masterHeaderMap = masterData.headerMap;
  const sourceSheetName = demoSheet.getName();


  pmrSet.forEach(pmr => {
    const demoPrimary = getPrimaryMergeRowItem_(demoBlocks.get(pmr) || [], demoData.headerMap);
    const masterPrimary = getPrimaryMergeRowItem_(masterBlocks.get(pmr) || [], masterHeaderMap);


    if (!demoPrimary) {
      result.missingInDemo++;
      return;
    }
    if (!masterPrimary) {
      result.missingInMaster++;
      return;
    }


    const changedColumns = getPrimaryRowChangedColumnDetails_(
      masterPrimary.values,
      masterHeaderMap,
      demoPrimary.values,
      demoData.headerMap
    ).map(item => item.column);


    if (changedColumns.length === 0) return;


    setMasterRowColumnsFromDemoRow_(
      masterSheet,
      masterPrimary.rowNumber,
      masterHeaders,
      masterHeaderMap,
      demoPrimary.values,
      demoData.headerMap,
      changedColumns,
      monthParts,
      sourceSheetName,
      "Primary row updated from Demo P"
    );


    result.rowsUpdated++;
    result.columnsUpdated += changedColumns.length;
  });


  clearSheetRuntimeCachesForSheet_(masterSheet);
  return result;
}


function mergeSecondaryRowsFromDemoPForPMRs_(demoSheet, masterSheet, pmrSet, monthParts) {
  const result = { rowsUpdated: 0, rowsAdded: 0, rowsRemoved: 0, missingInDemo: 0 };
  if (!demoSheet || !masterSheet || !pmrSet || pmrSet.size === 0) return result;


  const demoData = getDataValues_(demoSheet, HEADER_ROW, DATA_START_ROW);
  let masterData = getDataValues_(masterSheet, HEADER_ROW, DATA_START_ROW);
  const demoBlocks = buildMergeRowsByPMRFromData_(demoData);
  let masterBlocks = buildMergeRowsByPMRFromData_(masterData);
  const masterHeaders = masterData.headers;
  const masterHeaderMap = masterData.headerMap;
  const sourceSheetName = demoSheet.getName();
  const rowsToDelete = [];
  const rowsToAppend = [];


  pmrSet.forEach(pmr => {
    const demoRows = demoBlocks.get(pmr) || [];
    const masterRows = masterBlocks.get(pmr) || [];
    if (!demoRows.length) {
      result.missingInDemo++;
      return;
    }


    const demoKeys = buildSecondaryMergeKeyMapForRows_(demoRows, demoData.headerMap, pmr);
    const masterKeys = buildSecondaryMergeKeyMapForRows_(masterRows, masterHeaderMap, pmr);
    const allKeys = new Set([].concat(Array.from(demoKeys.keys()), Array.from(masterKeys.keys())));


    allKeys.forEach(key => {
      const demoItem = demoKeys.get(key);
      const masterItem = masterKeys.get(key);


      if (demoItem && masterItem) {
        const changedFields = getMergeAuditChangedFields_(masterItem.values, masterHeaderMap, demoItem.values, demoData.headerMap);
        if (changedFields.length > 0) {
          setMasterRowColumnsFromDemoRow_(
            masterSheet,
            masterItem.rowNumber,
            masterHeaders,
            masterHeaderMap,
            demoItem.values,
            demoData.headerMap,
            changedFields,
            monthParts,
            sourceSheetName,
            "Contact row updated from Demo P"
          );
          result.rowsUpdated++;
        }
      } else if (demoItem && !masterItem) {
        rowsToAppend.push(buildMappedMasterRowFromDemoRow_(
          demoItem.values,
          demoData.headers,
          demoData.headerMap,
          masterHeaders,
          masterHeaderMap,
          monthParts,
          sourceSheetName,
          "Contact row added from Demo P"
        ));
        result.rowsAdded++;
      } else if (!demoItem && masterItem) {
        rowsToDelete.push(masterItem.rowNumber);
        result.rowsRemoved++;
      }
    });
  });


  if (rowsToAppend.length) {
    const appendRow = Math.max(masterSheet.getLastRow() + 1, DATA_START_ROW);
    masterSheet.getRange(appendRow, 1, rowsToAppend.length, masterHeaders.length).setValues(rowsToAppend);
  }


  if (rowsToDelete.length) {
    deleteRowNumberBatches_(masterSheet, rowsToDelete);
  }


  clearSheetRuntimeCachesForSheet_(masterSheet);
  return result;
}


function buildMappedMasterRowFromDemoRow_(demoRow, demoHeaders, demoHeaderMap, masterHeaders, masterHeaderMap, monthParts, sourceSheetName, statusText) {
  const output = new Array(masterHeaders.length).fill("");


  demoHeaders.forEach((header, sourceIdx) => {
    if (!header) return;
    const targetIdx = masterHeaderMap[header];
    if (targetIdx !== undefined) output[targetIdx] = demoRow[sourceIdx];
  });


  applyMasterListUpdateMetadataToRow_(output, masterHeaderMap, monthParts, sourceSheetName, statusText);
  return output;
}


function setMasterRowColumnsFromDemoRow_(masterSheet, rowNumber, masterHeaders, masterHeaderMap, demoRow, demoHeaderMap, headersToUpdate, monthParts, sourceSheetName, statusText) {
  if (!masterSheet || !rowNumber || rowNumber < DATA_START_ROW) return;
  const rowValues = masterSheet.getRange(rowNumber, 1, 1, masterHeaders.length).getValues()[0];


  (headersToUpdate || []).forEach(header => {
    const masterIdx = masterHeaderMap[header];
    const demoIdx = demoHeaderMap[header];
    if (masterIdx === undefined || demoIdx === undefined) return;
    rowValues[masterIdx] = demoRow[demoIdx];
  });


  applyMasterListUpdateMetadataToRow_(rowValues, masterHeaderMap, monthParts, sourceSheetName, statusText);
  masterSheet.getRange(rowNumber, 1, 1, masterHeaders.length).setValues([rowValues]);
}


function applyMasterListUpdateMetadataToRow_(rowValues, headerMap, monthParts, sourceSheetName, statusText) {
  const statusIdx = headerMap["Master List Update Status"];
  const monthIdx = headerMap["Master List Update Month"];
  const sourceIdx = headerMap["Master List Source Sheet"];


  if (statusIdx !== undefined) rowValues[statusIdx] = statusText || "Updated from Demo P";
  if (monthIdx !== undefined) rowValues[monthIdx] = monthParts ? monthParts.firstDay : new Date();
  if (sourceIdx !== undefined) rowValues[sourceIdx] = sourceSheetName || "";
}


function getSystemAndTestingSheetNames_() {
  const names = new Set(SYSTEM_SHEETS_TO_HIDE || []);


  [
    RFF_DASHBOARD_SHEET,
    RFF_VALIDATION_SHEET,
    RFF_TIMING_SHEET,
    RFF_TEST6_DATE_FORMAT_SHEET,
    RFF_TEST7_VALIDATION_FAILURE_SHEET,
    RFF_TEST9_SUBHEADER_SHEET,
    RFF_TEST10_DASHBOARD_AUDIT_SHEET,
    RFF_TEST_DASHBOARD_SHEET,
    RFF_HEALTH_CHECK_SHEET
  ].forEach(function(name) {
    if (name) names.add(name);
  });


  // Templates are intentionally excluded. Template visibility is controlled only
  // by the existing Hide Report Templates / Show Report Templates workflow.
  return names;
}


function isSystemOrTestingSheet_(sheet) {
  if (!sheet) return false;


  const sheetName = String(sheet.getName() || "").trim();
  const lower = sheetName.toLowerCase();
  const explicitNames = getSystemAndTestingSheetNames_();


  // Do not treat Template - sheets as system sheets. Templates have their own
  // separate show/hide menu actions and triggers.
  return explicitNames.has(sheetName) ||
    lower.indexOf("framework test") !== -1 ||
    lower.indexOf("template validation") !== -1 ||
    lower.indexOf("framework health check") !== -1 ||
    lower.indexOf("dashboard audit") !== -1 ||
    lower.endsWith(" audit") ||
    lower.endsWith(" validation") ||
    lower.endsWith(" diagnostics") ||
    lower.endsWith(" health check") ||
    lower.indexOf("timing") !== -1;
}


function hideSystemSheets_() {
  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  let hiddenCount = 0;


  ss.getSheets().forEach(sheet => {
    if (!isSystemOrTestingSheet_(sheet)) return;


    try {
      if (!sheet.isSheetHidden()) {
        sheet.hideSheet();
        hiddenCount++;
      }
    } catch (err) {
      Logger.log("Could not hide system/testing sheet " + sheet.getName() + ": " + err.message);
    }
  });


  return hiddenCount;
}




function hideMasterListSourceColumns_(sheet) {
  /*
   * v1.4.25:
   * Runtime Master List column hiding is restricted. Hidden/show settings are
   * applied only by the dashboard template builder from Section D.
   */
  return 0;
}


function showMasterListSourceColumns_(sheet) {
  /*
   * v1.4.25:
   * Runtime Master List column showing is restricted. Hidden/show settings are
   * applied only by the dashboard template builder from Section D.
   */
  return 0;
}


function organizeWorkbookTabs_(monthParts) {
  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  if (!monthParts) return;


  const orderedNames = [
    INDEX_SHEET,
    buildMonthlySheetName_(MASTER_LIST_PREFIX, monthParts.firstDay, monthParts.lastDay),
    buildMonthlySheetName_(MONTHLY_CHANGE_REPORT_PREFIX, monthParts.firstDay, monthParts.lastDay),
    buildMonthlySheetNameNoDashAfterPrefix_(DEMO_P_PREFIX, monthParts.firstDay, monthParts.lastDay),
    buildStandardMonthlySheetName_("Banners", monthParts.firstDay),
    buildStandardMonthlySheetName_("Unlocked CP", monthParts.firstDay),
    buildStandardMonthlySheetName_("CP Due", monthParts.firstDay),
    DISENROLLED_EXCLUSION_SHEET,
    MASTER_LIST_CHANGE_LOG_SHEET
  ];


  let position = 1;
  orderedNames.forEach(sheetName => {
    const sheet = ss.getSheetByName(sheetName);
    if (!sheet) return;
    try {
      ss.setActiveSheet(sheet);
      ss.moveActiveSheet(position++);
    } catch (err) {
      Logger.log("Could not move sheet " + sheetName + ": " + err.message);
    }
  });


  hideSystemSheets_();


  const currentMaster = getMonthlySheetByPrefixAndDate_(ss, MASTER_LIST_PREFIX, monthParts.firstDay, monthParts.lastDay);
  if (currentMaster) currentMaster.activate();
}


function prepareMasterListSortOrderBeforeFormatting_(sheet) {
  sheet = sheet || SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSheet();


  sheet.showRows(DATA_START_ROW, Math.max(sheet.getLastRow() - DATA_START_ROW + 1, 1));
  assignPrimaryPMRRows_(sheet);
  assignSortOrderByParticipant_(sheet);
  sortBySortOrder_(sheet);
  formatSortOrderDisplayValues_(sheet);
}


function formatSortOrderDisplayValues_(sheet) {
  sheet = sheet || SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSheet();


  const headers = getHeaders_(sheet, HEADER_ROW);
  const sortIdx = headers.indexOf("Sort Order");


  if (sortIdx === -1) return;


  const lastRow = sheet.getLastRow();
  if (lastRow < DATA_START_ROW) return;


  const range = sheet.getRange(DATA_START_ROW, sortIdx + 1, lastRow - DATA_START_ROW + 1, 1);
  const values = range.getValues();


  const output = values.map(row => {
    const value = row[0];
    const num = Number(value);


    if (isNaN(num) || value === "" || value === null || value === undefined) return [value];


    const whole = Math.floor(num);
    const detail = Math.round((num - whole) * 1000);


    if (detail <= 0) return [String(whole)];
    return [whole + "." + detail];
  });


  range;
  range.setValues(output);
}


function applyFinalMasterListColorAndDisplay_(sheet) {
  sheet = sheet || SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSheet();


  sheet.showRows(DATA_START_ROW, Math.max(sheet.getLastRow() - DATA_START_ROW + 1, 1));
  hideMasterListSourceColumns_(sheet);
  applyParticipantAlternatingColorsBySortOrder_(sheet);
  hideDecimalSortOrderRows_(sheet);
  enforceMasterListFinalDisplay_(sheet);
}


function applyMasterListDisplaySettings_(sheet) {
  applyFinalMasterListColorAndDisplay_(sheet || SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSheet());
}

  const monthParts = promptForLockedYearReportMonth_("Hide Master List Source Columns");
  if (!monthParts) return;
  const sheet = getCurrentMasterListSheet_(monthParts) || SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSheet();
  hideMasterListSourceColumns_(sheet);
  notify_("Master List source columns hidden.");
}
