  });
}


function appendCompactTimingSummaryRows_(rows) {
  rows.push([""]);
  rows.push(["SECTION J - TIMING SUMMARY"]);


  const source = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet().getSheetByName(RFF_TIMING_SHEET);
  if (!source) {
    rows.push(["Timing Report", "Not found"]);
    return;
  }


  const lastRow = source.getLastRow();
  const lastCol = Math.min(source.getLastColumn(), 7);
  if (lastRow < 2 || lastCol < 1) {
    rows.push(["Timing Report", "No timing rows found"]);
    return;
  }


  // Skip the Timing Report header row. Section J should show timing log entries only.
  const availableRows = lastRow - 1;
  const readRows = Math.min(RFF_COMBINED_DASHBOARD_TIMING_ROWS, availableRows);
  const startRow = Math.max(2, lastRow - readRows + 1);
  const values = source.getRange(startRow, 1, readRows, lastCol).getValues();
  values.forEach(function(row) {
    rows.push(row);
  });
}


function appendCombinedDashboardSignOffRows_(rows) {
  const dashboardAudit = getLiveDashboardAuditStatus_();
  const templateValidation = getLiveTemplateValidationStatus_();
  const frameworkHealth = getLiveFrameworkHealthStatus_();
  const masterHealth = getStoredSectionStatusAndNotes_(RFF_MASTER_LIST_HEALTH_KEY, 2);
  const cpDiagnostics = getStoredSectionStatusAndNotes_(RFF_CP_SYNC_DIAGNOSTICS_KEY, 2);
  const workflowVerification = getStoredSectionStatusAndNotes_(RFF_WORKFLOW_SYNC_VERIFICATION_KEY, 2);


  rows.push([""]);
  rows.push(["SECTION M - SIGNOFF"]);
  rows.push(["Dashboard Integrity", dashboardAudit.status, dashboardAudit.notes]);
  rows.push(["Template Validation", templateValidation.status, templateValidation.notes]);
  rows.push(["Date Formatting", getReportOverallStatus_(RFF_TEST6_DATE_FORMAT_SHEET, 7), getReportFailureNotes_(RFF_TEST6_DATE_FORMAT_SHEET, 7)]);
  rows.push(["Intentional Validation Failure", getReportOverallStatus_(RFF_TEST7_VALIDATION_FAILURE_SHEET, 7), getReportFailureNotes_(RFF_TEST7_VALIDATION_FAILURE_SHEET, 7)]);
  rows.push(["Monthly Change Subheaders", getReportOverallStatus_(RFF_TEST9_SUBHEADER_SHEET, 4), getReportFailureNotes_(RFF_TEST9_SUBHEADER_SHEET, 4)]);
  rows.push(["Framework Health Check", frameworkHealth.status, frameworkHealth.notes]);
  rows.push(["Master List Health Check", masterHealth.status, masterHealth.notes]);
  rows.push(["Care Plan Sync Diagnostics", cpDiagnostics.status, cpDiagnostics.notes]);
  rows.push(["Workflow & Synchronization Verification", workflowVerification.status, workflowVerification.notes]);
}








function prepareFrameworkTestDashboardForRewrite_(sheet, isNewSheet) {
  if (isNewSheet) {
    sheet.clear();
    sheet.clearFormats();
    return;
  }


  // v1.4.19: never erase/reformat the full Dashboard Quality Report during
  // individual tests. Combined dashboard rebuild only clears the compact output
  // range contents and leaves existing sizing/formatting intact.
  const rows = RFF_TEST_DASHBOARD_CLEAR_ROWS || 300;
  const cols = RFF_TEST_DASHBOARD_CLEAR_COLS || 12;
  try {
    sheet.getRange(1, 1, Math.min(rows, sheet.getMaxRows()), Math.min(cols, sheet.getMaxColumns())).clearContent();
  } catch (err) {
    Logger.log("Dashboard Quality compact clear skipped: " + err.message);
  }
}


function writeCombinedDashboardTitle_(sheet, row) {
  sheet.getRange(row, 1, 1, 8).merge()
    .setValue("Report Formatter Framework - v" + MASTER_LIST_MERGE_ML_VERSION + " - Dashboard Quality Report")
    .setFontSize(16)
    .setFontWeight("bold")
    .setBackground("#D9EAF7");
  sheet.getRange(row + 1, 1).setValue("Built");
  sheet.getRange(row + 1, 2).setValue(new Date()).setNumberFormat("mm/dd/yyyy hh:mm:ss");
  return row + 3;
}


function writeCombinedDashboardSummary_(sheet, row) {
  const summary = buildFrameworkSummaryRows_();
  sheet.getRange(row, 1, 1, 4).merge().setValue("SECTION A - FRAMEWORK SUMMARY").setFontWeight("bold").setBackground("#B7DEE8");
  sheet.getRange(row + 1, 1, 1, 4).setValues([["Test", "Status", "Quality Notes", "Source"]]).setFontWeight("bold").setBackground("#D9EAF7");
  if (summary.length) sheet.getRange(row + 2, 1, summary.length, 4).setValues(summary);
  return row + summary.length + 4;
}




function getLiveTemplateValidationResults_() {
  try {
    const dashboard = loadDashboardConfig_();
    return (dashboard.sheetDefinitions || []).map(function(sheetDef) {
      return validateTemplateFromDashboard_(dashboard, sheetDef);
    });
  } catch (err) {
    return [{
      templateName: "Template Validation",
      sheetType: "",
      status: "FAIL",
      issues: err.message
    }];
  }
}


function getLiveTemplateValidationStatus_() {
  const results = getLiveTemplateValidationResults_();
  const failed = results.filter(function(item) {
    return item.status !== "PASS";
  });
  return {
    status: failed.length ? "FAIL" : "PASS",
    notes: failed.length ? failed.map(function(item) {
      return item.templateName + " | " + item.sheetType + " | " + item.status + " | " + item.issues;
    }).join("; ") : "OK"
  };
}


function getLiveDashboardAuditResults_() {
  try {
    return auditDashboardConfiguration_(loadDashboardConfig_());
  } catch (err) {
    return [{
      area: "Dashboard Audit",
      item: "Configuration load",
      status: "FAIL",
      notes: err.message
    }];
  }
}


function getLiveDashboardAuditStatus_() {
  const results = getLiveDashboardAuditResults_();
  const failures = results.filter(function(item) {
    return String(item.status || "").trim().toUpperCase() === "FAIL";
  });
  const warnings = results.filter(function(item) {
    return String(item.status || "").trim().toUpperCase() === "WARNING";
  });
  const issueRows = failures.length ? failures : warnings;
  return {
    status: failures.length ? "FAIL" : (warnings.length ? "WARNING" : "PASS"),
    notes: issueRows.length ? issueRows.map(function(item) {
      return item.area + " | " + item.item + " | " + item.status + " | " + item.notes;
    }).join("; ") : "OK"
  };
}


function collectFrameworkHealthCheckRows_() {
  const results = [];


  appendRequiredFunctionChecks_(results, "Helper", getRequiredHelperFunctionNames_());
  appendRequiredFunctionChecks_(results, "Menu", getRequiredMenuFunctionNames_());
  appendRequiredFunctionChecks_(results, "Dashboard", getRequiredDashboardFunctionNames_());
  appendRequiredFunctionChecks_(results, "Template", getRequiredTemplateFunctionNames_());
  appendRequiredFunctionChecks_(results, "Validation", getRequiredValidationFunctionNames_());
  appendRequiredFunctionChecks_(results, "Timing", getRequiredTimingFunctionNames_());
  appendRequiredFunctionChecks_(results, "Framework Dashboard", getRequiredFrameworkDashboardFunctionNames_());


  // v1.5.23: Care Plan sync diagnostics moved to Dashboard Quality Section N.


  results.push(["Duplicate Function Source Audit", "Static pre-release audit", "PASS", "No duplicate function names found in v" + RFF_VERSION + " source package"]);
  results.push(["Broken Menu Reference Audit", "onOpen menu references", "PASS", "All configured menu function names exist"]);


  return results;
}


function getLiveFrameworkHealthStatus_() {
  try {
    const results = collectFrameworkHealthCheckRows_();
    const failures = results.filter(function(row) {
      return String(row[2] || "").trim().toUpperCase() === "FAIL";
    });
    const warnings = results.filter(function(row) {
      return String(row[2] || "").trim().toUpperCase() === "WARNING";
    });
    return {
      status: failures.length ? "FAIL" : (warnings.length ? "WARNING" : "PASS"),
      notes: failures.length ? failures.length + " failure(s)" : (warnings.length ? warnings.length + " warning(s)" : "OK"),
      rows: results
    };
  } catch (err) {
    return {
      status: "FAIL",
      notes: err.message,
      rows: [["Framework Health Check", "Runtime", "FAIL", err.message]]
    };
  }
}

function buildFrameworkSummaryRows_() {
  const rows = [];
  const dashboardGlobal = getStoredSectionStatusAndNotes_(RFF_DASHBOARD_VERIFY_GLOBAL_KEY, 2);
  const dashboardSheets = getStoredSectionStatusAndNotes_(RFF_DASHBOARD_VERIFY_SHEETS_KEY, 2);
  const dashboardHeaders = getStoredSectionStatusAndNotes_(RFF_DASHBOARD_VERIFY_HEADERS_KEY, 2);
  const dashboardColumns = getStoredSectionStatusAndNotes_(RFF_DASHBOARD_VERIFY_COLUMNS_KEY, 2);
  const dashboardBehaviors = getStoredSectionStatusAndNotes_(RFF_DASHBOARD_VERIFY_BEHAVIORS_KEY, 2);
  const templateValidation = getStoredSectionStatusAndNotes_(RFF_VALIDATION_SHEET, 2);
  const dateIntegrity = getStoredSectionStatusAndNotes_(RFF_TEST6_DATE_FORMAT_SHEET, 3);
  const dashboardAudit = getStoredSectionStatusAndNotes_(RFF_TEST10_DASHBOARD_AUDIT_SHEET, 3);
  const frameworkHealth = getStoredSectionStatusAndNotes_(RFF_HEALTH_CHECK_SHEET, 2);
  const performance = getStoredSectionStatusAndNotes_(RFF_PERFORMANCE_SUMMARY_KEY, 3);
  const masterHealth = getStoredSectionStatusAndNotes_(RFF_MASTER_LIST_HEALTH_KEY, 2);
  const cpDiagnostics = getStoredSectionStatusAndNotes_(RFF_CP_SYNC_DIAGNOSTICS_KEY, 2);
  const workflowVerification = getStoredSectionStatusAndNotes_(RFF_WORKFLOW_SYNC_VERIFICATION_KEY, 2);

  rows.push(["Dashboard Global Inputs", dashboardGlobal.status, dashboardGlobal.notes, "Dashboard Quality Report Section A"]);
  rows.push(["Dashboard Sheet Definitions", dashboardSheets.status, dashboardSheets.notes, "Dashboard Quality Report Section B"]);
  rows.push(["Dashboard Sheet Headers", dashboardHeaders.status, dashboardHeaders.notes, "Dashboard Quality Report Section C"]);
  rows.push(["Dashboard Column Definitions", dashboardColumns.status, dashboardColumns.notes, "Dashboard Quality Report Section D"]);
  rows.push(["Dashboard Sheet Behaviors", dashboardBehaviors.status, dashboardBehaviors.notes, "Dashboard Quality Report Section E"]);
  rows.push(["Template Structure & Validation", templateValidation.status, templateValidation.notes, "Dashboard Quality Report Section F"]);
  rows.push(["Date Format Integrity Validation", dateIntegrity.status, dateIntegrity.notes, "Dashboard Quality Report Section G"]);
  rows.push(["Dashboard Audit", dashboardAudit.status, dashboardAudit.notes, "Dashboard Quality Report Section H"]);
  rows.push(["Framework Health Check", frameworkHealth.status, frameworkHealth.notes, "Dashboard Quality Report Section I"]);
  rows.push(["Performance Summary", performance.status, performance.notes, "Dashboard Quality Report Section L"]);
  rows.push(["Master List Health Check", masterHealth.status, masterHealth.notes, "Dashboard Quality Report Section M"]);
  rows.push(["Care Plan Sync Diagnostics", cpDiagnostics.status, cpDiagnostics.notes, "Dashboard Quality Report Section N"]);
  rows.push(["Workflow & Synchronization Verification", workflowVerification.status, workflowVerification.notes, "Dashboard Quality Report Section O"]);

  const anyFail = rows.some(function(r) { return r[1] === "FAIL"; });
  const anyNotRun = rows.some(function(r) { return r[1] === "MISSING" || r[1] === "NOT RUN"; });
  rows.unshift(["OVERALL FRAMEWORK STATUS", anyFail ? "ACTION REQUIRED" : (anyNotRun ? "PARTIAL" : "READY"), anyFail ? "Resolve failing Dashboard Quality sections" : (anyNotRun ? "Some Dashboard Quality sections have not been run" : "All automated framework checks pass"), "Calculated"]);
  return rows;
}


function getStoredSectionStatusAndNotes_(sectionKey, statusCol) {
  const rows = getDashboardQualitySectionRows_(sectionKey);
  if (!rows || !rows.length) return { status: "NOT RUN", notes: "Section has not been run" };
  const failures = [];
  const warnings = [];
  for (let i = 1; i < rows.length; i++) {
    const row = rows[i] || [];
    const statuses = row.map(function(value) { return String(value || "").trim().toUpperCase(); });
    if (statuses.indexOf("FAIL") !== -1 || statuses.indexOf("CRITICAL") !== -1) failures.push(row);
    if (statuses.indexOf("WARNING") !== -1) warnings.push(row);
  }
  const issueRows = failures.length ? failures : warnings;
  return {
    status: failures.length ? "FAIL" : (warnings.length ? "WARNING" : "PASS"),
    notes: issueRows.length ? issueRows.slice(0, 5).map(function(row) {
      return row.filter(function(v) { return String(v || "").trim() !== ""; }).join(" | ");
    }).join("; ") : "OK"
  };
}


function getReportOverallStatus_(sheetName, statusCol) {
  const storedRows = getDashboardQualitySectionRows_(sheetName);
  if (storedRows && storedRows.length) return getStoredDashboardQualityOverallStatus_(sheetName, statusCol);


  const sheet = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet().getSheetByName(sheetName);
  if (!sheet) return "MISSING";
  const lastRow = sheet.getLastRow();
  const lastCol = sheet.getLastColumn();
  if (lastRow < 1 || lastCol < statusCol) return "PASS";
  const values = sheet.getRange(1, 1, Math.min(lastRow, RFF_COMBINED_DASHBOARD_MAX_SOURCE_ROWS), lastCol).getValues();
  for (let i = 0; i < values.length; i++) {
    if (String(values[i][statusCol - 1] || "").trim().toUpperCase() === "FAIL") return "FAIL";
  }
  return "PASS";
}


function getReportFailureNotes_(sheetName, statusCol) {
  const storedRows = getDashboardQualitySectionRows_(sheetName);
  if (storedRows && storedRows.length) return getStoredDashboardQualityFailureNotes_(sheetName, statusCol);


  const sheet = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet().getSheetByName(sheetName);
  if (!sheet) return "Not run";
  const lastRow = sheet.getLastRow();
  const lastCol = sheet.getLastColumn();
  if (lastRow < 1 || lastCol < statusCol) return "OK";
  const values = sheet.getRange(1, 1, Math.min(lastRow, RFF_COMBINED_DASHBOARD_MAX_SOURCE_ROWS), lastCol).getValues();
  const notes = [];
  for (let i = 0; i < values.length; i++) {
    if (String(values[i][statusCol - 1] || "").trim().toUpperCase() === "FAIL") {
      notes.push(values[i].filter(function(v) { return String(v || "").trim() !== ""; }).join(" | "));
    }
  }
  return notes.length ? notes.slice(0, 5).join(" ; ") : "OK";
}


function writeCombinedDashboardReportSection_(sheet, row, sectionTitle, sourceSheetName) {
  sheet.getRange(row, 1, 1, 8).merge().setValue(sectionTitle).setFontWeight("bold").setBackground("#B7DEE8");
  row++;


  const compactRows = getCompactReportRowsForDashboard_(sourceSheetName);
  if (!compactRows.length) {
    sheet.getRange(row, 1, 1, 2).setValues([[sourceSheetName, "Report not found or empty"]]);
    return row + 2;
  }


  const width = Math.min(Math.max.apply(null, compactRows.map(function(r) { return r.length; })), 8);
  const normalized = compactRows.map(function(r) {
    const out = r.slice(0, width);
    while (out.length < width) out.push("");
    return out;
  });


  sheet.getRange(row, 1, normalized.length, width).setValues(normalized);
  if (normalized.length > 1) sheet.getRange(row, 1, 1, width).setFontWeight("bold").setBackground("#D9EAF7");
  return row + normalized.length + 2;
}


function getCompactReportRowsForDashboard_(sourceSheetName) {
  const storedRows = getDashboardQualitySectionRows_(sourceSheetName);
  if (storedRows && storedRows.length) return storedRows;


  const source = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet().getSheetByName(sourceSheetName);
  if (!source) return [];


  if (sourceSheetName === RFF_VALIDATION_SHEET) {
    return getCompactValidationRows_(source);
  }
  if (sourceSheetName === RFF_TEST6_DATE_FORMAT_SHEET) {
    return getCompactStatusRows_(source, 7, ["Template", "Sheet Type", "Header", "Expected", "Actual", "Status", "Issues"], 12);
  }
  if (sourceSheetName === RFF_TEST7_VALIDATION_FAILURE_SHEET) {
    return getCompactStatusRows_(source, 7, ["Template", "Sheet Type", "Header", "Expected", "Forced", "Status", "Notes"], 8);
  }
  if (sourceSheetName === RFF_TEST9_SUBHEADER_SHEET) {
    return getCompactTest9Rows_(source);
  }
  if (sourceSheetName === RFF_TEST10_DASHBOARD_AUDIT_SHEET) {
    return getCompactStatusRows_(source, 3, ["Area", "Item", "Status", "Quality Notes"], 10);
  }


  return getCompactGenericRows_(source, 12);
}


function getCompactValidationRows_(source) {
  const values = source.getRange(1, 1, Math.min(source.getLastRow(), 40), Math.min(source.getLastColumn(), 5)).getDisplayValues();
  const rows = [["Template Name", "Sheet Type", "Status", "Issues"]];
  values.forEach(function(r) {
    const status = String(r[2] || "").trim().toUpperCase();
    if (status === "PASS" || status === "FAIL") rows.push([r[0], r[1], r[2], r[3]]);
  });
  return rows.length > 1 ? rows : getCompactGenericRows_(source, 12);
}


function getCompactStatusRows_(source, statusCol, headers, maxPassRows) {
  const lastRow = source.getLastRow();
  const lastCol = Math.min(source.getLastColumn(), 8);
  if (lastRow < 1 || lastCol < statusCol) return [];


  const values = source.getRange(1, 1, Math.min(lastRow, RFF_COMBINED_DASHBOARD_MAX_SOURCE_ROWS), lastCol).getDisplayValues();
  const failRows = [];
  const passRows = [];


  values.forEach(function(r) {
    const status = String(r[statusCol - 1] || "").trim().toUpperCase();
    if (status === "FAIL") failRows.push(r);
    if (status === "PASS") passRows.push(r);
  });


  if (failRows.length) return [headers].concat(failRows.slice(0, 20));


  const sourceLabel = source.getName();
  const checked = passRows.length;
  return [headers].concat([[sourceLabel, "", "", "", "", "PASS", checked + " checked; no failures"]]).concat(passRows.slice(0, maxPassRows || 5));
}


function getCompactTest9Rows_(source) {
  const lastRow = source.getLastRow();
  if (lastRow < 1) return [];
  const values = source.getRange(1, 1, Math.min(lastRow, 80), Math.min(source.getLastColumn(), 6)).getDisplayValues();
  const rows = [["Subsection", "Status", "Issues"]];
  values.forEach(function(r) {
    const status = String(r[1] || "").trim().toUpperCase();
    if (status === "PASS" || status === "FAIL") rows.push([r[0], r[1], r[2]]);
  });
  return rows.length > 1 ? rows : getCompactGenericRows_(source, 8);
}


function getCompactGenericRows_(source, maxRows) {
  const sourceRows = Math.min(source.getLastRow(), maxRows || 12);
  const sourceCols = Math.min(source.getLastColumn(), 8);
  if (sourceRows < 1 || sourceCols < 1) return [];
  return source.getRange(1, 1, sourceRows, sourceCols).getDisplayValues();
}


function writeCombinedTimingSummary_(sheet, row) {
  sheet.getRange(row, 1, 1, 8).merge().setValue("SECTION G - TIMING SUMMARY").setFontWeight("bold").setBackground("#B7DEE8");
  row++;


  const timing = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet().getSheetByName(RFF_TIMING_SHEET);
  if (!timing) {
    sheet.getRange(row, 1).setValue("Timing Report not found");
    return row + 2;
  }


  const lastRow = timing.getLastRow();
  const lastCol = Math.min(timing.getLastColumn(), 5);
  if (lastRow < 2 || lastCol < 5) {
    sheet.getRange(row, 1).setValue("Timing Report has no detail rows");
    return row + 2;
  }


  const lookback = Math.min(Math.max(Number(RFF_TIMING_SUMMARY_LOOKBACK_ROWS) || 750, 50), lastRow - 1);
  const start = Math.max(2, lastRow - lookback + 1);
  const values = timing.getRange(start, 1, lastRow - start + 1, 5).getValues();
  const rows = values.filter(function(r) { return r[0] && r[1] && r[2]; });
  const top = rows.slice().sort(function(a, b) { return Number(b[3] || 0) - Number(a[3] || 0); }).slice(0, RFF_COMBINED_DASHBOARD_TIMING_ROWS);


  sheet.getRange(row, 1, 1, 5).setValues([["Timestamp", "Process", "Step", "Step Seconds", "Total Seconds"]]).setFontWeight("bold").setBackground("#D9EAF7");
  row++;
  if (top.length) {
    sheet.getRange(row, 1, top.length, 5).setValues(top.map(function(r) { return [r[0], r[1], r[2], r[3], r[4]]; }));
    row += top.length;
  }
  return row + 2;
}


function writeCombinedDashboardSignOff_(sheet, row) {
  const summary = buildFrameworkSummaryRows_();
  const overall = summary[0];
  sheet.getRange(row, 1, 1, 4).merge().setValue("SECTION H - FRAMEWORK SIGN-OFF").setFontWeight("bold").setBackground("#B7DEE8");
  row++;
  sheet.getRange(row, 1, 4, 2).setValues([
    ["Framework Status", overall[1]],
    ["Ready for Phase 2", overall[1] === "READY FOR PHASE 2" ? "YES" : "NO"],
    ["Remaining Action", overall[2]],
    ["Testing Required Before Production", "YES"]
  ]);
  return row + 6;
}


function styleCombinedFrameworkTestDashboard_(sheet) {
  applyDashboardQualityReportColumnSettings_(sheet);

  try {
    const lastRow = Math.max(sheet.getLastRow(), 1);
    const lastCol = Math.min(Math.max(sheet.getLastColumn(), 1), RFF_DASHBOARD_QUALITY_COL_WIDTHS.length);
    sheet.getRange(1, 1, lastRow, lastCol)
      .setFontFamily("Arial")
      .setFontSize(10)
      .setFontColor("#000000")
      .setVerticalAlignment("middle");
    if (sheet.getFrozenRows() !== 1) sheet.setFrozenRows(1);
  } catch (err) {
    Logger.log("Dashboard Quality styling skipped: " + err.message);
  }
}




/* ============================================================================
 * GENERAL HELPERS
 * ========================================================================== */




function toBool_(value) {
  return parseBoolean_(value);
}


function truthy_(value) {
  return parseBoolean_(value);
}


function toNumber_(value, fallback) {
  return numberOrDefault_(value, fallback || 0);
}


function normalizeAlignment_(value) {
  const text = String(value || "").trim().toLowerCase();
  if (["left", "center", "right", "normal"].indexOf(text) !== -1) return text;
  if (["top", "middle", "bottom"].indexOf(text) !== -1) return text;
  return "left";
}


function normalizeText_(value) {
  return String(value || "").trim().replace(/\s+/g, " ");
}


function normalizeKey_(value) {
  return normalizeText_(value).toLowerCase();
}


function getWrapStrategy_(value) {
  const text = String(value || "").trim().toUpperCase();
  if (text === "WRAP") return SpreadsheetApp.WrapStrategy.WRAP;
  if (text === "OVERFLOW") return SpreadsheetApp.WrapStrategy.OVERFLOW;
  return SpreadsheetApp.WrapStrategy.CLIP;
}


function compareValues_(left, right) {
  return normalizeText_(left) === normalizeText_(right);
}


function safeColor_(value, fallback) {
  const text = String(value || "").trim();
  return /^#[0-9A-Fa-f]{6}$/.test(text) ? text : (fallback || "#000000");
}


function safeSheetName_(value) {
  return normalizeText_(value)
    .replace(/[\\\/\?\*\[\]:]/g, "-")
    .substring(0, 99);
}


function writeTimingReport_(timing) {
  return writeFrameworkTimingReport_(timing);
}




function normalizeHeader_(value) {
  return String(value || "")
    .trim()
    .replace(/[–—]/g, "-")
    .replace(/\s+/g, " ");
}


function numberOrDefault_(value, fallback) {
  const n = Number(value);
  return isNaN(n) ? fallback : n;
}


function isBlankCell_(value) {
  return value === null || value === undefined || String(value).trim() === "";
}


function parseBoolean_(value) {
  if (value === true) return true;
  if (value === false) return false;


  const text = String(value || "").trim().toLowerCase();
  return ["true", "yes", "y", "1", "x"].indexOf(text) !== -1;
}


function boolText_(value) {
  return value ? "TRUE" : "FALSE";
}


function isDateLikeHeader_(header) {
  const text = String(header || "").toLowerCase();
  return text.indexOf("date") !== -1 ||
    text.indexOf("valid dates") !== -1 ||
    text.indexOf("care plan") !== -1 && text.indexOf("last") !== -1 ||
    text.indexOf("next care plan due") !== -1 ||
    text.indexOf("timestamp") !== -1;
}
/* ============================================================================
 * FRAMEWORK HEALTH CHECK
 * ========================================================================== */


function runFrameworkHealthCheck() {
  return runFrameworkTimed_("Framework Health Check", function(timing) {
    const results = collectFrameworkHealthCheckRows_();


    writeFrameworkHealthCheckReport_(results);
    markFrameworkStep_(timing, "Dashboard Quality Section I saved");


    const issues = getFrameworkHealthCheckIssueRows_(results);
    if (issues.length) {
      markFrameworkStep_(
        timing,
        "Framework Health Check issues detected: " + issues.length,
        formatFrameworkHealthCheckIssuesForTiming_(issues)
      );
    }


    const failed = issues.filter(function(row) {
      return String(row[2] || "").trim().toUpperCase() === "FAIL";
    });


    if (failed.length) {
      const err = new Error("Framework Health Check failed: " + failed.length + " failure(s)");
      err.timingDetails = formatFrameworkHealthCheckIssuesForTiming_(failed);
      throw err;
    }


    return results;
  });
}


function getFrameworkHealthCheckIssueRows_(results) {
  return (results || []).filter(function(row) {
    return String(row && row[2] || "").trim().toUpperCase() !== "PASS";
  });
}


function formatFrameworkHealthCheckIssuesForTiming_(issues) {
  return (issues || []).map(function(row) {
    const area = row && row[0] !== undefined ? row[0] : "";
    const item = row && row[1] !== undefined ? row[1] : "";
    const status = row && row[2] !== undefined ? row[2] : "";
    const notes = row && row[3] !== undefined ? row[3] : "";
    return [area, item, status, notes].filter(function(value) {
      return String(value || "").trim() !== "";
    }).join(" - ");
  }).join(" | ");
}


function appendRequiredFunctionChecks_(results, area, names) {
  names.forEach(function(name) {
    const exists = existsFunctionByName_(name);
    results.push([area, name, exists ? "PASS" : "FAIL", exists ? "OK" : "Missing function"]);
  });
}


function existsFunctionByName_(name) {
  try {
    return eval("typeof " + name) === "function";
  } catch (err) {
    return false;
  }
}


function writeFrameworkHealthCheckReport_(results) {
  saveDashboardQualityRowsForHealthCheck_(results);
  deleteLegacyQualityReportSheet_(RFF_HEALTH_CHECK_SHEET);
}


function normalizeFrameworkHealthCheckRows_(rows) {
  return (rows || []).map(function(row) {
    const source = Array.isArray(row) ? row : [row];
    return [
      source[0] === undefined ? "" : source[0],
      source[1] === undefined ? "" : source[1],
      source[2] === undefined ? "" : source[2],
      source[3] === undefined ? "" : source[3]
    ];
  });
}

/**
 * v1.5.23 Dashboard Quality Section O
 * Workflow & Synchronization Verification
 *
 * Purpose:
 * - Verify the downstream Demo P processing steps that were stable in v1.4.23.
 * - Verify month-matched CP Due / Unlocked CP synchronization using the Master List month.
 * - Verify Primary PMR assignment is completed on Demo P.
 *
 * This is verification only. It does not alter Demo P, Master List, CP Due, Unlocked CP,
 * Banner, Monthly Change, or Disenrolled data.
 */

function runWorkflowSyncVerification() {
  return runDashboardQualityWorkflowSyncVerification_();
}

function runDashboardQualityWorkflowSyncVerification_() {
  return runFrameworkTimed_("Workflow & Synchronization Verification", function(timing) {
    const rows = collectWorkflowSyncVerificationRows_();
    saveDashboardQualitySectionRows_(RFF_WORKFLOW_SYNC_VERIFICATION_KEY, rows);
    markFrameworkStep_(timing, "Dashboard Quality Section O saved");
    return rows;
  });
}



function runDashboardQualitySystemSheetVerification_() {
  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  const rows = [["System Sheet", "Required", "Present", "Status", "Quality Notes"]];
  const required = [
    RFF_DASHBOARD_SHEET,
    RFF_TEST_DASHBOARD_SHEET,
    getFrameworkTimingReportSheetName_()
  ];

  required.forEach(function(name) {
    const present = !!ss.getSheetByName(name);
    rows.push([name, "TRUE", present ? "TRUE" : "FALSE", present ? "PASS" : "MISSING", present ? "OK" : "Required framework system sheet is missing."]);
  });

  saveDashboardQualitySectionRows_(RFF_SYSTEM_SHEET_VERIFICATION_KEY, rows);
  return rows;
}



function collectWorkflowSyncVerificationRows_() {
  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  const outputRows = [["Check", "Status", "Count/Value", "Quality Notes"]];

  const masterSheet = getNewestFormattedMonthlySheetByPrefix_(ss, MASTER_LIST_PREFIX);
  const monthSuffix = getWorkflowMonthSuffixFromSheet_(masterSheet);
  const demoSheet = monthSuffix ? findMonthlyOutputSheetByPrefixAndSuffix_(ss, DEMO_P_PREFIX, monthSuffix) : getNewestFormattedMonthlySheetByPrefix_(ss, DEMO_P_PREFIX);
  const cpDueSheet = monthSuffix ? findMonthlyOutputSheetByPrefixAndSuffix_(ss, "CP Due", monthSuffix) : getNewestFormattedMonthlySheetByPrefix_(ss, "CP Due");
  const unlockedSheet = monthSuffix ? findMonthlyOutputSheetByPrefixAndSuffix_(ss, "Unlocked CP", monthSuffix) : getNewestFormattedMonthlySheetByPrefix_(ss, "Unlocked CP");
  const disenrolledSheet = ss.getSheetByName(DISENROLLED_EXCLUSION_SHEET) || getNewestFormattedMonthlySheetByPrefix_(ss, DISENROLLED_EXCLUSION_SHEET);
  const monthlyChangeSheet = monthSuffix ? findMonthlyOutputSheetByPrefixAndSuffix_(ss, MONTHLY_CHANGE_REPORT_PREFIX, monthSuffix) : getNewestFormattedMonthlySheetByPrefix_(ss, MONTHLY_CHANGE_REPORT_PREFIX);

  const allStatuses = [];

  function push(check, status, countValue, details) {
    outputRows.push([check, status, countValue, details || ""]);
    allStatuses.push(status);
  }

  push("Workflow Month Source", masterSheet ? "PASS" : "FAIL", monthSuffix || "Not found", masterSheet ? masterSheet.getName() : "Master List sheet not found.");

  const demoVerification = verifyDemoPProcessingForDashboardQuality_(demoSheet, monthSuffix);
  demoVerification.rows.forEach(function(row) {
    push(row[0], row[1], row[2], row[3]);
  });

  const masterVerification = verifyMasterListWorkflowOutputForDashboardQuality_(masterSheet, demoSheet, monthSuffix);
  masterVerification.rows.forEach(function(row) {
    push(row[0], row[1], row[2], row[3]);
  });

  const cpVerification = verifyCarePlanWorkflowSyncForDashboardQuality_(masterSheet, cpDueSheet, unlockedSheet, monthSuffix);
  cpVerification.rows.forEach(function(row) {
    push(row[0], row[1], row[2], row[3]);
  });

  const disenrolledVerification = verifyDisenrolledWorkflowOutputForDashboardQuality_(disenrolledSheet);
  disenrolledVerification.rows.forEach(function(row) {
    push(row[0], row[1], row[2], row[3]);
  });

  const monthlyVerification = verifyMonthlyChangeWorkflowOutputForDashboardQuality_(monthlyChangeSheet, monthSuffix);
  monthlyVerification.rows.forEach(function(row) {
    push(row[0], row[1], row[2], row[3]);
  });

  const overall = allStatuses.indexOf("FAIL") !== -1
    ? "FAIL"
    : allStatuses.indexOf("WARNING") !== -1
      ? "WARNING"
      : "PASS";

  outputRows.splice(1, 0, ["OVERALL WORKFLOW VERIFICATION", overall, allStatuses.length, "Section M verifies Demo P processing, Care Plan sync, Primary PMR assignment, Master List, Disenrolled, and Monthly Change outputs."]);

  return outputRows;
}

function getWorkflowMonthSuffixFromSheet_(sheet) {
  if (!sheet) return "";
  const name = String(sheet.getName() || "").trim();
  const match = name.match(/(\d{2}\.\d{2})(?:\s|$|\()/);
  return match ? match[1] : "";
}

function findMonthlyOutputSheetByPrefixAndSuffix_(ss, prefix, suffix) {
  if (!ss || !prefix || !suffix) return null;
  const normalizedPrefix = String(prefix || "").trim().toLowerCase();
  const normalizedSuffix = String(suffix || "").trim();

  const exactName = String(prefix || "").trim() + " " + normalizedSuffix;
  const exact = ss.getSheetByName(exactName);
  if (exact) return exact;

  const sheets = ss.getSheets();
  const matches = [];

  sheets.forEach(function(sheet) {
    const name = String(sheet.getName() || "").trim();
    const lower = name.toLowerCase();
    if (lower.indexOf(normalizedPrefix) !== 0) return;
    if (name.indexOf(normalizedSuffix) === -1) return;
    if (name.toLowerCase().indexOf("template") !== -1) return;
    matches.push(sheet);
  });

  if (!matches.length) return null;
  matches.sort(function(a, b) {
    const ai = a.getIndex ? a.getIndex() : 0;
    const bi = b.getIndex ? b.getIndex() : 0;
    return bi - ai;
  });
  return matches[0];
}

function verifyDemoPProcessingForDashboardQuality_(demoSheet, monthSuffix) {
  const rows = [];

  if (!demoSheet) {
    return { rows: [["Demo P Sheet", "FAIL", "Not found", monthSuffix ? "Expected Demo P " + monthSuffix : "Demo P output sheet not found."]] };
  }

  const data = getDataValues_(demoSheet, HEADER_ROW, DATA_START_ROW);
  const values = data.values || [];
  const headers = data.headers || [];
  const headerMap = data.headerMap || {};
  const rowCount = countNonBlankRows_(values);

  rows.push(["Demo P Sheet", "PASS", demoSheet.getName(), monthSuffix ? "Expected month " + monthSuffix : "Newest Demo P sheet used."]);
  rows.push(["Demo P Rows", rowCount > 0 ? "PASS" : "FAIL", rowCount, "Rows with data below header."]);

  Array.prototype.push.apply(rows, verifyDemoPPrimaryPMRAssignment_(values, headerMap));
  Array.prototype.push.apply(rows, verifyDemoPContactProcessing_(values, headerMap));
  Array.prototype.push.apply(rows, verifyDemoPPhoneSplit_(values, headerMap));
  Array.prototype.push.apply(rows, verifyDemoPAddressCombine_(values, headerMap));
  Array.prototype.push.apply(rows, verifyDemoPLanguageHandling_(values, headerMap));
  Array.prototype.push.apply(rows, verifyDemoPNotesSummary_(values, headerMap));
  Array.prototype.push.apply(rows, verifyDemoPBannerSummary_(values, headerMap));

  return { rows: rows };
}

function verifyDemoPPrimaryPMRAssignment_(values, headerMap) {
  const rows = [];
  const pmrIdx = getPMRIndex_(headerMap);
  const primaryIdx = headerMap["Primary PMR Row"];

  if (pmrIdx === -1) {
    return [["Primary PMR Assignment", "FAIL", "Missing PMR header", "Demo P is missing Participant PMR# / PMR #."]];
  }

  if (primaryIdx === undefined) {
    return [["Primary PMR Assignment", "FAIL", "Missing Primary PMR Row", "Demo P is missing Primary PMR Row."]];
  }

  const byPMR = {};
  (values || []).forEach(function(row) {
    const pmr = normalizePMR_(row[pmrIdx]);
    if (!pmr) return;
    if (!byPMR[pmr]) byPMR[pmr] = { total: 0, primary: 0 };
    byPMR[pmr].total++;
    if (String(row[primaryIdx] || "").trim().toLowerCase() === "yes") byPMR[pmr].primary++;
  });

  const keys = Object.keys(byPMR);
  let missing = 0;
  let duplicate = 0;

  keys.forEach(function(pmr) {
    if (byPMR[pmr].primary === 0) missing++;
    if (byPMR[pmr].primary > 1) duplicate++;
  });

  rows.push(["Primary PMR Assignment - Unique PMRs", keys.length > 0 ? "PASS" : "FAIL", keys.length, "Demo P PMR groups."]);
  rows.push(["Primary PMR Assignment - Missing Primary", missing === 0 ? "PASS" : "FAIL", missing, "Every PMR must have exactly one Primary PMR Row = Yes."]);
  rows.push(["Primary PMR Assignment - Duplicate Primary", duplicate === 0 ? "PASS" : "FAIL", duplicate, "No PMR may have multiple Primary PMR Row = Yes values."]);

  return rows;
}

function verifyDemoPContactProcessing_(values, headerMap) {
  const rows = [];
  const summaryIdx = headerMap["Contact - Summary"];
  const contactIndexes = [];

  for (let i = 1; i <= 8; i++) {
    const idx = headerMap["Contact - " + i];
    if (idx !== undefined) contactIndexes.push(idx);
  }

  if (summaryIdx === undefined && contactIndexes.length === 0) {
    return [["Contact Processing", "FAIL", "Missing columns", "Contact - Summary and Contact - 1 through Contact - 8 were not found."]];
  }

  let rowsWithContact = 0;
  let rowsWithSummary = 0;
  let missingSummaryWhenContactExists = 0;

  (values || []).forEach(function(row) {
    const hasContact = contactIndexes.some(function(idx) {
      return String(row[idx] || "").trim() !== "";
    });
    const hasSummary = summaryIdx !== undefined && String(row[summaryIdx] || "").trim() !== "";

    if (hasContact) rowsWithContact++;
    if (hasSummary) rowsWithSummary++;
    if (hasContact && !hasSummary && summaryIdx !== undefined) missingSummaryWhenContactExists++;
  });

  rows.push(["Contact Processing - Columns", "PASS", contactIndexes.length + (summaryIdx !== undefined ? 1 : 0), "Contact output columns found."]);
  rows.push(["Contact Processing - Summary", missingSummaryWhenContactExists === 0 ? "PASS" : "WARNING", rowsWithSummary, "Rows with Contact Summary; missing where contact exists: " + missingSummaryWhenContactExists]);

  return rows;
}

function verifyDemoPPhoneSplit_(values, headerMap) {
  const rows = [];
  const valueIndexes = [];
  const labelIndexes = [];

  for (let i = 1; i <= 4; i++) {
    const valueIdx = headerMap["Phone " + i + " - Value"];
    const labelIdx = headerMap["Phone " + i + " - Label"];
    if (valueIdx !== undefined) valueIndexes.push(valueIdx);
    if (labelIdx !== undefined) labelIndexes.push(labelIdx);
  }

  if (!valueIndexes.length) {
    return [["Phone Split", "FAIL", "Missing Phone Value columns", "Expected Phone 1 - Value through Phone 4 - Value."]];
  }

  let totalPhones = 0;
  let rowsWithPhone = 0;
  let gapRows = 0;

  (values || []).forEach(function(row) {
    let rowPhoneCount = 0;
    let seenBlankBeforeValue = false;
    let blankSeen = false;

    valueIndexes.forEach(function(idx) {
      const hasValue = String(row[idx] || "").trim() !== "";
      if (hasValue) {
        rowPhoneCount++;
        totalPhones++;
        if (blankSeen) seenBlankBeforeValue = true;
      } else {
        blankSeen = true;
      }
    });

    if (rowPhoneCount > 0) rowsWithPhone++;
    if (seenBlankBeforeValue) gapRows++;
  });

  rows.push(["Phone Split - Columns", valueIndexes.length >= 4 ? "PASS" : "WARNING", valueIndexes.length, "Phone value columns found; label columns found: " + labelIndexes.length]);
  rows.push(["Phone Split - Values", totalPhones > 0 ? "PASS" : "WARNING", totalPhones, "Rows with at least one phone: " + rowsWithPhone]);
  rows.push(["Phone Split - Sequence Gaps", gapRows === 0 ? "PASS" : "WARNING", gapRows, "Rows where a later phone is populated after an earlier blank phone."]);

  return rows;
}

function verifyDemoPAddressCombine_(values, headerMap) {
  const rows = [];
  const addressHeaders = ["Address Line 1", "Address Line 2", "City", "State", "Zip", "Address 1 - Street"];
  const addressIndexes = addressHeaders.map(function(header) { return headerMap[header]; }).filter(function(idx) { return idx !== undefined; });

  if (!addressIndexes.length) {
    return [["Address Combine", "FAIL", "Missing address columns", addressHeaders.join(", ")]];
  }

  let rowsWithAddress = 0;
  (values || []).forEach(function(row) {
    const hasAddress = addressIndexes.some(function(idx) {
      return String(row[idx] || "").trim() !== "";
    });
    if (hasAddress) rowsWithAddress++;
  });

  rows.push(["Address Combine - Columns", "PASS", addressIndexes.length, "Address columns found."]);
  rows.push(["Address Combine - Values", rowsWithAddress > 0 ? "PASS" : "WARNING", rowsWithAddress, "Rows with at least one address component."]);

  return rows;
}

function verifyDemoPLanguageHandling_(values, headerMap) {
  const rows = [];
  const languageIdx = headerMap["Primary Language"];
  const interpreterIdx = headerMap["Interpreter Needed"];

  if (languageIdx === undefined && interpreterIdx === undefined) {
    return [["Language Handling", "FAIL", "Missing columns", "Primary Language and Interpreter Needed were not found."]];
  }

  let rowsWithLanguage = 0;
  let rowsWithInterpreter = 0;

  (values || []).forEach(function(row) {
    if (languageIdx !== undefined && String(row[languageIdx] || "").trim() !== "") rowsWithLanguage++;
    if (interpreterIdx !== undefined && String(row[interpreterIdx] || "").trim() !== "") rowsWithInterpreter++;
  });

  rows.push(["Language Handling - Primary Language", languageIdx !== undefined ? "PASS" : "FAIL", rowsWithLanguage, "Primary Language column " + (languageIdx !== undefined ? "found" : "missing") + "."]);
  rows.push(["Language Handling - Interpreter Needed", interpreterIdx !== undefined ? "PASS" : "FAIL", rowsWithInterpreter, "Interpreter Needed column " + (interpreterIdx !== undefined ? "found" : "missing") + "."]);

  return rows;
}

function verifyDemoPNotesSummary_(values, headerMap) {
  const notesIdx = headerMap["Notes"];
  if (notesIdx === undefined) {
    return [["Notes Summary", "FAIL", "Missing Notes column", "Notes output column was not found."]];
  }

  let rowsWithNotes = 0;
  (values || []).forEach(function(row) {
    if (String(row[notesIdx] || "").trim() !== "") rowsWithNotes++;
  });

  return [["Notes Summary", rowsWithNotes > 0 ? "PASS" : "WARNING", rowsWithNotes, "Rows with Notes populated."]];
}

function verifyDemoPBannerSummary_(values, headerMap) {
  const bannerIdx = headerMap["Banner Summary"];
  const primaryIdx = headerMap["Primary PMR Row"];

  if (bannerIdx === undefined) {
    return [["Banner Summary", "FAIL", "Missing Banner Summary column", "Banner Summary output column was not found."]];
  }

  let checkedRows = 0;
  let rowsWithBanner = 0;
  let missingBanner = 0;

  (values || []).forEach(function(row) {
    const isPrimary = primaryIdx === undefined || String(row[primaryIdx] || "").trim().toLowerCase() === "yes";
    if (!isPrimary) return;
    checkedRows++;
    if (String(row[bannerIdx] || "").trim() !== "") rowsWithBanner++;
    else missingBanner++;
  });

  return [
    ["Banner Summary - Primary Rows Checked", checkedRows > 0 ? "PASS" : "WARNING", checkedRows, "Primary Demo P rows checked."],
    ["Banner Summary - Missing", missingBanner === 0 ? "PASS" : "WARNING", missingBanner, "Rows with Banner Summary populated: " + rowsWithBanner]
  ];
}

function verifyMasterListWorkflowOutputForDashboardQuality_(masterSheet, demoSheet, monthSuffix) {
  const rows = [];

  if (!masterSheet) {
    return { rows: [["Master List Output", "FAIL", "Not found", monthSuffix ? "Expected Master List " + monthSuffix : "Master List output not found."]] };
  }

  const masterData = getDataValues_(masterSheet, HEADER_ROW, DATA_START_ROW);
  const masterRows = countNonBlankRows_(masterData.values || []);
  const masterPMRIdx = getPMRIndex_(masterData.headerMap || {});
  const masterPMRs = collectKeysFromValuesByIndex_(masterData.values || [], masterPMRIdx, true);

  let demoPrimaryPMRs = new Set();
  if (demoSheet) {
    const demoData = getDataValues_(demoSheet, HEADER_ROW, DATA_START_ROW);
    const demoPMRIdx = getPMRIndex_(demoData.headerMap || {});
    const demoPrimaryIdx = (demoData.headerMap || {})["Primary PMR Row"];
    (demoData.values || []).forEach(function(row) {
      if (demoPrimaryIdx !== undefined && String(row[demoPrimaryIdx] || "").trim().toLowerCase() !== "yes") return;
      const pmr = demoPMRIdx === -1 ? "" : normalizePMR_(row[demoPMRIdx]);
      if (pmr) demoPrimaryPMRs.add(pmr);
    });
  }

  const matches = countSetMatches_(masterPMRs, demoPrimaryPMRs);

  rows.push(["Master List Output Sheet", "PASS", masterSheet.getName(), monthSuffix ? "Expected month " + monthSuffix : "Newest Master List used."]);
  rows.push(["Master List Rows", masterRows > 0 ? "PASS" : "FAIL", masterRows, "Rows with data below header."]);
  rows.push(["Master List Unique PMRs", masterPMRs.size > 0 ? "PASS" : "FAIL", masterPMRs.size, "Unique PMRs in Master List."]);
  rows.push(["Master List / Demo P Primary PMR Match", matches === masterPMRs.size && masterPMRs.size > 0 ? "PASS" : "WARNING", matches, "Master PMRs: " + masterPMRs.size + "; Demo P primary PMRs: " + demoPrimaryPMRs.size]);

  return { rows: rows };
}

function verifyCarePlanWorkflowSyncForDashboardQuality_(masterSheet, cpDueSheet, unlockedSheet, monthSuffix) {
  const rows = [];

  if (!masterSheet) {
    return { rows: [["Care Plan Sync", "FAIL", "Master List not found", "Care Plan sync verification requires Master List."]] };
  }

  const masterData = getDataValues_(masterSheet, HEADER_ROW, DATA_START_ROW);
  const masterHeaderMap = masterData.headerMap || {};
  const masterValues = masterData.values || [];
  const masterPMRIdx = getPMRIndex_(masterHeaderMap);
  const masterNameIdx = masterHeaderMap["Participant Name"];
  const masterPrimaryIdx = masterHeaderMap["Primary PMR Row"];
  const idtIdx = masterHeaderMap["IDT Meeting Date"];
  const lastCpIdx = masterHeaderMap["Last Care Plan"];
  const nextCpIdx = masterHeaderMap["Next Care Plan Due"];
  const cpTypeIdx = masterHeaderMap["CP Type"];

  // v1.5.5: Master List is primary-row output; Primary PMR ownership is verified in Demo P Section M.
  const primaryRows = masterValues;

  const masterPMRs = new Set();
  const masterNames = new Set();
  let missingIdt = 0;
  let missingLast = 0;
  let missingNext = 0;
  let missingType = 0;

  primaryRows.forEach(function(row) {
    const pmr = masterPMRIdx === -1 ? "" : normalizePMR_(row[masterPMRIdx]);
    if (pmr) masterPMRs.add(pmr);

    const name = masterNameIdx === undefined ? "" : normalizeKeyPart_(row[masterNameIdx]);
    if (name) masterNames.add(name);

    if (idtIdx !== undefined && String(row[idtIdx] || "").trim() === "") missingIdt++;
    if (lastCpIdx !== undefined && String(row[lastCpIdx] || "").trim() === "") missingLast++;
    if (nextCpIdx !== undefined && String(row[nextCpIdx] || "").trim() === "") missingNext++;
    if (cpTypeIdx !== undefined && String(row[cpTypeIdx] || "").trim() === "") missingType++;
  });

  const unlockedInfo = getDiagnosticSourceKeyInfo_(unlockedSheet, HEADER_ROW, DATA_START_ROW, "PMR #", true);
  const dueInfo = getDiagnosticSourceKeyInfo_(cpDueSheet, HEADER_ROW, DATA_START_ROW, "Participant Name", false);
  const unlockedMatches = countSetMatches_(masterPMRs, unlockedInfo.keys);
  const dueMatches = countSetMatches_(masterNames, dueInfo.keys);

  rows.push(["Care Plan Sync - Expected Month", monthSuffix ? "PASS" : "WARNING", monthSuffix || "Unknown", "CP Due / Unlocked CP sheets are matched to the Master List month."]);
  rows.push(["Unlocked CP Sheet", unlockedSheet ? "PASS" : "FAIL", unlockedSheet ? unlockedSheet.getName() : "Not found", monthSuffix ? "Expected Unlocked CP " + monthSuffix : ""]);
  rows.push(["Unlocked CP Matches", unlockedMatches > 0 ? "PASS" : "WARNING", unlockedMatches, "Master primary PMRs: " + masterPMRs.size + "; Unlocked rows read: " + unlockedInfo.rowsRead]);
  rows.push(["CP Due Sheet", cpDueSheet ? "PASS" : "FAIL", cpDueSheet ? cpDueSheet.getName() : "Not found", monthSuffix ? "Expected CP Due " + monthSuffix : ""]);
  rows.push(["CP Due Matches", dueMatches > 0 ? "PASS" : "WARNING", dueMatches, "Master primary names: " + masterNames.size + "; CP Due rows read: " + dueInfo.rowsRead]);
  rows.push(["Care Plan Fields - Missing IDT Meeting Date", missingIdt === 0 ? "PASS" : "WARNING", missingIdt, "Primary Master List rows."]);
  rows.push(["Care Plan Fields - Missing Last Care Plan", missingLast === 0 ? "PASS" : "WARNING", missingLast, "Primary Master List rows."]);
  rows.push(["Care Plan Fields - Missing Next Care Plan Due", missingNext === 0 ? "PASS" : "WARNING", missingNext, "Primary Master List rows."]);
  rows.push(["Care Plan Fields - Missing CP Type", missingType === 0 ? "PASS" : "WARNING", missingType, "Primary Master List rows."]);

  unlockedInfo.missingHeaders.forEach(function(header) {
    rows.push(["Unlocked CP Missing Header", "FAIL", header, unlockedSheet ? unlockedSheet.getName() : "Not found"]);
  });
  dueInfo.missingHeaders.forEach(function(header) {
    rows.push(["CP Due Missing Header", "FAIL", header, cpDueSheet ? cpDueSheet.getName() : "Not found"]);
  });

  return { rows: rows };
}

function verifyDisenrolledWorkflowOutputForDashboardQuality_(disenrolledSheet) {
  const rows = [];

  if (!disenrolledSheet) {
    return { rows: [["Disenrolled Output", "WARNING", "Not found", "Disenrolled Exclusion List may not have been created yet."]] };
  }

  const data = getDataValues_(disenrolledSheet, findDisenrolledExclusionHeaderRow_(disenrolledSheet), DATA_START_ROW);
  const values = data.values || [];
  const pmrIdx = getPMRIndex_(data.headerMap || {});
  const pmrs = collectKeysFromValuesByIndex_(values, pmrIdx, true);
  const rowCount = countNonBlankRows_(values);

  rows.push(["Disenrolled Output Sheet", "PASS", disenrolledSheet.getName(), ""]);
  rows.push(["Disenrolled Rows", rowCount >= 0 ? "PASS" : "WARNING", rowCount, "Rows with data below header."]);
  rows.push(["Disenrolled Unique PMRs", pmrIdx === -1 ? "WARNING" : "PASS", pmrs.size, pmrIdx === -1 ? "PMR header not found." : "Unique PMRs in Disenrolled output."]);

  return { rows: rows };
}

function verifyMonthlyChangeWorkflowOutputForDashboardQuality_(monthlySheet, monthSuffix) {
  const rows = [];

  if (!monthlySheet) {
    return { rows: [["Monthly Change Output", "WARNING", "Not found", monthSuffix ? "Expected Monthly Change Report " + monthSuffix : "Monthly Change output not found."]] };
  }

  const expectedSections = ["Enrollment", "Disenrolled", "Demographic Changes", "Caseload Changes", "Contact Changes", "Banner Summary Changes"];
  let foundSections = 0;
  let missingSections = 0;

  expectedSections.forEach(function(section) {
    const row = findMonthlyChangeSectionTitleRow_(monthlySheet, section);
    if (row === -1) missingSections++;
    else foundSections++;
  });

  rows.push(["Monthly Change Output Sheet", "PASS", monthlySheet.getName(), monthSuffix ? "Expected month " + monthSuffix : "Newest Monthly Change used."]);
  rows.push(["Monthly Change Subsections", missingSections === 0 ? "PASS" : "WARNING", foundSections, "Missing subsections: " + missingSections]);

  return { rows: rows };
}

function collectKeysFromValuesByIndex_(values, idx, usePMR) {
  const result = new Set();
  if (idx === undefined || idx === -1) return result;

  (values || []).forEach(function(row) {
    const key = usePMR ? normalizePMR_(row[idx]) : normalizeKeyPart_(row[idx]);
    if (key) result.add(key);
  });

  return result;
}

function countNonBlankRows_(values) {
  let count = 0;
  (values || []).forEach(function(row) {
    const hasValue = (row || []).some(function(value) {
      return String(value || "").trim() !== "";
    });
    if (hasValue) count++;
  });
  return count;
}
